12|87|Ta shuo: Wo de haizimen! Nimen qu dating you su fu he ta didi de xiaoxi ba. Nimen buyao juewang yu zhenzhu de ci'en, zhiyou buxindao de renmen cai juewang yu zhenzhu de ci'en.
12|88|Dang tamen jinqu jian you su fu de shihou, tamen shuo: Quangui a! Women he women de juanshu zaoyule zaihai, zhi dai laile yidian lie zhi caiwu, qing ni gei women zu liang de liangshi, qing ni shishe gei women. Zhenzhu yiding hui baochou shishe zhe.
12|89|Ta shuo: Nimen zhidao ma? Dang nimen shi yumei de shihou, nimen shi zenyang duidai you su fu he ta didi de ne?
12|90|Tamen shuo: Zenme, ni ya! Zhenshi you su fu ma? Ta shuo: Wo shi you su fu, zhe shi wo didi, zhenzhu que yi jiang en gei women. Shei jingwei erqie jianren,(shei bi shou baochou), yin wei zhenzhu bi bu shi xingshan zhe tulao wu chou.
12|91|Tamen shuo: Zhi zhenzhu fashi, zhenzhu que yi cong women dangzhong jianxuanle ni. Congqian, women que shi youzui de.
12|92|Ta shuo: Jintian dui nimen hao wu qianze, dan yuan zhenzhu raoshu nimen. Ta shi zui ci'ai de.
12|93|Nimen ba wo zhe jian chenyi dai huiqu, ba ta meng zai wo fuqin de lian shang, ta jiu hui huifu shili. Ranhou, nimen ba ziji de juanshu quanbu dai dao wo zheli lai ba!
12|94|Dang dui shang chufa de shihou, tamen de fuqin shuo: Wo que yi wen dao you su fu de qiweile, yao bushi nimen shuo wo shi lao hutu.
12|95|Tamen shuo: Zhi zhenzhu fashi, ni dique hai zai ni na jiu you de mi wu zhi zhong.
12|96|Dang baoxi zhe lai dao hou, ta jiu. Jian. Gu. X zai ta de lian shang, ta de yanjing liji huifule shili. Ta shuo: Nandao wo meiyou dui nimen shuoguo ma? Wo dique cong zhenzhu zhidao nimen suo bu zhidao de.
12|97|Tamen shuo: Women de fuqin a! Qing ni wei women qiurao, women que shi youzui de.

12|99|Dang tamen jinqu jian you su fu de shihou, ta yongbao ta de shuangqin, ta shuo: Nimen ping'an di jin ai ji ba! Ruguo zhenzhu yiyu.
12|100|Ta qing ta de shuangqin zuo zai gaozuo shang, tamen wei ta er fufu koutou, ta shuo: Wo de fuqin a! Zhe jiushi wo yiqian de meng zhao de jieshi. Wo de zhu yi shi nage meng zhao bian cheng wei shishile. Ta que yi youdai wo, yinwei ta ba wo cong jianyu li shifang chulai, ta zai emo lijian wo he wo gegemen zhihou, ba nimen cong shamo lidai dao zheli lai. Wo de zhu, dui tasuo yiyu zhe que shi ci'ai de. Ta que shi quanzhi de, que shi zhi rui de.
12|101|Wo de zhu a! Ni que yi shangci wo yibufen zhengquan, bing jiao gei wo yixie yuanmeng de zhishi. Tiandi de chuangzao zhe a! Zai jinshi he houshi, ni dou shi wo de zhuzai. Qiu ni shi wo zuowei shuncong zhe er siqu, qiu ni shi wo ru yu shanren zhi lie.
12|102|Na shi yibufen youxuan de xiaoxi, wo ba ta qishi ni. Dang tamen yong jimou juece de shihou, ni buzai tamen mianqian,
12|103|ni suiran qiewang shiren xindao, dan tamen daban shi bu xindao de.
12|104|Ni bu wei chuanshou “gulanjing” er xiang tamen yaoqiu renhe baochou.“Gulanjing” zhishi dui shiren de jiaohui.
12|105|Tiandi jian you xuduo jixiang, tamen cong pangbian zouguo, er bu zhuyi.
12|106|Tamen suiran daban xinyang zhenzhu, dan tamen dou shi yi wu pei zhu de.
12|107|Nandao tamen bupa zhenzhu chengfa zhong de da zai jianglin tamen, huo fuhuo shi zai tamen bu zhi bu jue zhi zhong, turan jianglin tamen ma?
12|108|Ni shuo: Zhe shi wo de dao, wo haozhao renmen xinyang zhenzhu, wo he suicong wo de ren, dou shi yiju mingzheng de.(Wo zheng) zhenzhu, chaojue wanwu! Wo bushi yi wu pei zhu de.
12|109|Zai ni zhiqian, wo zhi paiqianle chengshi jumin zhong de ruogan nanzi, wo qishi tamen, nandao tamen meiyou zai dadishang luxing, yin'er guancha qian ren de jieju shi zenyang de ma? Houshi de zhusuo, duiyu jingwei zhe shi geng hao de. Nandao nimen bu lijie ma?
12|110|Zhidao zhong shizhe juewang, erqie caixiang ziji bei qipian de shihou, wo de yuanzhu cai lailin tamen, er wo zhengjiule wo suo yiyu de ren. Wo suo jia yu fanzui de renmen de chengfa shi buke kangju de.
12|111|Zai tamen de gushi li, duiyu you lizhi de renmen, que youyi zhong jiaoxun. Zhe bushi weizao de xun ci, que shi zhengshi qian jing, xiangjie wanshi, xiangdao xinshi, bing shi yi ci'en de.
13|1|Ai lie fu, lia mu, mi mu, la yi. Zhexie shi tian jing de jie wen. Cong ni de zhu jiang shi yu ni de jingdian, que shi zhenshi de, dan zhongren daban bu xin.
13|2|Zhenzhu jianli zhu tian, er buyong nimen suo neng kanjian de zhizhu. Suihou ta duan zuo zai baozuo shang, zhifu ri yue, shi qi gezi yunxing dao yige dingqi. Ta chuli wanshi, jieshi jixiang, yibian nimen quexin jiang yu nimen de zhu xiang hui.
13|3|Ta zhankai da di, bing zai da dishang anzhi xuduo shanyue he heliu, ta ba mei zhong guoshi zaocheng liangxing de, ta yi heiye fugai baizhou. Duiyu neng siwei de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
13|4|Da dishang you xuduo linjin de quyu, you putao yuan, you zhuangjia, you ye zao shu, qizhong you er zhu tonggen sheng de, er zhu yi gen sheng de,(zhexie dou shi) yong tongyang de shui guangai de, wo que shi zhe yibufen guoshi bi na yibufen jiamei. Duiyu neng lijie de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
13|5|Ruguo ni gandao jingya, namo, tamen de zhe ju hua cai shi qiguai de: Dang women bian cheng wei chentu de shihou, women biding yao chongxin shou zao ma? Zhe deng ren shi buxin tamen de zhu de, zhe deng ren shi yao dai jiasuo de; zhe deng ren shi juzhu huo yu de, tamen jiang yong ju qizhong.
13|6|Zai enhui jianglin zhiqian, tamen yaoqiu ni zaori zhaoshi chengfa. Xuduo chengjie chufa zai tamen zhiqian que yi shiqule. Zhongren suiran bu yi, dan ni de zhu duiyu tamen que shi raoshu de. Ni de zhu de chengfa que shi yanli de.
13|7|Bu xindao zhe shuo: Weisheme meiyou yi zhong jixiang, cong ta de zhu jianglin ta ne? Ni zhishi yige jinggao zhe, mei ge minzu dou you yige yindao zhe.
13|8|Zhenzhu zhidao mei ge nuxing de huaiyun, he zigong de shousuo he pengzhang. Zai zhu nali, wanwu shi ge you dingliang de.
13|9|Ta shi quanzhi youming de, shi weida de, shi chonggao de.
13|10|Nimen zhong qieqie siyu de, gaotankuolun de, yincang zai heiye de, chuxian zai baizhou de,(zai ta) kan lai dou shi yiyang de.
13|11|Mei geren de qianmian he houmian, dou you xuduo jiezhong er lai de tianshen, tamen feng zhenzhu de mingling lai jianhu ta. Zhenzhu biding bu biangeng renhe minzhong de qingkuang, zhidao tamen biangeng ziji de qingkuang. Dangzhenzhu yu jiang zaihai yu renhe minzhong de shihou, na zaihai shi buke kangju de. Chu zhenzhu wai, tamen jue wu baoyou zhe.
13|12|Ta shi yi dianguang zhaoshi nimen, yi yinqi nimen de kongju he xiwang, bing xingqi miyun.
13|13|Leiting zai zansong zhenzhu chaojue wanwu, zhong tianshen yin wei weiju ta er zansong ta. Ta fachu pili yi ji sha tasuo yiyu zhe. Tamen wei zhu er zhenglun, er ta shi you qiangda moulue de.
13|14|Zhenshi de qidao zhi guiyu ta, tamen she ta er qidao de (ouxiang), yidian ye buneng daying tamen de qiqiu. Dan tamen haoxiang yige ren, ba liang zhi shouzhang shen xiang shuizhong, yibian shui dadao ta de kou, qishi, shui jue bu hui dadao ta de kou de. Bu xindao zhe de qidao, zhi zai mi wu zhong.
13|15|Fan zai tiandi jian de wanwu, dou shunfu de huo mianqiang di wei zhenzhu er koutou, tamen de yinying ye zhaoxi wei ta er koutou.(Ci chu koutou!)※
13|16|Ni shuo: Shei shi tiandi de zhu? Ni shuo: Zhenzhu. Ni shuo: Nandao nimen she zhenzhu er ba naxie buneng zizhu huo fu zhe dang zuo baoyou zhe ma? Ni shuo, mangren yu fei mangren shi yiyang de ma? Hei'an yu guangming shi yiyang de ma? Tamen wei zhenzhu shulile xuduo huoban, nandao naxie huoban neng xiang zhenzhu nayang chuangzao wanwu, yizhi tamen fenbian bu chu liang zhong chuangzao ma? Ni shuo: Zhenzhu shi wanwu de chuangzao zhe, ta que shi du yi de, que shi wanneng de.
13|17|Zhenzhu cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, yiqie gouhe jiu jinliang liuxing. Shanhong zaizhe fu zha--tamen wei zhizao shoushi he qimin er ronghua de jinshu, yeyou tongyang de fu zha. Zhenzhu ruci chanming zhen wei--zhiyu zhazi ze bei chong zou, zhiyu youyi yu ren de dongxi ze liucun zai dimian shang. Zhenzhu ruci chanming xuduo biyu.
13|18|Yijing daying zhenzhu de ren, jiang shou ji meide baochou; meiyou daying zhu de ren, jiaruo tiandi shang de yiqie bi gui tamen suoyou, zai jia shang yi bei, tamen biding du yong lai zuo shujin. Zhe deng ren jiang shou yanli de qingsuan, tamen de guisu shi huo yu, na chuangpu zhen zaogao!
13|19|Cong ni de zhu jiang shi ni de, zheng shi zhenli, nandao renshi zhege daoli zhe gen mangren shi yiyang de ma? Wei you lizhi pu caineng ji zhu.
13|20|Tamen shi shijian zhenzhu de shiyue erqie bu pohuai mengyue de.
13|21|Tamen shi lianjie zhenzhu ming ren lianjie zhe de, shi jing'ai tamen de zhu, weiju yanli de qingsuan de.
13|22|Tamen shi wei qiu dezhu de xiyue er jianren de, shi jin shou bai gong de, shi mimi de he gongkai di fen she wo suo ci gei tamen de caiwu de, shi yidebaoyuan de. Zhe deng ren de chi houshi de shan guo
13|23|changzhu de leyuan, tamen jiang jinru leyuan. Tamen de zuxian, qizi he houyi zhong de shanliang zhe, dou jiang jinru leyuan. Zhong tianshen cong mei daomen jinqu jian tamen,
13|24|(shuo): Zhu nimen ping'an! Zhe shi nimen yin jianren er de de baochou, houshi de shan guozhen youmei.
13|25|Yu zhenzhu diyue, ranhou jiayi pohuai de, duanjue zhenzhu ming ren lianjie zhe de, zai difang shang jinxing pohuai de, zhe deng ren jiang bei zuzhou, jiang chi houshi de eguo.
13|26|Zhenzhu shi tasuo yiyu zhe xiangshou kuanyu de jiyang huo jiongpo de jiyang. Tamen yin jinshi de shenghuo er huanxi, ran'er jinshi de shenghuo bi qi houshi de shenghuo lai, zhishi yi zhong (zhanshi) de xiangshou.
13|27|Bu xindao de renmen shuo: Zenme meiyou yi zhong jixiang cong ta de zhu jianglin ta ne? Ni shuo: Zhen zhu biding shi tasuo yiyu zhe wu ru mitu, biding shi guiyi ta de ren zou shang zhenglu.
13|28|Tamen xindao, tamen de xinjing yin jiyi zhenzhu er anjing, zhen de, yiqie xinjing yin jiyi zhenzhu er anjing.
13|29|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, de xiang xingfu he youmei de guisu.
13|30|Wo zheyang paiqian ni qu jiaohua yige minzu, zai tamen zhiqian you xuduo minzu que yi shiqule, yibian ni dui tamen xuandu wo suo qishi ni de jingdian, tamen shi buxin zhiren zhu de. Ni shuo: Ta shi wo de zhu, chu ta zhi wai, jue wu ying shou chongbai de. Wo zhi xintuo ta, wo zhi yi ta wei yigui.
13|31|Jiaruo youyi bu “gulanjing”, keyong lai yidong shanyue, huo polie dadi, huo shi siren shuohua,(tamen bi buxin ta). Buran, yiqie shiqing zhi guizhenzhu, nandao xindao de renmen bu zhidao ma? Jiaruo zhenzhu yiyu, de bi yindao quan renlei. Bu xindao de renmen hai yaoyin ziji de xingwei er zaoshou zaiyang, huo tamen zhuzhai de fujin zaoshou zaiyang, zhidao zhenzhu de yingxu daolai. Zhenzhu que shi bu shuangyue de.
13|32|Zai ni zhiqian, you xuduo shizhe que yi bei ren chaonongle, ju wo dui bu xindao zhe huanxing. Suihou, wo chengzhi tamen. Wo de chengfa shi zenyang de ne?
13|33|Jianshi mei ge linghun de mouqiu zhe, nandao xiang na buneng jianshi de ma? Tamen wei zhenzhu shulile xuduo huoban, ni shuo: Nimen zhichu tamen de mingcheng ba. Nandao nimen ba zhenzhu zai da dishang suo bu zhidao de gaosu ta ma? Buran, nimen ju fu ci er cheng tamen wei zhenzhu de huoban. Buran, bu xindao zhe, yi wei ziji de jimou suo mihuole. Tamen bei zunao er buneng ru zhengdao. Zhenzhu shi shei mi wu, shei jiu meiyou xiangdao.
13|34|Tamen zai jinshi jiang shou chengfa, houshi de chengfa que shi geng yanli de. Tamen jue wu renhe baowei zhe yi kangju zhenzhu.
13|35|Yi yingxu jingwei zhe de leyuan, qi qingzhuang shi zheyang de: Na leyuan xia lin zhu he, qizhong de guoshi shi yongheng de, qizhong de yin ying yeshi yongheng de. Zhe shi jingwei zhe de guobao; bu xindao zhe de guobao shi huo yu.
13|36|Meng wo shangci jingdian de ren xihuan jiang shi gei ni de jingdian, tongmeng zhe dangzhong, youren fouren zhe jingdian de yibufen. Ni shuo: Wo zhi fengming chongbai zhenzhu, er bu yi wu pei ta, wo zhi haozhao ren chongbai ta, wo zhi guiyi ta.
13|37|Wo zheyang ba ta jiang shi wei alabo wen de zhihui. Zai zhishi jianglin ni zhihou, ruguo ni shuncong tamen de yuwang, namo, ni dui zhenzhu de (chengfa) jue wu renhe baohu zhe, ye jue wu renhe baowei zhe.
13|38|Zai ni zhiqian, wo que yi paiqianle xuduo shizhe, bing shangci tamen qizi he ernu. Chufei feng zhenzhu de mingling, renhe shizhe buneng zhaoshi jixiang. Mei ge qixian, ge you panding.
13|39|Zhenzhu renyi gouxiao he queding (jingdian de mingwen), zai ta na li you tian jing de yuanben.
13|40|Ruguo wo ba wo yong lai donghe tamen de xingfa zhaoshi ni yidian er,(na hui shi ni manyi), ruguo wo shi ni shou zhong, name, ni zhi fu chuanda de zeren, wo zifu qingsuan de zeren.
13|41|Nandao tamen bu zhidao ma? Wo dao tamen di difang lai suoxiao tamen de bianjing. Zhenzhu ziyou panjue, renhe ren buneng fankang qi panjue. Ta shi qingsuan shensu de.
13|42|Zai tamen zhiqian de ren, que yi shiyong jimou; dan yiqie jimou, zhi guizhenzhu, ta zhidao mei ge linghun de mouqiu.
13|43|Bu xindao zhe jiangyao zhidao, jinshi de shan guo jiang gui shei suoyou. Bu xindao de renmen shuo: Ni bushi shizhe. Ni shuo: Zhenzhu zuyi wei wo he nimen zhi jian de jianzheng, renshi tian jing de ren ye zuyi wei wo he nimen zhi jian de jianzheng.
14|1|Ai lie fu, lia mu, la yi.(Zhe shi) yi zhang jing, wo ba ta jiang shi ni, yibian ni feng zhu de mingling er ba zhongren cong chongchong hei'an zhong yinru guangming, yinru qiangda de, ke song de zhu de dadao.
14|2|Zhenzhu shi you tiandi wanwu de. Ai zai bu xindao zhe! Tamen jiang shou yanli de xingfa.
14|3|Tamen ning yao jinshi, er buyao houshi, bing zu'ai zhenzhu de dadao, erqie xiang zai qizhong xunqiu pian xiedao, zhe deng ren shi zai shen shen de mi wu zhi zhong de.
14|4|Wo bu paiqian yige shizhe ze yi, dan paiqian de shihou, zong shi yi ta de zongzu de yuyan (jiang shi jingdian), yibian ta wei tamen chanming zhengdao. Er zhenzhu shi tasuo yiyu zhe wu ru mitu, shi tasuo yiyu zhe zunxun zhenglu. Ta que shi qiangda de, que shi zhi rui de.
14|5|Wo que yi paiqian mu sa daizhe wo de xuduo jixiang qu,(wo shuo): Ni ba ni de zongzu cong chongchong hei'an zhong yinru guangming ba. Ni yingdang yi zhen zhu de yixie jinian ri tixing tamen. Duiyu mei ge jianren zhe he gan'en zhe, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
14|6|Dangshi, mu sa ceng dui ta de zongzu shuo: Nimen yingdang mingji zhen zhu ci gei nimen de endian, ta ceng shi nimen tuoli falao de chenmin. Tamen shi nimen zaoshou kuxing, tusha nimen de nanzi, liu xia nimen de nuzi, ci zhong you cong nimen de zhu jiangxia de da nan.
14|7|Dangshi, nimen de zhu ceng xuanbu shuo: Ruguo nimen ganxie, wo shi bi dui nimen en shang jia en; ruguo nimen wang'enfuyi, namo, wo de xingfa que shi yanli de.
14|8|Mu sa shuo: Ruguo nimen he da dishang de ren tongtong dou wang'enfuyi,(ye wusun yu zhenzhu), yin wei zhenzhu que shi wu qiu de, que shi ke song de.
14|9|Nimen yiqian de minzu--nu ha de zongzu, a de ren, sai mo de ren he tamen yihou de ren, zhiyou zhenzhu neng zhidao tamen--nandao zhe deng ren de xiaoxi meiyou lailin nimen ma? Tamen zu zhong de shizhe zhaoshi tamen xuduo mingzheng, dan tamen ba ziji de shouzhi charu kounei, shuo: Women biding buxin nimen suo feng de shiming, women duiyu nimen suo xuanchuan de shiqing, que shi zai shi ren bu'an di yihuo zhi zhong.
14|10|Tamen zu zhong de shizhe shuo: Nandao duiyu zhenzhu--tiandi de chuangzao zhe--hai you huaiyi ma? Ta haozhao nimen xingshan, yibian ta raoshu nimen de zuiguo, bing dui nimen huanxing dao yige dingqi. Tamen shuo: Nimen zhishi xiang women yiyang de fanren, nimen yu zuzhi women chongbai women de zuxian suo chongbai de (ouxiang), nimen zhaoshi women yige mingzheng ba!
14|11|Tamen zu zhong de yige shizhe dui tamen shuo: Women zhishi xiang nimen yiyang de fanren, dan zhenzhu shi en yu tasuo yiyu de puren. Women bu gai zhaoshi nimen renhe mingzheng, chufei feng zhenzhu de mingling, xindao zhe zhi xintuo zhenzhu.
14|12|Women zen neng buxintuo zhenzhu ne? Ta que yi yindao women zou shang zhengdao. Women shi bi renshou nimen de zhemo, rang xintuo zhe zhi xintuo zhenzhu.
14|13|Bu xindao zhe dui tamen zu zhong de shizhe shuo: Women shi bi ba nimen quzhu chujing, huozhe nimen shi bi gai xin women de zongjiao! Tamen de zhu jiu qishi tamen shuo: Wo shi bi huimie bu yi zhe,
14|14|wo shi bi shi nimen zai tamen huimie zhihou juzhu tamen di difang. Zhe shi weiju zhan zai wo mianqian (shou shenxun), erqie weiju wo de donghe zhe suode xiangshou de.
14|15|Tamen ceng yaoqiu panjue. Mei ge wangu de baonue zhe dou shiwangle.
14|16|Zai ta de shenhou, jiang you huo yu, ta jiang yin nong zhi,
14|17|yikou yikou di yin, jihu yan buxiaqu. Siwang jiang cong ge chu jianglin ta, dan ta yong bu hui si. Zai na zhong xingfa zhihou, hai you yanjun de xingfa.
14|18|Bu xin zhu zhe, tamen de shangong biru yi dui hui, zai baofeng zhi ri, bei kuangfeng chui san, tamen duiyu ziji suo mouqiu de, buneng huode yidian baochou. Zhe que shi shen shen de mi wu.
14|19|Nandao ni meiyou kanjian zhenzhu yi ben zhenli er chuangzao tiandi ma? Ruguo ta yiyu, ta jiu xiaomie nimen, er chuangzao xinren.
14|20|Zhe zai zhenzhu jue bushi kunnan de.
14|21|Tamen jiangyao yitong chulai jian zhenzhu, er nuoruo zhe jiang dui zi da de renmen shuo: Women yuanlai shi nimen de bu xia, nimen neng ti women dikang zhenzhu de yidian er xingfa ma? Tamen jiang shuo: Jiaruo zhenzhu yindao women, women ye biran yindao nimen. Women wulun jizao huo rennai, zhe zai women shi yiyang de, women jue wu binan suo.
14|22|Dang shiqing yi bei panjue de shihou, emo shuo: Zhenzhu que yi zhenshi di yingxu nimen, wo ye ceng yingxu nimen, dan wo dui nimen shuangyuele. Wo dui nimen benlai meiyou she me quanli, buguo shi wo zhaohuan nimen, er nimen xiangying wo de haozhao. Suoyi nimen buyao zebei wo, yingdang zebei ziji, wo buneng yuanjiu nimen, nimen ye buneng yuanjiu wo. Wo bu chengren yiqian nimen ceng ba wo pei zhu, bu yi zhe bi shou tongku de xingfa.
14|23|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, jiang meng zhu de yunxu er jinru na xia lin zhu he de leyuan, bing yong ju qizhong, tamen zai leyuan li de zhuci shi ping'an.
14|24|Nandao ni bu zhidao zhenzhu youguo zheyang yige biyu ma? Yiju liangyan, haobi yi ke youliang de shu, qi gen di shi shen gu de, qi zhitiao gaosong ru yun,
14|25|ping zhu de xuke, anshi jieguo. Zhenzhu wei zhongren dale xuduo bifang, yibian tamen jiqu jiaohui.
14|26|Yiju e yan, qiasi yi ke elie de shu, cong da dishang bei liangenba qu, jue meiyou yidian anding.
14|27|Zai jinshi he houshi, zhenzhu yi jiangu de yanci shi xindao zhe jianxin, zhenzhu shi bu yi zhe wu ru mitu, zhenzhu shi weisuoyuwei de.
14|28|Nandao ni meiyou kanjian na deng ren ma? Tamen dui zhenzhu wang'enfuyi, bing shi ziji de zongzu xianyu miewang zhi jing
14|29|huo yu zhi zhong. Tamen jiang jinru huo yu, na guisu zhen zaogao,
14|30|tamen wei zhenzhu shuli xuduo pidi, yibian tamen shi ren beili zhu de dadao. Ni shuo: Nimen xiangshou ba, yinwei nimen bi guiyu huo yu!
14|31|Ni yao dui wo di naxie xindao de puren, shuo: Rang tamen jin shou bai gong, bingqie zai na ji wu maimai you wu youyi zhi ri lailin yiqian, mimi de he gongkai di fen she wo suo ciyu tamen de caiwu.
14|32|Zhenzhu chuangzao tiandi, bing cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, er jie yushui shengchan ge zhong guoshi, zuowei nimen de jiyang; ta wei nimen zhifu chuanbo, yibian tamen feng ta de mingling er hangxing haizhong; ta wei nimen zhifu heliu;
14|33|ta wei nimen zhifu ri yue, shi qi jingchang yunxing, ta wei nimen zhifu zhouye.
14|34|Nimen dui zhu de yaoqiu, ta dui nimen dou you suo shangci. Ruguo nimen jisuan zhenzhu de enhui, nimen buneng jiayi tongji. Ren que shi hen bu yi de, que shi wang'enfuyi de.
14|35|Dangshi yi bo la xin shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni shi zhege difang bian cheng anquan de, qiu ni shi wo he wo de zisun, yuanli ouxiang chongbai.
14|36|Wo de zhu a! Ouxiangmen que yi shi xuduo ren mi wu. Shei shuncong wo, ta que shi wo de tongdao; shei weikang wo, namo, ni shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
14|37|Women de zhu a! Wo que yi shi wo de bufen houyi zhu zai yige meiyou zhuangjia de shangu li, zhu zai ni de jin fang fujin--women de zhu a!--Yibian tamen jin shou bai gong, qiu ni shi yibufen ren de xin yilian tamen, qiu ni yi yibufen guoshi gongji tamen, yibian tamen ganxie.
14|38|Women de zhu a! Ni biding zhidao women suo yinhui de he women suo biaobai de. Tiandi jian meiyou she me shiwu neng manguo zhenzhu.
14|39|Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Ta zai wo laomai de shihou, shangci wo yi sima yi he yi si ha ge. Wo de zhu que shi tingqu qi chou de.
14|40|Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni shi wo he yibufen houyi jin shou bai gong. Women de zhu a! Qiu ni jieshou wo de qi chou.
14|41|Women de zhu a! Qiu ni zai qingsuan shixian zhi ri raoshu wo he wo de shuangqin he xinshimen.
14|42|Ni jue buyao yiwei zhenzhu hushi bu yi zhe de xingwei, ta zhi dui tamen huanxing dao dengyan de rizi,
14|43|(zai na ri), tamen jiang taizhe tou wang qian benzou, tamen de yanjing bu gan kan ziji, tamen de xin shi kongxu de.
14|44|Ni yingdang jinggao zhongren, jianglai yao you zheyang de yi ri, xingfa jiang lailin tamen, er bu yi zhe jiang shuo: Women de zhu a! Qiu ni rang women yanchi dao yige linjin de dingqi, yibian women xiangying ni de haozhao, shuncong ni de shizhe. Nandao nimen yiqian meiyou fashi shuo, nimen jue bu hui miewang ma?
14|45|Nimen ceng juzhu zai zi kui zhe suo zhu di difang, erqie mingbai wo shi zenyang chuzhi tamen de. Wo ye wei nimen dale xuduo bifang.
14|46|Tamen que yi yong jimou, zai zhenzhu nali, you tamen de jimou (de guobao). Tamen de jimou, buzu yi yidong qun shan.
14|47|Ni jue buyao yiwei zhenzhu dui ta de shizhe shuangyue. Zhenzhu que shi qiangda de, que shi cheng e de.
14|48|Zai na ri, zhe dadi yao bian cheng bie de dadi, zhu tian ye yao bian cheng wei bie de zhu tian, tamen yao chulai jian du yi de, quanneng de zhenzhu.
14|49|Zai na ri, ni jiang kanjian zui renmen daizhe zhigu, cheng shuang cheng dui di bei kunbang qilai;
14|50|tamen de chenyi shi yong liqing zuo de, huo jiang longzhao tamen de lian.
14|51|Yibian zhenzhu yiju ge ren suo xing de shan e er jiayi baochou. Zhen zhu que shi qingsuan shensu de.
14|52|Zhe shi dui zhongren de chongfen de biaoshi, yibian tamen yinci er shou jinggao, yibian tamen zhidao ta zhishi du yi de bei chongbai zhe, yibian you lizhi de ren jiqu jiaohui.
15|1|Ai lie fu, lia mu, la yi. Zhexie shi tian jing--mingbai de “gulanjing” de jie wen.
15|2|Buxindao zhe huoxu yao xiwang tamen yuan shi guishun de.
15|3|Ni tingren tamen chihe wanle ba! Ni tingren tamen shou xiwang de youhuo ba! Yinwei tamen bujiu jiu hui zhidao de.
15|4|Wo bu huimie yige chengshi ze yi, dan huimie ta, jiu you yige kezhi de dingqi.
15|5|Renhe minzu dou buneng xian qi dingqi er miewang, ye buneng hou qi dingqi er lunsang.
15|6|Tamen shuo: Shouxiang shi jiaohui de ren a! Ni que shi yige fengzi.
15|7|Ni zen bu zhaoshi women yixie tianshen ne? Ruguo ni shi shuo shihua de.
15|8|Wo zhi ping zhenli er jiang tianshen, dao na shi, tamen shi bu meng huanxing de.
15|9|Wo que yi jiang shi jiaohui, wo que shi jiaohui de baohu zhe.
15|10|Zai ni zhiqian, wo que yi paiqianle xuduo shizhe, qu jiaohua gudai de ge zongpai.
15|11|Meiyou yige shizhe lailin tamen ze yi, dan you shizhe lailin, tamen dou jiayi chaoxiao.
15|12|Wo zheyang shi aihao chaoxiao shenru zui renmen de xin.
15|13|Tamen bu xin wo de jiaohui, qishi, guren de changdao yi shiqule.
15|14|Jiaruo wo wei tamen kaipi yidao tianmen, er tamen cong na dao tianmen jixu deng tian,
15|15|tamen biding shuo: Women de yanjing shou mengbile, buran, women shi zhongle moshu de minzhong.
15|16|Wo que yi zai tianshang chuangzaole (shi'er) gong, wo wei guancha zhe er xiushi tiankong.
15|17|Wo baohuzhe tian, buxu renhe shou zuzhou de emo deyi qinru,
15|18|dan qieting de emo ze you mingxian de liuxing gan shang ta.
15|19|Wo zhankaile dadi, bing ba xuduo shanyue anzhi zai da dishang, erqie shi ge zhong junheng de dongxi sheng chulai.
15|20|Wo zai da dishang wei nimen he nimen suo buneng gongyang zhe er chuangzaole xuduo shenghuo ziliao.
15|21|Mei yi zhong shiwu, wo zheli dou you qi cangku, wo zhi yi dingshu jiangxia ta.
15|22|Wo paiqian zirun de feng, wo jiu cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, yi gongji nimen yinliao, nimen jue bushi yushui de xu cang zhe.
15|23|Wo que shi neng shi wanwu sheng, neng shi wanwu si de; wo que shi wanwu de jicheng zhe.
15|24|Wo que yi zhidao nimen zhong xianjin de, wo que yi zhidao nimen zhong houjin de.
15|25|Ni de zhu biding jihe tamen. Ta que shi zhi rui de, que shi quanzhi de.
15|26|Wo que yi yong heise de chengxing de niantu chuangzaole ren.
15|27|Yiqian, wo ceng yong liehuo chuangzaole jingling.
15|28|Dangshi, ni de zhu ceng dui tianshenmen shuo: Wo biding yao yong heise de niantu suzao renxiang er chuangzao ren.
15|29|Dang wo ba ta su cheng, erqie ba wo de jingshen chui ru ta de suxiang de shihou, nimen yingdang dui ta fufu koutou.
15|30|Suihou, tianshenmen yitong koutou,
15|31|wei du yi bo lie si bu ken koutou.
15|32|Zhu shuo: Yi bo lie si a! Ni zenme bu koutou ne?
15|33|Ta shuo: Ni yong heise niantu su chengren xiang er chuangzao de ren, wo bu gai xiang ta koutou.
15|34|Zhu shuo: Ni cong zheli chuqu ba. Yinwei ni que shi bei fangzhu de.
15|35|Ni bi zao zuzhou, zhidao baoying ri.
15|36|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni dui wo huanxing, zhidao renlei fuhuo zhi ri.
15|37|Zhu shuo: Ni que shi bei huanxing
15|38|dao kezhi de riqi.
15|39|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Ni yi panding wo shi mi wu de, suoyi wo shi bi zai da dishang yi zui'e youhuo tamen, wo biding yao shi tamen yitong mi wu.
15|40|Chufei tamen zhong ni suo xuanba de puren.
15|41|Zhu shuo: Zhe shi wo yingdang weichi de zhenglu.
15|42|Wo de puren, ni dui tamen jue wu quanli, chufei naxie shuncong ni de mi wu zhe.
15|43|Huo yu biding shi tamen quanti de yueding di difang.
15|44|Huo yu you 7 daomen, mei dao menjiang shourong tamen zhong bei pai ding de yibufen ren.
15|45|Jingwei zhemen biding zai yixie leyuan he yuanquanzhi jian,
15|46|nimen pingping'an'an di jinru leyuan ba!
15|47|Wo qingchu tamen xiongzhong de yuanhen, tamen jiang chengwei dixiong, zai gao ta shang xiang dui er zuo.
15|48|Tamen zai nali bu ganjue pifa, tamen jue bu bei zhu chu.
15|49|Ni gaosu wo de pu renmen, wo que shi zhi she de, zhi ci de;
15|50|wo de xingfa que shi tongku de.
15|51|Ni yingdang dui tamen xushu yi bo la xin de kerenmen de gushi.
15|52|Dangshi, tamen jinqu jian ta, shuo: Zhu ni ping an. Ta shuo: Women que shi weiju nimen de.
15|53|Tamen shuo: Ni buyao weiju, women dique yi yige congming de nanhai xiang ni baoxi.
15|54|Ta shuo: Wo yi laomai, nimen hai xiang wo baoxi ma? Nimen yi shenme xiang wo baoxi ne?
15|55|Tamen shuo: Women ping zhenli er xiang ni baoxi, suoyi ni buyao juewang.
15|56|Ta shuo: Chu mi wu zhe wai, shei hui juewang yu zhenzhu de enhui ne?
15|57|Ta shuo: Shizhemen a! Nimen you she me chaishi ne?
15|58|Tamen shuo: Women feng pai qu chengzhi yiqun fanzui de minzhong.
15|59|Lu te de jiazu chuwai, women que yao ba tamen quandou jiu chulai;
15|60|dan ta de qizi chuwai, women yi yuding ta he qiyu de ren tong shou xingfa.
15|61|Dang shizhemen lai dao lu te de jiali de shihou,
15|62|ta shuo: Nimen que shi yixie mosheng de ren.
15|63|Tamen shuo: Buran; women ba tamen yixiang zhenglun de (xingfa) dai lai gei nile.
15|64|Women ba zhenli dai lai gei nile, women que shi chengshi de.
15|65|Ni yingdang daizhe ni de jiazu zai shenye chuxing, ni yao gen zai tamen de houmian, nimen zhong de renhe ren ye buyao huitou kan. Nimen yingdang wang qian zou, yizhi zou dao nimen fengming daoda di difang.
15|66|Wo qishi ta zhege panjue: Jiushi zhe deng ren, zai zaochen jiang bei genchu.
15|67|Cheng li de jumin xinran er lai,
15|68|ta shuo: Zhexie shi wo de keren, nimen buyao lingru wo,
15|69|nimen yingdang jingwei zhenzhu, nimen buyao cha ru wo.
15|70|Tamen shuo: Nandao women meiyou jinzhi ni yu shiren wanglai ma?
15|71|Ta shuo: Zhexie shi wo de nu'er, ruguo nimen yao gan shenme.
15|72|Zhi ni de shouming fashi, tamen bi jiang fanghuang yu ziji de diankuang zhi zhong.
15|73|Nahan sheng zai ri chu shi xijile tamen.
15|74|Wo shi nage shi zhen tianfandifu, bing shi tao shixiang yudian ban jiangluo zai tamen shenshang.
15|75|Duiyu neng kaocha zhe, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
15|76|Nage shi zhen que shi zai yitiao rengran cunzai de daolushang de.
15|77|Duiyu xindao zhe, ci zhong que youyi zhong jixiang.
15|78|Na conglin de jumin que shi bu yi de,
15|79|guwo chengzhile tamen. Zhe liang ge difang dou zai pingtan de lu shang.
15|80|Shigu de jumin que yi fouren shizhemen.
15|81|Wo que yi ba wo de xuduo jixiang zhaoshi tamen, dan tamen beilile ta.
15|82|Tamen anquan de zao shan wei wu,
15|83|dan nahan sheng zai zaochen xijile tamen.
15|84|Tamen suo mouqiu de, duiyu tamen wujiyushi.
15|85|Wo zhi ping zhenli chuangzao tiandi wanwu, fuhuo shi shi biding lailin de. Suoyi ni yingdang wenhe di yuanliang zhongren.
15|86|Ni de zhu que shi chuangzao wanwu de zhu, que shi quan zhi de.
15|87|Wo que yi shangci ni changchang fanfu songdu de qi jie jing wen he weida de “gulanjing”.
15|88|Ni buyao jiyu wo suo shi tamen zhong ge deng ren suo xiangshou de shiwu, ni buyao wei tamen er bei'ai. Ni yingdang wenhe di duidai xinshimen.
15|89|Ni shuo: Wo que shi tanshuai de jinggao zhe.
15|90|Na zhengru wo suo jiang shi fenpei zhemen de (dongxi) yiyang de,
15|91|tamen ba “gulanjing” fenge cheng ruogan zhiti.
15|92|Zhi ni de zhu fashi, wo bi jiang tamen quanti jiayi shenwen
15|93|shenwen tamen shengqian de xingwei.
15|94|Ni yingdang gongkai xuanbu ni suo feng de mingling, erqie bi kai yi wu pei zhu zhe.
15|95|Zai duifu chaoxiao zhe fangmian, wo bi shi ni manzu.
15|96|Chaoxiao zhe chu zhenzhu wai hai chongbai bie de shenling, bujiu tamen jiu hui zhidaole.
15|97|Wo que yi zhidao ni wei tamen de lanyan er fanmen.
15|98|Ni yingdang zansong ni de zhu chaojue wanwu, ni yingdang yu zhongren yiqi koutou,
15|99|ni yingdang chongbai ni de zhu, zhidao na wuyi de xiaoxi lailin.
16|1|Zhenzhu de mingling biding lailin, suoyi nimen bubi yaoqiu qi zaori shixian, zansong zhenzhu chaojue wanwu, ta chao hu tamen suoyong yi pei ta de.
16|2|Ta shi tianshenmen feng ta de mingling, xietong jingshen, jianglin tasuo yiyu de puren, shuo: Nimen yingdang jinggao shiren shuo: Chu wo zhi wai, jue wu ying shou chongbai de, suoyi nimen yingdang jingwei wo.
16|3|Ta ping zhenli chuangzaole tiandi, ta chao hu tamen suoyong yi pei ta de.
16|4|Ta yong jingye chuangzaole ren, er ren que turan bian chengle (ta de) mingxian de duishou.
16|5|Ta chuangzaole shengchu, nimen keyi qi mao he pi yuhan, keyi qi ru he rou chongji, hai you xuduo yichu.
16|6|Nimen ba shengchu gan hui jia huo fang chuqu chi cao de shihou, shengchu duiyu nimen dou you guangcai.
16|7|Shengchu ba nimen de huowu tuo yun dao nimen xu jing kunnan caineng daoda di difang qu. Nimen de zhu que shi zhiren de, que shi zhi ci de.
16|8|Ta chuangzao ma, luo, lu, yi gong nimen qi cheng, yi zuo nimen de zhuangshi. Ta hai chuangzao nimen suo bu zhidao de dongxi.
16|9|Zhenzhu fuze zhishi zhengdao de zeren. Youxie daolu shi pian xie de, jiaruo ta yiyu, ta bi jiang nimen quanti yinru zhengdao.
16|10|Ta cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, nimen keyi yong zuo yinliao, nimen lai yi fangmu de shumu yin zhi er shengzhang.
16|11|Ta wei nimen er shengchan zhuangjia, youganlan, ye zao, putao he ge zhong guoshi. Duiyu neng siwei de minzhong, ci zhong que youyi zhong jixiang.
16|12|Ta wei nimen er zhifule zhouye he ri yue, qunxing dou shi yin ta de yizhi er bei zhifu de; duiyu neng lijie de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
16|13|(Ta you wei nimen er zhifu) tasuo wei nimen chuangzao yu dadi de gese wupin, duiyu neng jiqu jiaohui de minzhong, ci zhong que youyi zhong jixiang.
16|14|Ta zhifu haiyang, yibian nimen yu qu qizhong de xian rou, zuo nimen de shipin; huo caiqu qizhong de zhubao, zuo nimen de zhuangshi. Ni kan chuanbo zai qizhong polang er xing, yibian nimen xunqiu ta de enhui, yibian nimen ganxie.
16|15|Ta zai dadishang anzhi xuduo shanyue, yimian da di dongdang, er nimen bude anju. Ta kaipi xuduo heliu he daolu, yibian nimen zunxun zhenglu.
16|16|Ta sheli xuduo biaozhi, tamen jiezhu naxie biaozhi he xingsu er zunxun zhenglu.
16|17|Nandao zaowuzhu tong buneng chuangzao de (ouxiang) shi yiyang de ma? Nimen zenme bu jiqu jiaohui ne?
16|18|Ruguo nimen yao jisuan zhenzhu de enhui, nimen shi wufa tongji de. Zhenzhu que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
16|19|Zhenzhu zhidao nimen suoyinhui de, he nimen suo biaobai de.
16|20|Tamen she zhenzhu er qidao de buneng chuangzao renhe wu, er tamen shi bei chuangzao de.
16|21|Tamen shi si de, bushi huo de, tamen bu zhidao chongbai zhemen jiang zai he shi fuhuo.
16|22|Nimen suo yingdang chongbai de shi weiyi de shou chongbai zhe. Buxin houshi de ren, tamen de xin shi fouren de, tamen shi zi da de.
16|23|Wuyi de, zhenzhu zhidao tamen suo yinhui de, he tamen suo biaobai de, ta que shi bu xi'ai zi da zhe de.
16|24|Youren wen tamen: Nimen de zhu ceng jiang shi shenme? Tamen shuo: Guren de shenhua.
16|25|Yibian tamen zai fuhuo ri chengdan ziji de quanbu zeren, yiji bei tamen wuzhi di jiayi wudao zhe de yibufen zeren. Zhen de, tamen suo chengdan de zhen elie!
16|26|Qian ren que yi yong jimou, dan zhenzhu ba tamen de jianzhu wu chedi jiayi cuihui, er tamen de wuding luo zai tamen de shenshang. Xingfa cong tamen liao xiangbudao di difang lailin tamen.
16|27|Ranhou zai fuhuo ri ta yao lingru tamen, bing shenwen tamen shuo: Wo naxie huoban--nimen weile tamen er yuxin shimen xiang zhenglun de--rujin zai nali ne? You xueshi zhe jiangyao shuo: Lingru he xingfa jinri bi guiyu bu xindao zhe.
16|28|Tamen zai zi kui de qingkuang xia, tianshenmen shi tamen siwang. Tamen biaoshi qufu, shuo: Women meiyou fanguo shen me zui'e. Buran! Zhenzhu que shi quanzhi nimen de xingwei de.
16|29|Tamen bei ya jin huo yu er yong ju qizhong. Zi da zhe de zhuchu zhen elie!
16|30|Youren wen jingwei zhe shuo: Nimen de zhu ceng jiang shi shenme? Tamen shuo: Ta jiang shi shan yan. Xingshan zhe zai jinshi jiang xiangshou meiman de shenghuo, er houshi de zhuzhai que shi geng hao de. Jing'ai zhe de zhuzhai zhen youmei.
16|31|Chang zai de leyuan jiang ren sui tamen jinqu, naxie leyuan xia lin zhu he, qizhong you tamen suo yiyu de. Zhenzhu zheyang baochou jingwei zhe.
16|32|Tamen zai lianghao de qingkuang xia, tianshenmen shi tamen siwang. Tian shen dui tamen shuo: Zhu nimen ping'an, nimen keyi yinwei ziji de shangong er jinru leyuan.
16|33|(Bu xindao zhe) zhi neng dengdai tianshenmen lailin tamen, huo dengdai ni de zhu de mingling jianglin. Zai tamen zhiqian de ren jiushi zheyang zuo de. Zhenzhu meiyou kui wang tamen, dan tamen que kui wangle ziji.
16|34|Suo yi tamen bi zaoshou tamen de xingwei de e bao, er tamen yixiang chaoxiao de (xingfa) jiang baowei tamen.
16|35|Yi wu pei zhu zhe shuo: Jiaruo zhenzhu yiyu, ze women he women de zuxian bu hui she ta er chongbai renhe wu de, women ye bu hui shanzi jiechu renhe wu de. Zai tamen zhiqian de ren, ceng zheyang zuoguole. Shizhemen zhi fu mingbai de chuanda de zeren.
16|36|Wo zai mei ge minzu zhong, que yi paiqian yige shizhe, shuo: Nimen dang chongbai zhenzhu, dang yuanli emo. Dan tamen zhong you zhenzhu suoyindao de, youyingdang mi wu de. Gu nimen dang zai dadishang luxing, yingdang guancha fouren (shizhe) de renmen de jieju shi zenyang de.
16|37|Ruguo nimen rewang tamen huode yindao, namo,(ni de rewang shi turan de), zhenzhu bu yindao na wudao ren zhe, tamen jue meiyou renhe yuanzhu zhe.
16|38|Tamen zhi zhenzhu er fachu zui yanzhong de shiyan, shuo: Zhenzhu bu shi siren fuhuo. Buran! Zhe shi ta yingdang shijian de nuoyan. Dan shiren daban bu zhidao.
16|39|(Ta jiang shi tamen fuhuo), yibian ta wei tamen chanming tamen suo zhenglun de shifei, bingqie rang buxindao zhe zhidao ziji yuan shi shuohuang de.
16|40|Dang wo yao chuangzao yi jian shiwu de shihou, wo zhi dui ta shuo sheng you, ta jiu youle.
16|41|Zai bei yapo zhihou, wei zhenzhu er qianju zhe, wo zai jinshi shi bi shi tamen huode yige youmei de zhuchu, houshi de baochou shi geng da de, jiaruo tamen zhidao.
16|42|Tamen shi jianren de, shi xinlai tamen de zhu de.
16|43|Zai ni zhiqian, wo zhi paiqianle wo suo qishi de yixie nanzi. Nimen yingdang qingjiao shen ming jiaohui zhe, ruguo nimen bu zhidao.
16|44|(Wo ceng paiqian tamen) daizhe yixie mingzheng he jingdian,(qu jiaohua zhongren), wo jiang shi ni jiaohui, yibian ni dui zhongren chanming tamen suo shou de qishi, yibian tamen siwei.
16|45|Shiyong guiji yi zuo'e zhe, nandao bupa zhenzhu shi tamen sui dimian er xianluo, huo xingfa cong tamen liao xiangbudao di difang lailin tamen ma?
16|46|Huo zai tamen de lutu zhong chengzhi tamen, er tamen jue buneng taobi.
16|47|Huo zhujian chengzhi tamen, yinwei nimen de zhu que shi zhi ai de, que shi zhi ci de.
16|48|Nandao tamen meiyou guancha zhenzhu suo chuangzao de wanwu ma? Ge wu de yinying, pianxiang zuobian he youbian, wei zhenzhu er koutou, tongshi tamen shi beijian de.
16|49|Tiandi jian de dongwu he tianshenmen, dou zhi wei zhenzhu er koutou, tamen bu ganzi da.
16|50|Tamen weiju zai tamen shangmian de zhuzai, tamen zunxing ziji suo feng de mingling.(Ci chu koutou!)※
16|51|Zhenzhu shuo: Nimen buyao chongbai liang ge zhuzai, ying shou chongbai de, zhishi yige zhuzai. Suoyi nimen yingdang zhi weiju wo.
16|52|Tiandi wanwu zhishi ta de, shuncong changchang zhi guiyu ta. Nandao nimen she zhenzhu er jingwei ta wu ma?
16|53|Fan nimen suo xiangshou de enhui dou shi cong zhenzhu jiangxia de. Ranhou, dang nimen zaonan de shihou, nimen zhi xiang ta qidao.
16|54|Ranhou, dang ta jiechu nimen de huannan de shihou, nimen zhong youyibufen ren, like yi wu pei tamen de zhu,
16|55|yizhi gufu tasuo shangci tamen de enhui, nimen xiangshou ba. Bujiu nimen jiu yao zhidaole.
16|56|Wo suo gongji tamen de caichan, tamen yi qizhong de yibufen qu gongfeng naxie wuzhi de (ouxiang). Zhi zhenzhu fashi, guanyu nimen suo niezao de (shiwu), nimen bi shoushen wen.
16|57|Tamen yi nu'er guizhenzhu--zansong zhenzhu, chaojue wanwu--er yi tamen suo yuanwang de gui ziji.
16|58|Dang tamen zhong de yige ren ting shuo ziji de qi zi sheng nu'er de shihou, ta de lian anran shise, erqie manfu laosao.
16|59|Ta wei zhege ehao er bu yu zongzu huimian, ta duofang kaolu: Jiujing shi renru baoliu ta ne? Haishi ba ta huomai zai tu li ne? Zhen de, tamen de panduan zhen elie.
16|60|Bu xin houshi zhe, you e li; zhenzhu you dianxing. Ta que shi quanneng de, que shi zhi rui de.
16|61|Ruguo zhenzhu wei shiren de bu yi er chengzhi tamen, namo, ta bu liu yige ren zai da dishang, dan ta rang tamen yanchi dao yige dingqi, dang tamen de dingqi lailin de shihou, tamen bude yanchi yi shashi,(dang qi wei lailin de shihou), tamen buneng tiqian yi shashi.
16|62|Tamen yi ziji suo yanwu de guizhenzhu, tamen wangyan ziji jiang shou zui jia de baochou. Wuyi de, tamen jiang shou huo yu de baochou. Tamen shi bei yiqi de.
16|63|Zhi zhen zhu fashi, zai ni zhiqian, wo que yi paiqian xuduo shizhe qu jiaohua ge minzu; dan emo yi tamen de xingwei mihuo tamen, suo yi jintian ta shi tamen de baohu zhe, tamen jiang shou tongku de xingfa.
16|64|Wo jiang shi zhe bu jingdian, zhi wei shi ni dui tamen chanming tamen suo zhenglun de (shifei), bingqie yi zhe bu jingdian zuowei xindao de minzhong de xiangdao he enhui.
16|65|Zhen zhu cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, bing jie yushui shi yi si de da di fuhuo; dui shanyu tinghua de minzhong, ci zhong que youyi zhong jixiang.
16|66|Zai shengchu zhong, duiyu nimen, que you yi zhong jiaoxun. Wo shi nimen de yin na cong shengchu fu nei de fen he xue zhi jian tichu de you chunjie you kekou de ruzhi.
16|67|Nimen yong ye zao he putao niang zhi chunjiu he jiamei de jiyang, duiyu neng lijie de minzhong, ci zhong que you yi zhong jixiang.
16|68|Ni de zhu ceng qishi mifeng: Ni keyi zhu fang zai shanshang he shu shang, yiji renmen suo jianzao de fengfang li.
16|69|Ranhou, ni cong mei zhong guoshi shang chi yidian, bing xunfu de zunxun ni de zhu de daolu. Jiang youyi zhong yanse butong, er keyizhi bing de yinliao, cong ta de fu zhong tu chulai; duiyu neng siwei de minzhong, ci zhong que youyi zhong jixiang.
16|70|Zhenzhu chuangzao nimen, ranhou shi nimen siwang. Nimen zhong youren fu fan yu yisheng zhong zui elie de jieduan, yi zhi ta zai you zhishi zhihou you bian de yi wu suo zhi. Zhenzhu que shi quanzhi de, que shi quanneng de.
16|71|Zai jiyang shang, zhenzhu shi nimen zhong yibufen ren chaoyue ling yibufen ren, jiyang youhou zhe jue bu yuan ba ziji de jiyang rang ji ziji de nupu, cong'er tamen zai jiyang shang yu ziji pingdeng, nandao tamen fouren zhenzhu de enhui ma?
16|72|Zhenzhu yi nimen de tonglei zuo nimen de qizi, bing wei nimen cong qizi chuangzao ersun. Zhenzhu hai yi jiamei de shiwu gongji nimen. Nandao tamen xinyang xuwang, er gufu zhu en ma?
16|73|Tamen she zhenzhu er chongbai (ouxiang), na shi buneng wei tamen zhuchi cong tianshang jiangxia de he cong dishang shengchu de yidian jiyang, erqie hao wu nengli de.
16|74|Nimen buyao wei zhenzhuda biyu. Zhenzhu zhidao, er nimen bu zhidao.
16|75|Zhenzhuda yige biyu: Yige nuli, buneng ziyou chuli renhe shiwu, yige ziyou ren, wo shangci ta you hou de jiyang, er ta mimi de he gongkai di jiayi shishe; tamen lia ren shi yiyang de ma? Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Dan tamen daban bu zhidao.
16|76|Zhenzhu you da yige biyu: Liang ge nanren, yige shi yaba, shenme shi ye buneng zuo, que shi ta zhuren de leizhui, wulun zhuren dafa ta dao nali qu, dou buneng dai yidian fuli huilai; ling yige zou de shi zhenglu, ta quan ren zhuchi gongdao. Tamen lia ren shi yiyang de ma?
16|77|Tiandi de youxuan zhishi zhenzhu de. Fuhuo shike de daolai, zhi zai zhuan shunjian, huo geng wei xunsu. Zhenzhu duiyu wanshi, que shi quanneng de.
16|78|Zhenzhu shi nimen cong mu fu chusheng, nimen shenme ye bu zhidao, ta wei nimen chuangzao ermu he xinling, yibian nimen ganxie.
16|79|Nandao tamen meiyou kanjian zai kongzhong bei zhifu de qun niao ma? Zhiyou zhenzhu weichi tamen; duiyu xindao de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
16|80|Zhenzhu yi nimen de jia wei nimen anju zhi suo, yi shengchu de pige, wei nimen de fangwu, nimen zai qicheng zhi ri he zhu dingzhi ri, dou ganjue qi qingbian. Ta yi mianyangmao, luotuo mao he shan yang mao gong nimen zhizao jiaju he zhanshi de xiangshou.
16|81|Zhenzhu yi tasuo chuangzao de dongxi zuo nimen de zhe yin, yi qun shan zuo nimen de yinni chu, yi yifu gong nimen fangshu (he yuhan), yi kuijia gong nimen fangyu chuangshang. Ta ruci wancheng ta dui nimen de enhui, yibian nimen shunfu.
16|82|Ruguo tamen weibei zhengdao, namo, ni zhi fu mingbai chuanda de zeren.
16|83|Tamen renshi zhenzhu de enhui, dan jiayi fouren, tamen daban shi wang'enfuyi de.
16|84|Zai na ri, wo yao zai mei ge minzu zhong tuiju yige jianzheng, ranhou, bu xindao zhe bude wei ziji bianhu, ye bude xiang tamen taohao.
16|85|Dang bu yi zhe kanjian xingfa de shihou, tamen bude jianxing, ye bude huanxing.
16|86|Dang yi wu pei zhu zhe kanjian tamen de pei zhu de shihou, tamen jiangyao shuo: Women de zhu a! Zhexie shi women de pei zhu, women ceng she ni er qidao tamen. Naxie pei zhujiang huida tamen shuo: Nimen que shi shuohuang de.
16|87|Zai na ri, tamen jiang xiang zhenzhu biaoshi qufu, er tamen suo niezao zhe jiang huibi tamen.
16|88|Bu xindao erqie zu'ai zhu dao zhe, wo jiang yin tamen de pohuai er zengjia tamen suo shou de xingfa.
16|89|Wo yao zai mei ge minzu zhong, tuiju tamen zu zhong de yige jianzheng, lai fanzheng tamen, zai na ri, wo yao tuiju ni lai fanzheng zhe deng ren. Wo ceng jiang shi zhe bu jingdian, chanming wanshi, bing zuo guishun zhe de xiangdao, enhui he xixun.
16|90|Zhenzhu dique ming ren gongping, xingshan, shi ji qinqi, bing jin ren yinluan, zuo'e shi, badao; ta quan jie nimen, yibian nimen jiqu jiaohui.
16|91|Dang nimen dijie mengyue de shihou, nimen yingdang luxing. Nimen ji yi zhenzhu wei nimen de baozheng zhe, ze dijie mengyue zhihou jiu buyao weibei shiyan. Zhenzhu dique zhidao nimen de xingwei.
16|92|Nimen buyao xiang nage fu ren, ta ba fangzhi de hen jieshi de xian you fen chai cheng ruogan lu; nimen yi mengshi wei huxiang qizha de shouduan, yinwei zhe yizu bi na yizu hai yao fushu. Zhen zhu zhi yi ci shi kaoyan nimen. Fuhuo ri, ta bi wei nimen chanming nimen suo zhenglun de shifei.
16|93|Jiaruo zhen zhu yiyu, ta bi shi nimen chengwei yige minzu; dan ta shi tasuo yiyu zhe wu ru mitu, shi tasuo yiyu zhe zunxun zhenglu. Nimen shibi yao wei nimen de xingwei er shoushen wen.
16|94|Nimen buyao yi mengshi wei huxiang qizha de shouduan; yimian zhan wen zhihou zai shizu, er nimen jiang yinwei zu'ai zhen zhu de dadao er changshi zaihuo, nimen hai yao shou zhongda de xingfa.
16|95|Nimen buyao yi lianjia chumai zhenzhu de mengyue; zai zhenzhu nali de, duiyu nimen shi geng hao de, ruguo nimen zhidao.
16|96|Nimen suoyou de shi yao hao jin de, zai zhenzhu nali de shi wuqiong de. Wo shi biyao yi jianren zhe suo xing de zuida shangong baochou tamen.
16|97|Fan xingshan de nannu xinshi, wo shi biyao shi tamenguo yi zhong meiman de shenghuo, wo shi biyao yi tamen suo xing de zuida shangong baochou tamen.
16|98|Dang ni yao songdu “gulanjing” de shihou, ni yingdang qiu zhenzhu baohu, yi fang shou zuzhou de emo de ganrao.
16|99|Dui xindao erqie xinlai zhenzhu zhe, ta hao wu quanli.
16|100|Ta de quanli zhi xianyu he ta jiao pengyou, erqie yi ta pei zhu zhe.
16|101|Dang wo yi yi jie jing wen diaohuan ling yi jie jing wen de shihou--zhenzhu zhidao ziji suo jiang shi de--tamen shuo: Ni zhishi yige niezao zhe. Buran! Tamen daban shi bu zhidao de.
16|102|Shengling cong ni de zhu nali jiang shi zhe bu baohan zhenli de jingdian, yibian ta shi xindao zhe jianding, bingyong zuo gui xinzhe de xiangdao he xixun.
16|103|Wo dique zhidao, tamen shuoguo: Zhe zhishi yige fanren suo chuanshou de. Tamen suo qingxiang di nage ren de yuyan shi hua wairen (de yuyan), er zhe (bu jingdian de yuyan) shi mingbai de alabo yu.
16|104|Buxin zhenzhu de jixiang zhe, zhenzhu biding bu yindao tamen, er tamen jiang shou tongku de xingfa.
16|105|Buxin zhenzhu de jixiang zhe, cai shi niezaole huangyan de, zhe deng ren que shi shuohuang de.
16|106|Ji xin zhenzhu zhihou, you biaoshi buxin zhe--chufei bei po xuancheng buxin, neixin que wei xinyang er jianding zhe--wei buxin er xinqing shuchang zhe jiang zao tianqian, bing shou zhongda de xingfa.
16|107|Zhe shi yinwei tamen ning ai jinshi shenghuo er bu ai houshi, ye yin wei zhenzhu bu yindao bu xindao de minzhong.
16|108|Tamen shi zhenzhu jiang fengbi qi xinling he shiting de ren. Zhe deng ren shi qingshuai de.
16|109|Wuyi de, tamen zai houshi zheng shi kui she zhe.
16|110|Ranhou, ni de zhu duiyu beihai zhihou qianju, ranhou fendou, erqie jianren zhe, ni de zhu zai na zhihou que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
16|111|(Ni huiyi) zai na ri, mei ge linghun dou lai wei ziji bianhu, er mei ge linghun dou de xiangshou ziji xingwei de wanquan de baochou. Tamen bu shou kui wang.
16|112|Zhenzhuda yige biyu: Yige shi zhen, yuan shi anquan de, anwen de, fengfu de jiyang cong ge fang yun lai, dan zhen shang de jumin gufu zhenzhu de enhui, suoyi zhenzhuyin tamen de xingwei er shi tamen changshi jidu de jihuang he kongbu.
16|113|Tamen zu zhong de yige shizhe que yi lailin tamen, dan tamen fourenle ta. Zai tamen bu yi de qingkuang xia, xingfa xijile tamen.
16|114|Nimen keyi chi zhenzhu shangci nimen de hefa er jiamei de shiwu, nimen yingdang ganxie zhenzhu de enhui, ruguo nimen zhi chongbai ta.
16|115|Ta zhi jinzhi nimen chi zi si wu, xieye, zhurou, yiji song fei zhenzhu zhi ming er tuzai zhe. Dan wei shi suo po, fei chu ziyuan, qie buguo fen zhe, namo, zhenzhu que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
16|116|Nimen duiyu ziji suo xushu de shi, buyao wangyan: Zhe shi hefa de, na shi weifa de. Yizhi nimen jiajie zhenzhu de mingyi er zaoyao. Jiajie zhenzhu de mingyi er zaoyao zhe bi bu chenggong.
16|117|(Tamen zhide) dao yidian xiangshou, er tamen jiang shou tongku de xingfa.
16|118|Dui youtai jiaotu, wo ceng jin jie wo congqian suo gaosuguo ni di naxie shiwu, wo meiyou kui wang tamen, dan tamen kui wangle ziji.
16|119|Ranhou, ni de zhu duiyu wuzhi er zuo'e, yihou you huiguo zi xin de ren, que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
16|120|Yi bo la xin yuanlai shi yige biaoshuai, ta fucong zhenzhu, xinfeng zhengjiao, erqie bushi yi wu pei zhu de.
16|121|Ta yuan shi ganxie zhu en de, zhu tiaoxuanle ta, bing jiang ta yin shangle zhenglu.
16|122|Zai jinshi, wo ceng yi xingfu shangci ta, zai houshi, ta biding juyu shanren zhi lie.
16|123|Ranhou, wo qishi ni shuo: Ni yingdang zunshou xinfeng zhengjiao de yi bo la xin de zongjiao, ta bushi yi wu pei zhu de.
16|124|Anxiri shi naxie wei zhi er zhenglun de ren suo yingdang zunshou de dingzhi. Fuhuo ri, ni de zhu bi panjue tamen suo zhenglun de shifei.
16|125|Ni ying ping zhihui heshan yan er quan ren zunxun zhu dao, ni yingdang yi zui youxiu de taidu yu ren bianlun, ni de zhu dique zhidao shei shi beili ta de zhengdao de, ta dique zhidao shei shi zunxun ta de zhengdao de.
16|126|Ruguo nimen yao baofu, jiu yingdang yizhao nimen suo shou de shanghai er baofu. Ruguo nimen rongren, na duiyu rongren zhe shi geng hao de.
16|127|Ni yingdang rongren--ni de rongren zhi lai zhenzhu de youzhu--ni buyao wei tamen er beishang, buyao wei tamen de jimou er fannao.
16|128|Zhen zhu que shi tong jingwei zhe he xingshan zhe zai yiqi de.
17|1|Zanmei zhen zhu, chaojue wanwu, ta zai yiye zhi jian, shi ta de puren, cong jin si xing dao yuan si. Wo zai yuan si de sizhou jiang fu, yibian wo zhaoshi ta wo de yibufen jixiang. Zhen zhu que shi quan cong de, que shi quan ming de.
17|2|Wo ba jingdian shangci mu sa, bingyong zuo yiselie de zisun de xiangdao. Wo shuo: Nimen buyao she wo er caiqu renhe jianhu zhe!
17|3|Wo ceng shi qi yu nu ha tongzhougongji zhe de zisun a! Ta yuan shi yige gan'en de puren.
17|4|Wo ceng zai jingdian li qishi dui yiselie de houyi panjue shuo: Nimen biding yao zai da dishang liang ci zuoluan, nimen biding hen aoman.
17|5|Dang di yici zuoluan de yue qi lailin de shihou, wo paiqian wo de xuduo qiangda de puren qu chengzhi nimen, tamen jiu sousuole zhuzhai, na shi yao luxing de nuoyan.
17|6|Ranhou, wo wei nimen huifule dui tamen de youshi, wo yi caifu he zisun zizhu nimen, wo shi nimen gengjia fushu.
17|7|Wo shuo: Ruguo nimen xingshan, namo, nimen shi wei ziji er xingshan, ruguo nimen zuo'e, namo, nimen shi wei ziji er zuo'e. Dang di 2 ci zuoluan de yue qi lailin de shihou,(wo you paiqian tamen), yibian tamen shi nimen bian cheng wei choumeikulian de, yibian tamen xiang tou yi ci nayang zai ru jin si, yibian tamen ba ziji suo zhanling di difang jiayi cuihui.
17|8|(Ruguo nimen huigai), nimen de zhu huoxu hui lianmin nimen. Ruguo nimen chongxin weikang wo, wo jiang chongxin chengzhi nimen. Wo yi huo yu wei buxindao zhe de jianyu.
17|9|Zhe bu “gulanjing” bi yindao ren yu zhi zhengzhidao, bing yugao xingshan de xinshi, tamen jiangyao xiangshou zuida de baochou.
17|10|(Hai yugao) bu xin houshi zhe, wo yi wei tamen yubeile tongku de xingfa.
17|11|Ren qidao huohuan, xiang qidao xingfu yiyang, ren shi jizao de.
17|12|Wo yi zhouye wei liang zhong jixiang, wo mo diao heiye de jixiang, bing yi baizhou wei mingliang de, yibian nimen xunqiu cong nimen de zhu fachu de enhui, yibian nimen zhidao lifa he suanshu. Wo mingbai di jieshi yiqie shiwu.
17|13|Wo shi mei geren de xingwei fuzhuo zai ta de bozi shang. Zai fuhuo ri, wo yao wei mei geren quchu yige zhankai de benzi,
17|14|(shuo:) Ni du ni de benzi ba! Jintian, ni yi zu wei ziji de qingsuan ren.
17|15|Shei zunxun zhengdao, shei zi shou qi yi; shei wu ru mitu, shei zi shou qi hai. Yige fu zui zhe, bu fu taren de zui. Paiqian shizhe zhiqian, wo bu chengfa (renhe ren).
17|16|Dang wo yao huimie yige shi zhen de shihou, wo mingling qizhongguo anle shenghuo zhe fucong wo, dan tamen fangdang bu jian, suoyi ying shou xingfa de panjue. Yushi wo huimie tamen.
17|17|Zai nu ha zhihou, wo hui mie liao ruogan shidai. Ni de zhu duiyu qi puren de zuixing, zu wei che zhi zhe he mingcha zhe.
17|18|Fan yu huode xianshi shenghuo zhe, wo jiang zai xianshi yi wo suo yiyu de baoda tamen zhong wo suo yiyu zhe. Ranhou, wo jiang yi huo yu chengzhi tamen, tamen jiang shou zebei, zao qi juedi jinru huo yu.
17|19|Fan yu huode houshi, bing wei ci er jinle nuli de xindao zhe, zhe deng ren de nuli shi you baochou de.
17|20|Zhe deng ren he na deng ren, wo du yao yi ni de zhu de shangci zizhu tamen, ni de zhu de shangci, bushi shou zu'ai de.
17|21|Ni kan wo zenyang shi tamen zhong de yibufen ren chaoyue ling yibufen ren; houshi que shi pinji geng gao, youyue geng shen de.
17|22|Ni buyao shi renhe wu yu zhenzhu tong shou chongbai, yimian ni bian cheng shou zebei, zao yiqi de.
17|23|Ni de zhu ceng xialing shuo: Nimen yingdang zhi chongbai ta, yingdang xiaojing fumu. Ruguo ta lia zhong de yiren huozhe liang ren zai ni de tangshang dadao laomai, namo, ni buyao dui ta lia shuo: Pei! Buyao he chi ta lia, ni yingdang dui ta lia shuo you limao dehua.
17|24|Ni yingdang bigongbijing de fushi ta lia, ni yingdang shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni lianmin ta lia, jiu xiang wo nian you shi ta lia yangyu wo nayang.
17|25|Nimen de zhu shi zui zhi dao nimen de xinqing de. Ruguo nimen shi shanliang de, namo, ta duiyu changchang huiguo zhe que shi zhi she de.
17|26|Ni yingdang ba qinqi, pinmin, luke suo ying de de zhouji fen gei tamen, ni buyao huihuo;
17|27|huihuo zhe que shi emo de pengyou, emo yuan shi gufu zhu en de.
17|28|Ruguo ni bixu qiu de ni suo xiwang de cong zhu jiang shi de enhui hou caineng zhouji tamen, namo, ni yinggai dui tamen shuo wenhe dehua.
17|29|Ni buyao ba ziji de shou shu zai bozi shang, ye buyao bashou wanquan shen kai, yimian ni bian cheng huihen de shou zebei zhe.
17|30|Ni de zhu bi wei tasuo yiyu zhe er shi jiyang fuyu, bi wei tasuo yiyu zhe er shi jiyang jiongpo. Ni de zhu duiyu ta de zhong pu, que shi che zhi de, que shi mingcha de.
17|31|Nimen buyao yinwei pa pinqiong er shahai ziji de ernu, wo gongji tamen he nimen. Shahai tamen que shi dazui.
17|32|Nimen buyao jiejin si tong, yinwei si tong que shi xialiu de shi, zhe xingjing zhen elie!
17|33|Nimen buyao weibei zhenzhu de jinling er sharen, chufei yinwei zhengyi. Wugu'er bei sha zhe, wo yi ba quanbing shouyu ta de qinqi, dan tamen buke lan sha, tamen que shi shou yuanzhu de.
17|34|Nimen buyao jiejin gu er de caichan, chufei yizhao zui youliang de fangshi, zhidao ta chengnian. Nimen yingdang luxing nuoyan; nuoyan que shi yao bei shenwen de shi.
17|35|Dang nimen mai liang de shihou, yingdang liang zu fenliang, nimen yingdang shiyong gongping de cheng cheng huowu, zhe shi shanshi, shi jieju zui you de.
17|36|Ni buyao suicong ni suo bu zhidao de yanxing, ermu he xinling dou shi yao bei shenwen de.
17|37|Ni buyao jiao'ao ziman di zai dadishang xingzou, ni jue buneng ba dadi ta chuan, jue buneng yu shan bi gao.
17|38|Zhexie shi, qi elie shi ni de zhu suo yanwu de.
17|39|Zhe shi ni de zhu suo qishi ni de zhihui, ni buyao shi renhe shenming yu zhenzhu tong shou chongbai, fouze, ni jiang zai shou zebei he zao qi jue de qingkuang xia bei touru huo yu.
17|40|Nandao nimen de zhu ba nan'er shangci nimen, er yi zhong tianshen wei ziji de nu'er ma? Nimen dique shuo chu huangmiu dehua.
17|41|Zai zhe bu “gulanjing” li, wo que yi fanfu shenshu zhege zongzhi, yibian tamen mingji. Zhe zhong shenshu zhi hui shi tamen gengjia zengwu.
17|42|Ni shuo: Jiaruo you xuduo shenming he ta zai yiqi, youru tamen suo shuo di nayang, namo, naxie shenling biding xiangfangshefa yu baozuo de zhu zheng heng.
17|43|Zansong zhenzhu, chaojue wanwu, ta jue ran chao hu tamen suo shuo de!
17|44|Qi ceng tian he da di, yiji wan you, dou zansong ta chaojue wanwu, wu yi wu bu zansong ta chaojue wanwu. Dan nimen bu liaojie tamen de zansong. Ta que shi rongren de, que shi zhi she de.
17|45|Dang nimen songdu “gulanjing” de shihou, wo zai nimen he buxin houshi zhe zhi jian anzhi yidao yin wei de pingzhang.
17|46|Wo zai tamen de xin shang jiale xuduo zhaozi, yimian tamen liaojie “gulanjing”; you zai tamen de er li zao zhong ting, dang ni zai “gulanjing” li zhi ti dao ni de zhu de shihou, tamen zengwu de li qu.
17|47|Wo zui zhidao tamen weihe yao qingting ni song jing, dangshi tamen lai qingting ni song jing, bingqie mimi de tanhua. Dangshi bu yi zhemen shuo: Nimen zhishi shuncong yige zhongle moshu de ren.
17|48|Ni kan tamen wei ni dale xuduo biyu, dan tamen suo shuo de dou bu zhongken, tamen buneng huode yitiao chulu.
17|49|Tamen shuo: Women bian cheng kugu he chentu hou, nandao women huan yiding hui bei fuhuo chengwei xinren ma?
17|50|Ni shuo: Jinguan nimen bian cheng shitou, huo tie kuai,
17|51|huo nimen renwei geng nanyu jieshou shengming de shenme dongxi. Tamen jiang shuo: Shei shi women fuhuo ne? Ni shuo: Chuci chuangzao nimen de zhu. Tamen jiang dui ni yaotou shuo: Zhe jian shi jiang zai he shi fachu ne? Ni shuo: Zhe jian shi huoxu shi linjinle.
17|52|Zai na shi, ta jiang zhaohuan nimen, er nimen jiang yi rongci daying ta. Nimen jiang caixiang ziji zai fenmu li zhi douliule yihui'er.
17|53|Ni gaosu wo de purenmen shuo: Jiao tamen shuo zhe ju zui youmei dehua--emo biding yao lijian tamen, emo que shi renlei de ming di
17|54|nimen de zhu shi zui zhidao nimen de, ta yao lianmin nimen jiu lianmin nimen; ta yao chengfa nimen jiu chengfa nimen. Wo mei paiqian ni zuo tamen de jianhu zhe.
17|55|Ni de zhu shi zhidao tiandi wanwu de. Wo que yi shi yibufen xianzhi chaoyue ling yibufen; wo ceng yi jingdian shangci da wu de.
17|56|Ni shuo: Nimen she zhenzhu er cheng wei shenming zhe, nimen qidao tamen ba! Tamen buneng ti nimen xiao zai, ye buneng ti nimen jia huo.
17|57|Tamen suo cheng wei shenming zhe, zishen qiu jin zhu zhi jie. Bi tamen geng jin yu zhu zhe ye qiu jin zhu zhi jie, tamen xiwang zhu de enhui, weiju zhu de xingfa. Ni de zhu de xingfa shi yinggai fangbei de.
17|58|Yiqie shi zhen, zai fuhuo ri zhiqian, wo du yao jiayi huimie, huo jiayi yanli de chengfa, zhe shi jilu zai tian jing li de.
17|59|Wo bu jiang shi jixiang, zhi wei qian ren bu chengren ta. Wo ceng yi mu tuo gei sai mo de ren zuo mingzheng, dan tamen pohai (huo nuedai) ta. Wo jiang jixiang zhishi weile donghe.
17|60|Dangshi wo ceng dui ni shuo: Ni de zhu shi zhouzhi zhongren de. Wo suo zhaoshi ni de meng zhao he zai “gulanjing” li bei zuzhou di na ke shu, wo zhi yi zhe liang jian shiwu kaoyan zhongren, bing jiayi donghe, dan wo de donghe zhi shi tamen gengjia manheng.
17|61|Dangshi wo ceng dui zhong tianshen shuo: Nimen yingdang xiang a dan koutou. Tamen jiu xiang ta koutou, dan yi bo lie si chuwai. Ta shuo: Ni yong nitu zaocheng de, wo zen neng xiang ta koutou ne!
17|62|Ta shuo: Ni gaosu wo ba, zhe jiushi ni shi ta chaoyue wo de ren ma? Ruguo ni kuanxian wo dao fuhuo ri, wo shi bi genjue ta de houyi, dan shaoshu ren chuwai.
17|63|Zhenzhu shuo: Ni qu ba! Tamen zhong fan shuncong ni de, huo yu biding shi tamen he ni de chongfen de baochou.
17|64|Ni keyi yong ni de shengyin qu donghe tamen zhong ni suo neng donghe de ren; ni keyi tongshuai ni de qibing he bubing, qu fandui tamen; ni keyi he tamen tong xiang tamen de caichan he ernu; ni keyi xu gei tamen renhe dongxi--emo zhi xu gei tamen wangxiang
17|65|wo de pu ren, ni dui tamen meiyou renhe quanbing, ni de zhu zu wei jianhu zhe.
17|66|Nimen de zhu wei nimen er shi chuanzhi zai haishang hangxing, yibian nimen xunqiu ta de enhui. Ta dui nimen que shi zhi ci de.
17|67|Dang nimen zai haishang zaoshou zaihai de shihou, nimen xianglai ting qidao de yi huibi nimenle, er nimen zhiyou qidao zhule. Dangzhu shi nimen ping'an denglu de shihou, nimen beipanle zhu. Ren yuan shi gu en de.
17|68|Nandao nimen bupa zhu shi nimen lunxian dixia, huo shi feishazoushi de kuangfeng saodang nimen, er nimen buneng wei ziji zhaodao renhe jianhu zhe ma?
17|69|Nandao nimen bupa zhu shi nimen zai qu hanghai, er shi kuangfeng xiji nimen, shi nimen yin gu en er chenni, ranhou, nimen buneng wei ziji zhaodao renhe dui zhu baochou zhe ma?
17|70|Wo que yi youdai a dan de houyi, er shi tamen zai lu shang huo haishang du you suo qi cheng, wo yi jiamei de shiwu gongji tamen, wo shi tamen dada di chaoguo wo suo chuangzao de xuduo ren.
17|71|(Ni ji zhu,) zai na ri, wo jiang zhaohuan mei ge minzu ji qi biaoshuai. Yi youshou jieshou qi gongguo bu zhe, jiang yuedu ziji de benzi; tamen bu shou yi sihao kui she.
17|72|Zai jinshi shi mangren zhe, zai houshi reng shi mangren, erqie gengjia mi wu.
17|73|Tamen que yi shi ni jihu weibei wo suo qishi de jiaoxun, yibian ni jiajie wo de mingyi, er niezao qita de jiaoxun. Name tamen jiu hui ba ni dang pengyou.
17|74|Yao bushi wo shi ni jianding, ni jihu yi qingxiang yu tamenle.
17|75|Ruguo nayang, wo bi shi ni zai shengqian changshi jiabei de xingfa, zai si hou changshi jiabei de xingfa, shi ni buneng zhaodao renhe ren bangzhu ni lai duikang wo.
17|76|Tamen que yi shi ni jihu buneng anju guxiang, yibian ba ni zhu chu jingwai. Ruguo nayang, tamen zai ni bei zhu zhihou, zhide douliu yihui'er.
17|77|Zhe shi zai ni zhiqian wo suo paiqian de zhong shizhe de changdao, ni duiyu wo de changdao buneng faxian renhe biangeng.
17|78|Ni yingdang jin shou cong chen shi dao heiye de bai gong; bing yingdang jin shou zaochen de bai gong, zaochen de bai gong que shi bei canjia de.
17|79|Zai yeli de yiduan shijian, ni yingdang jin shou ni suo dang shou de fujia de bai gong, zhu huoxu ba ni ti dao yige zhide chengsong di diwei.
17|80|Ni shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni shi wo shunli er ru, qiu ni shi wo shunli er chu, qiu ni shangci wo cong ni nali fachu de quanbing, yi zuo wo de fubi.
17|81|Ni shuo: Zhenli yi lailinliao, xuwang yi xiaomiele; xuwang que shi yi mie de.
17|82|Wo jiang shi keyi wei xinshimen zhiliao he gei tamen yi enhui de “gulanjing”, ta zhi hui shi bu xindao zhe gengjia kui she.
17|83|Dang wo shi en yu ren de shihou, ta diaotou bugu; dang ta zaoyu huohuan de shihou, ta bian cheng juewang de.
17|84|Ni shuo: Ge ren yi ziji de fangfa er gongzuo, nimen de zhu zui zhidao shei shi geng jin yu zhengdao de.
17|85|Tamen wen ni jingshen shi shenme? Ni shuo: Jingshen shi wo de zhu de jimi. Nimen zhi huode hen shao de zhishi.
17|86|Ruguo wo yiyu, wo shi bi ba wo qishi ni de (“gulanjing”) xiaomie jingjin, ranhou, ni dui wo buneng faxian renhe jianhu zhe.
17|87|Dan wo wei cong ni de zhu fachu de enhui (cai baocun ta), ni de zhu suo shi yu ni de enhui shi zhongda de.
17|88|Ni shuo: Ruguo renlei he jingling lianhe qilai chuangzao yi bu xiang zheyang de “gulanjing”, namo, tamen jishi huxiang bangzhu, ye bi buneng chuangzao xiang zheyang de miao wen.
17|89|Zai zhe bu “gulanjing” li, wo wei zhongren que yi shenshu ge zhong biyu, dan zhongren daban buxin.
17|90|Tamen shuo: Women jue buxin ni, zhidao ni wei women er shi yidao yuanquan cong dixia yong chu,
17|91|huozhe ni youyizuo yuanpu, zhongzhizhe ye zao he pu tao, ni shi heliu guanchuan qijian;
17|92|huozhe ni shi tian ru ni suo shuo di nayang, yikuai kuai di luo zai women de tou shang; huozhe ni qing zhenzhu he zhong tianshen lai (yu women) jianmian;
17|93|huozhe ni you yi suo huangjin wu; huozhe ni sheng shangtian qu, women jue buxin ni que yi shengtian, zhidao ni jiang shi women suo neng yuedu de jingdian. Ni shuo: Zansong wo de zhu chaojue wanwu! Wo zhishi yige ceng feng shiming de fanren.
17|94|Dang zhengdao jianglin zhongren de shihou, fang'ai tamen xindao de zhishi tamen de zhe ju hua: Nandao zhenzhu paiqian yige fanren lai zuo shizhe ma?
17|95|Ni shuo: Jiaruo da dishang you xuduo tianshen anran buxing, namo wo bi cong tianshang jiangxia yige tianshen qu tamen nali zuo shizhe.
17|96|Ni shuo: Zhenzhu zu wei wo yu nimen zhi jian de jianzheng, ta duiyu ta de pu renmen que shi che zhi de, que shi mingcha de.
17|97|Zhenzhu yindao shei, shei jiushi zunxun zhengdao de; zhenzhu shi shei mi wu, ni buneng wei shei faxian zhenzhu yiwai de baohu zhe. Zai fuhuo ri, wo jiang shi tamen you xia you ya you long de pufuzhe jihe qilai, tamen de guisu shi huo yu. Mei dang huoshi jianruo de shihou, wo zengjia tamen de huoyan.
17|98|Zhe shi tamen de baochou, yinwei tamen buxin wo de jixiang, bingqie shuo: Women bian cheng kugu he chentu hou, nandao women yiding hui bei fuhuo cheng xinren ma?
17|99|Nandao tamen bu zhidao ma? Chuangzaole tiandi wanwu de zhenzhu neng chuangzao xiang tamen nayang de ren, bing neng wei tamen queding yige hao wu keyi de qixian, bu yi de renmen zhi yuan buxin.
17|100|Ni shuo: Jiaruo wo de zhu de enhui de kucang gui nimen guanli, namo, nimen biding yinwei pa kaizhi er kouliu ta de enhui. Ren shi linse de.
17|101|Dang mu sa lailin yiselie ren de shihou, wo que yi shangci mu sa jiu zhong mingxian de jixiang. Ni wen yi wen yiselie ren ba, falao dui ta shuo: Mu sa a! Wo dique caixiang ni shi zhongle moshu de ren.
17|102|Ta shuo: Ni queshi zhidao, zhiyou tiandi de zhu neng jiang shi zhexie zuowei mingzheng. Falao a! Wo dique caixiang ni shi yao huimie de.
17|103|Ta yao ba tamen zhu chu jingwai, dan wo shi ta he ta de jundui tongtong yan si.
17|104|Zai ta miewang zhihou, wo dui yiselie ren shuo: Nimen juzhu zhege difang ba! Dang houshi de yue qi lailin de shihou, wo yao ba nimen zada de zhaoji lai.
17|105|Wo zhi ben zhenli er jiang shi “gulanjing”, er “gulanjing” ye zhi han zhenli er jiangxia. Wo zhi paiqian ni zuo baoxi xinzhe he jinggao zhe.
17|106|Zhe shi yi bu “gulanjing”, wo shi ta yiyi mingbai, yibian ni congrongbupo di dui zhongren xuandu ta; wo zhujian de jiang shi ta.
17|107|Ni shuo: Nimen keyi xinyang ta, ye keyi buxinyang ta. Zai jiang shi ta zhiqian yi huode zhishi de renmen, dang ting dao renmen songdu ta de shihou, tamen fufu koutou.
17|108|Tamen shuo: Zansong women de zhu chaojue wanwu! Women de zhu de nuoyan biding yao bei luxing.
17|109|Tamen tongkuzhe fufu xiaqu,“gulanjing” shi tamen geng gongjing.(Ci chu koutou!)
17|110|(Ni shuo:) Nimen keyi cheng ta wei zhenzhu, ye keyi cheng ta wei zhiren zhu. Yinwei ta you xuduo ji youmei de ming hao, nimen wulun yong shenme ming hao chenghu ta,(dou shi hen hao de). Ni zai bai zhong buyao gao sheng langsong, ye buyao di sheng modu, ni yingdang xunqiu yitiao shizhong de daolu.
17|111|Ni shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Ta meiyou shouyang ernu, meiyou tong ta gongxiang guo quan de, meiyou wei mian beijian er she de fuzhu zhe. Ni yingdang zansong ta de zunda.
18|1|Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Ta yi duanzheng de jingdian jiang shi ta de puren, er wei zai qizhong zhizao renhe pian xie,
18|2|yibian ta jinggao shiren, zhenzhuyao jiangxia yanli de chengfa; bing yugao xingshan de xinshimen, tamen de shou youmei de baochou,
18|3|er yong ju qizhong;
18|4|qie jinggao wangyan zhenzhu shouyang ernu de ren.
18|5|Tamen he tamen de zuxian, duiyu zhe ju hua dou hao wu zhishi, tamen xinkoukaihe de shuo zhe ju huangmiu juelun dehua.
18|6|Ruguo tamen bu xin zhe xun ci, zai tamen beili zhihou, ni huoxu wei beishang er zisha.
18|7|Wo que yi shi dadishang de yiqie shiwu chengwei dadi de zhuangshi pin, yibian wo kaoyan shiren, kan shei de gongzuo shi zui youmei de.
18|8|Wo bi huimie da dishang de yiqie shiwu, er shi da di bian wei huangliang de.
18|9|Nandao ni yiwei yandong he beiwen de zhuren shi wo de jixiang zhong de yi jian qi shi ma?
18|10|Dangshi, you ji ge qingnian bi ju shandong zhong, tamen shuo: Women de zhu a! Qiu ni ba ni nali de enhui shangci women, qiu ni shi women de shiye wanquan duanzheng.
18|11|Wo jiu shi tamen zai shandong li ji nian buneng tingwen.
18|12|Houlai wo shi tamen suxing, yibian wo zhidao liang pai zhong de na yipai geng neng jisuan tamen suo tingliu de shijian.
18|13|Wo ba tamen de gushi, chengshi di gaosu ni, tamen shi ji ge qingnian, tamen xinyang tamen de zhu, er wo gei tamen zengjia zhengdao.
18|14|Wo ceng shi tamen de xin jianren. Dangshi, tamen zhan qilai shuo: Women de zhu, shi tiandi de zhu, women jue bu she ta er qidao renhe shenming, fouze, women biding shuo chu bu jin qingli dehua.
18|15|Women de zhexie tongzu, she ta er chongbai bie de xuduo shenming, tamen zenme buyong yige mingzheng lai zhengshi naxie shenming shi ying shou chongbai de ne? Jiajie zhenzhu de mingyi er zaoyao de ren, you shei bi tamen hai bu yi ne?
18|16|Dang nimen liqi tamen he tamen she zhenzhu er chongbai de shenming, ke bi ju shandong, nimen de zhujiang dui nimen guang shi enhui--wei nimen de shiye wei youli de.
18|17|Ni kan taiyang chulai de shihou, cong tamen de shandong de youbian xieshe guoqu; taiyang luoshan de shihou, cong ta de zuobian xieshe guoqu, er tamen jiu zai dong de kong chu. Zhe shi zhen zhu de yi zhong jixiang, zhen zhu yindao shei, shei zunxun zhengdao; zhen zhu shi shei mi wu, ni jue buneng wei shei faxian renhe pengyou zuowei yindao zhe.
18|18|Ni yiwei tamen shi juexing de, qishi tamen shi hanshui de, wo shi tamen zuoyou fanzhuan, tamen de gou shenzhe liang tiao tui wo zai dongkou. Ruguo ni kanjian tamen, ni bi xia de zhuan lian er tao, manhuai kongbu.
18|19|Wo ruci shi tamen juexing, yibian tamen huxiang xunwen, qizhong youyigeren shuo: Nimen douliule duojiu? Tamen shuo: Women douliule yitian, huo bu dao yitian. Tamen shuo: Nimen de zhu zui qingchu nimen douliu de shijian de. Nimen ziji pai yi ge ren, daizhe nimen de zhexie yinbi dao cheng li qu, kan kan shei jia de shipin zui qingjie, jiao ta maidian shipin lai gei nimen, yao jiao ta hen jinshen, buyao shi renhe ren zhidao nimen.
18|20|Cheng li de ren, ruguo nazhe nimen, jiang yong shitou da si nimen, huozhe qiangpo nimen xinfeng tamen de zongjiao, namo, nimen jiu yong bu hui chenggongle.
18|21|Wo zheyang shi bieren kuijian tamen, yibian tamen zhidao zhenzhu de nuoyan shi zhenshi de, fuhuo de shike shi hao wu keyi de. Dangshi, tamen wei ci shi er zhenglun, tamen shuo: Nimen zai tamen de 4 zhou xiuyi du weiqiang--tamen de zhu shi zui liaojie tamen de! Zhuchi shiwu de ren shuo: Women biding zai tamen de sizhou jianzhu yi suo libaisi.
18|22|Youren jiang shuo: Tamen shi san ge, di si ge shi tamen de gou. Youren jiang shuo: Tamen shi wu ge, di liu ge shi tamen de gou. Zhe shi youyu caice youxuan. Hai youren jiang shuo: Tamen shi qi ge, di ba ge shi tamen de gou. Ni shuo: Wo de zhu shi zui zhidao tamen de shumu di, ciwai, zhiyou shaoshu ren zhidao. Guanyu tamen de shiqing, zhi ke zuo biaomian de bianlun, guanyu tamen de shiqing, buyao qingjiao renhe ren.
18|23|Ni buyao wei mou shi er shuo: Mingtian wo yiding zuo na jian shi.
18|24|Chufei tongshi shuo: Ruguo zhenzhu yiyu. Ni ruguo wangle, jiu yingdang jiyi qi ni de zhu, bingqie shuo: Wo de zhu huoxu zhishi wo bi zhe geng qiejin de zhengdao.
18|25|Tamen zai shandong li douliule sanbai nian,(an yinli suan) tamen you jia jiu nian.
18|26|Zhenzhu shi zui zhidao tamen douliu de shijian de. Wei you ta zhidao tiandi de youxuan. Ta de shijue zhen ming! Ta de tingjue zhen cong! Chu zhenzhu wai, tamen jue wu yuanzhu zhe, zhenzhu bu rang renhe ren shen yu ta de panjue.
18|27|Ni yingdang xuandu ni de zhu suo qishi ni de jingdian, ta de yanci, jue bushi renhe ren suo neng biangeng de. Ni jue buneng faxian yige yinbi suo.
18|28|Zai zaochen he wan xi qidao ziji de zhu er qiu qi xiyue zhe, ni yingdang naixin di he tamen zai yiqi, buyao miaoshi tamen, er qiu jinshi shenghuo de fuhua. Wo shi mou xie ren de xin hushi wo de jiaoxun, er shuncong ziji de yuwang. Tamen de xingwei shi guofen de, zhe zhong ren nimen buyao shuncong tamen.
18|29|Ni shuo: Zhenli shi cong nimen de zhu jiang shi de, shei yuan xindao jiu rang ta xin ba, shei bu yuan xindao, jiu rang ta buxin ba. Wo yi wei bu yi de ren, yubeile liehuo, na liehuo de yanmu jiang longzhao tamen. Ruguo tamen (wei gan ke er) qiujiu, jiu yi yi zhong shui gong tamen jieke, na zhong shui xiang liqing nayang shaozhuo ren mian, na yinliao zhen zaogao! Na guisu zhen elie!
18|30|Xindao er xingshan zhe, wo bi bu shi tamen de shanxing tulao wu chou,
18|31|zhe deng ren de xiangshou changzhu de leyuan, tamen xia lin zhu he, tamen zai leyuan li, pei jin zhi de shouzhuo, chuan ling luo jinduan de lu pao, kao zai chuangshang. Na baochou, zhen youmei! Na guisu, zhen meihao!
18|32|Ni yi liang geren de qingkuang wei tamen da yige biyu. Wo wei qizhong de yige ren chuangzaole liang ge putao yuan, er wei yi ye zao lin, bingqie yi liang yuan zhi jian di difang wei gengdi.
18|33|Liang yuan dou chuchan guoshi, hao bu qianque, bing zai liang yuan zhi jian, kaizao yitiao he.
18|34|Ta fuyou caichan, gu yi jinkua de taidu, dui ta de pengyou shuo: Wo caichan bi ni duo, ren bi ni qiang.
18|35|Ta zifu de zou jin ziji de yuanpu, shuo: Wo xiang zhege yuanpu yong bu huangwu,
18|36|wo xiang fuhuo shike bu hui lailin. Jishi wo bei zhao gui zhu, wo ye neng faxian bi zhe yuanpu geng hao de guisu.
18|37|Ta de pengyou yi bianbo de taidu dui ta shuo: Ni buxin zaowuzhu ma? Ta chuangzao ni, xian yong nitu, ji yong jingye, ranhou shi ni bian cheng yige wanzheng de nanzi.
18|38|Danshi (wo shuo), zhenzhu shi wo de zhu, wo bu yi renhe wu pei wo de zhu.
18|39|Ni zou jin ni de yuanpu de shihou, ni zenme bu shuo:'Zhe jian shi shi zhenzhu yiyu de. Chu zhenzhu wai, wo jue wu nengli!'Ruguo ni renwei wo de caichan he housi dou buru ni,
18|40|namo, wo de zhu huoxu hui shangci wo bi ni de yuanpu geng hao de dongxi, er jiang pili yu ni de yuanpu, yizhi (ta) hua wei guangtutu de tudi;
18|41|huo yuan li de shui yidan ganhe, ni jiu buneng xunqiu.
18|42|Ta de caichan, quan zao huimie. Yuan li de putao jia daota zai dishang, ta wei tongxi jianshe yuanpu de feiyong er fanfu fanzhuan ta de liang zhang, ta shuo: Dan yuan wo meiyou ba renhe wu pei wo de zhu.
18|43|Chu zhenzhu wai, meiyou qunzhong yuanzhu ta, ta ye buneng zizhu.
18|44|Zai zheli, yuanzhu quan gui zhenshi de zhenzhu, ta shi shangfa yanming de.
18|45|Ni wei tamen da yige bifang: Jinshi de shenghuo, youru wo cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, zhiwu de yu, jiu pengbo shengzhang, ji'er lingluo, sui feng piaosan. Zhenzhu duiyu wanshi shi quanneng de.
18|46|Caichan he housi shi jinshi shenghuo de zhuangshi; chang cun de shangong, zai ni de zhu kan lai, shi baochou geng hao de, shi xiwang geng da de.
18|47|Zai na ri, wo jiang shi shanyue xiaoshi, ni kan dadi bian cheng guangtutu de. Wo jiang jihe tamen, er bu yilou renhe ren.
18|48|Tamen jiang fen lie chengxing di jieshou ni de zhu de jianyue. Nimen que yi lai jian wo, youru wo chuci chuangzao nimen de shihou yiyang. Buran, nimen ceng shuo wo jue bu wei nimen queding yige yue qi.
18|49|Gongguo bu jiang zhanxian chulai, suoyi ni jiang hui kan dao zui renmen weiju qizhong de jilu. Tamen shuo: Aya! Zhege gongguo bu zenme la, bulun xiao zui dazui, dou hao bu yilou, yiqie dou jiayi jilu. Tamen jiang faxian ziji suo zuo de shi dou yiyi jilu zai benzi shang. Ni de zhu bu kui wang renhe ren.
18|50|Dangshi wo dui zhong tianshen shuo: Nimen yingdang xiang a dan koutou. Tamen dou koule tou, dan yi bo lie si chuwai. Ta ben shi jingling, suoyi weibei ta de zhu de mingling. Ta he ta de zisun, shi nimen de choudi, nimen que she wo er yi tamen wei baohu zhe ma? Bu yi zhe de daoxingnishi zhen elie!
18|51|Wo meiyou shi tamen yanjian tiandi de chuangzao, ye meiyou shi tamen yanjian qi zishen de chuangzao, wo meiyou ba shi ren mi wu zhe dangzuo zhushou.
18|52|Zai na ri, zhenzhu jiang shuo: Nimen suo cheng wei wo de huoji de, nimen ba tamen zhaohuan lai ba. Tamen jiu zhaohuan naxie tongshi, dan tamen bu daying. Wo jiang shi tamen tongguiyujin.
18|53|Zuifanmen jiang kanjian huo yu, bi duo qizhong, wu chu taobi.
18|54|Zai zhe “gulanjing” li, wo que yi wei zhongren chanshule ge zhong biyu, ren shi zhengbian zuiduo de.
18|55|Dang zhengdao lailin zhongren de shihou, tamen bu xindao, ye bu xiang tamen de zhu qiurao, na zhishi yinwei tamen yao dengdai (zhenzhu jiang) guren de changdao xianxian yu tamen, huo yanjian xingfa lailin tamen.
18|56|Wo zhi paiqian shizhemen baoxi xin chuan jinggao, er bu xindao de renmen que yi wangyan xiang zhengbian, yu jie ci fanbo zhenli. Tamen ba wo de jixiang he dui tamen de jinggao, dangzuo xiaobing.
18|57|Youren yi zhu de jixiang jiaohui tamen, dan tamen biqi ta, bingqie wangji tamen yiqian suo fan de zui'e; you shei bi tamen hai bu yi ne? Wo que yi jiang bomo jia zai tamen de xin shang, yimian tamen liaojie jing yi, bingqie zai tamen de er li zao zhong ting. Ruguo ni zhao tamen yu zhengdao, namo, tamen jiang yong bu zunxun zhengdao.
18|58|Ni de zhu que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de. Jiaruo ta wei tamen suo fan de zui'e er chengzhi tamen, namo, ta bi wei tamen er cujin xingfa de lailin, dan tamen you ge dingqi, tamen dui nage dingqi, jue buneng huode yige binan suo.
18|59|Naxie shi zhen de jumin duo xing bu yi de shihou, wo huimie tamen, wo wei tamen de huimie er yuding yige qixian.
18|60|Dangshi, mu sa dui ta de tong pu shuo: Wo jiang bu ting bu, zhidao wo daoda liang hai xiangjiao chu, huo jixu luxing ruogan nian.
18|61|Dang ta lia daoda liang hai xiang jiaojie chu de shihou, wangjile ta lia de yu, na wei yu bian ruhai youran er qu.
18|62|Dang ta lia zou guoqu de shihou, ta dui ta de tong pu shuo: Na zaofan lai chi! Women queshi pijuanle.
18|63|Ta shuo: Ni gaosu wo ba, dang women daoda na zuo panshi xia xiuxi de shihou,(wo jiujing shi zenyang de ne?) Wo que yi wangjile na wei yu--zhi yin emo wo cai wangjile gaosu ni,--na wei yu yi ruhai er qu, na zhenshi guaishi!
18|64|Ta shuo: Zhe zheng shi women suo xunqiu de. Ta lia jiu yi lai shi de zuji zhuanshen huiqu.
18|65|Ta lia faxian wo de yige puren, wo yi ba cong wo zheli fachu de enhui shangci ta, wo yi ba cong wo zheli fachu de zhishi chuanshou ta.
18|66|Mu sa dui ta shuo: Wo yao zhuisui ni, xiwang ni ba ni suo xue de de zhengdao chuanshou wo. Hao ma?
18|67|Ta shuo: Ni buneng naixin di he wo zai yiqi.
18|68|Ni meiyou chedi renshi de shiqing ni zenme neng renshou ne?
18|69|Mu sa shuo: Ruguo zhenzhu yiyu, ni jiang faxian wo shi jianren de, bu hui weikang ni de renhe mingling.
18|70|Ta shuo: Ruguo ni zhuisui wo, namo,(yu shi) buyao wen wo shenme daoli, deng wo ziji jiang gei ni ting.
18|71|Ta lia jiu tongxing, daole cheng chuan de shihou, ta ba chuan zaole yige dong, mu sa shuo: Ni ba chuan zaole yige dong, yao xiang shi chuan li de ren yan si ma? Ni que yi zuole yi jian beimiu de shi!
18|72|Ta shuo: Wo meiyou dui ni shuoguo ma? Ni buneng naixin he wo zai yiqi.
18|73|Mu sa shuo: Gangcai wo wangle ni de zhufu, qing ni buyao zebei wo, buyao yi wo suo da nan de shi zebei wo!
18|74|Ta lia you tongxing, houlai yujianle yige er tong, ta jiu ba nage er tong shale, mu sa shuo: Ni zenme wang sha wugu de ren ne? Ni que yi zuole yi jian xiong'e de shile!
18|75|Ta shuo: Nandao wo meiyou dui ni shuoguo ma? Ni buneng naixin di he wo zai yiqi.
18|76|Mu sa shuo: Cihou, ruguo wo zai wen ni shenme daoli, ni jiu keyi buxu wo zai zhuisui ni, ni duiyu wo, zongsuan renzhiyijinle.
18|77|Ta lia you tongxing, lai daole yige chengshi, jiu xiang cheng li jumin qiu shi, tamen bu ken kuandai. Houlai ta lia zai cheng li faxian yi du qiang kuaiyao daotale, ta jiu ba na du qiang xiuli haole, mu sa shuo: Ruguo ni yiyu, ni bi wei zhe jian gongzuo er suoqu gongqian.
18|78|Ta shuo: Wo he ni congci zuobiele. Ni suo buneng renshou di naxie shi, wo jiang gaosu ni qizhong de daoli.
18|79|Zhiyu na zhi chuan, ze shi zai haili gongzuo de ji ge qiongren de, wo yao shi chuan you quexian, shi yinwei tamen de qianmian you yige guowang, yaoqiang zheng yiqie chuanzhi.
18|80|Zhiyu nage er tong, ze ta de fumu dou shi xindao zhe, women pa ta yi beini he buxin qiangjia yu ta de fumu,
18|81|suoyi women yao ta lia de zhu ling shangci ta lia yige geng chunjie, geng xiaojing de erzi.
18|82|Zhiyu na du qiang, ze shi chengzhong liang ge gu'er de; qiang xia you ta lia de caibao. Ta lia de fuqin, yuan shi shanliang de. Ni de zhuyao ta lia chengnian hou, quchu ta lia de caibao, zhe shi shuyu ni de zhu de enhui, wo meiyou suizhe wo de si yi zuo zhe jian shi. Zhe shi ni suo buneng renshou de shiqing de daoli.
18|83|Tamen xunwen zuo lei gai er naiying de gushi, ni shuo: Wo jiang dui nimen xushu youguan ta de yige baogao.
18|84|Wo que yi shi ta zai da dishang deshi, wo shangci ta chuli wanshi de tujing.
18|85|Ta jiu zunxun yitiao tujing,
18|86|zhidao ta daodale riluo zhi chu, ta juede taiyang shi luo zai hei ni yuan zhong, ta zai na hei ni yuan pang faxian yi zhong ren. Wo shuo: Zuo lei gai er naiying a! Ni huo chengzhi tamen, huo shandai tamen.
18|87|Ta shuo: Zhiyu bu yi zhe, wo jiang chengfa ta, ranhou ta de zhuzai jiang ba ta zhao qu, jiayi yanli chengchu.
18|88|Zhiyu xindao erqie xingshan zhe, jiang xiangshou zui youhou de baochou, wo jiang mingling ta zuo jianyi de shiqing.
18|89|Suihou ta you zunxun yitiao lu,
18|90|yizhi zou dao ri chu zhi chu, ta faxian taiyang zheng shaizhe yi zhong ren, wo meiyou gei tamen fang ri shai de gongju.
18|91|Shishi jiu xiang shuo di nayang. Wo yi che zhi ta yongyou de yiqie.
18|92|Suihou, ta you zunxun yitiao lu,
