18|93|yizhi dao ta daodale liang shan zhi jian de shihou, ta faxian qianmian youyi zhong ren, jihu bu dong (ta de) hua.
18|94|Tamen shuo: Zuo lei gai er naiying a! Ya zhu zhe he ma zhu zhe, dique zai difang daoluan, women xiang ni jingong, wu qing ni zai women he tamen zhi jian jianzhu yizuo bilei, hao ma?
18|95|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu shi wo nenggou xiangshou de, youwei youmei. Nimen yi renli fuzhu wo, wo jiu zai nimen he tamen zhi jian jianzhu yizuo bilei.
18|96|Nimen na tie kuai lai gei wo ba. Daole ta dui man liang shan zhi jian de shihou, ta shuo: Nimen la fengxiang ba. Daole ta shi tie kuai hong ru huoyan de shihou, ta shuo: Nimen na rong tong lai gei wo, wo jiu ba ta qingzhu zai bilei shang.
18|97|Tamen jiu buneng pandeng, ye buneng zao kong.
18|98|Ta shuo: Zhe shi cong wo de zhu jiangxia de enhui, dang wo de zhu de yingxu jianglin de shihou, ta jiang shi zhe bilei hua wei pingdi. Wo de zhu de yingxu shi zhenshi de.
18|99|Na ri, wo jiang shi tamen zhixu wenluan. Haojiao yi xiang, wo jiu ba tamen wanquan jihe qilai.
18|100|Zai na ri, wo yao ba huo yu chenlie zai buxindao zhe de mianqian.
18|101|Tamen de yan zai yi zi zhong, buneng kan dao wo de jiaohui, tamen buneng tingcong.
18|102|Nandao buxindao zhe, renwei keyi she wo er yi wo de zhong pu wei baohu zhe ma? Wo que yi yubei huo yu wei bu xindao zhe de zhaodaisuo.
18|103|Ni shuo: Wo gaosu nimen zai hang wei fangmian zui chikui de ren, hao ma?
18|104|Tamen jiushi zai jinshi shenghuo zhong tulaowugong, er renwei ziji shi shoufa qiaomiao de ren.
18|105|Zhe deng ren bu xin tamen de zhu de jixiang, ye bu xin jiang yu ta xiang hui, suoyi tamen zai jinshi shenghuo zhong de shangong bian wei wuxiao de, fuhuo ri wo bu wei tamen shuli quanheng.
18|106|Tamen de baochou shi huo yu, yinwei tamen bu xindao, bingqie ba wo de jixiang he shizhe dangzuo xiaobing.
18|107|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, deyi leyuan wei zhaodaisuo,
18|108|bing yong ju qizhong, bu yuan qian chu.
18|109|Ni shuo: Jiaruo yi haishui wei mozhi, yong lai jizai wo de zhu de yanci, namo, haishui biding yong jin, er wo de zhu de yanci shangwei qiongjin, jishi women yi tong liang di haishui buchong zhi.
18|110|Ni shuo: Wo zhishi yige tong nimen yiyang de fanren, wo feng de qishi shi: Nimen suo yingdang chongbai de, zhishi yige zhuzai, gu shei xiwang yu ta de zhu xiang hui, jiu jiao shei li xingshan gong, jiao shei buyao yi renhe wu yu ta de zhu shou tongyang de chongbai.
19|1|Ka fu, ha, ya, a yin, sa de.
19|2|Zhe shi xushu ni de zhu duiyu ta de puren zai kai li ya de enhui.
19|3|Dangshi, ta di sheng di huyu ta de zhu shuo:
19|4|Wo de zhu a! Wo de guge yi ruanruole, wo yi bai fa cangcangle, wo de zhu a! Wo meiyou wei qidao ni er shiwang.
19|5|Wo dique danxin wo si hou tang xiongdimen buneng jicheng wo de zhiwei, wo de qizi you shi bu hui shengyu de, qiu ni shangci wo yige er zi,
19|6|lai jicheng wo, bing jicheng ye er gu bai de bufen houyi. Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni shi ta chengwei kexi de.
19|7|Zai kai li ya a! Wo biding yi yige er zi xiang ni baoxi, ta de mingzi shi ye ha ya, wo yiqian meiyou shi renhe ren yu ta tongming.
19|8|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Wo de qizi shi bu hui shengyu de, wo ye laotailongzhongle, wo zenme hui you erzi ni?
19|9|Zhu shuo: Shiqing jiushi zheyang. Ni de zhu shuo: Zhe duiyu wo shi rongyi de. Yiqian ni bu cunzai, er wo chuangzaole ni.
19|10|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni wei wo yuding yi zhong jixiang. Ta shuo: Ni de jixiang shi ni wu ji wu bing, dan san ri san ye ni buneng he ren shuohua.
19|11|Ta cong sheng suo li zou chulai jian ta de zuren, jiu anshi tamen: Nimen yingdang zhaoxi zansong zhenzhu.
19|12|Ye ha ya a! Ni yingdang jianchi jingdian. Ta zai tongnian shidai wo yi shangci ta zhihui,
19|13|yu cong wo fachu de enhui he chunjie. Ta shi jingwei de,
19|14|shi xiaojing ni de, bushi badao de, bushi wuni de.
19|15|Ta zai chusheng ri, siwang ri, fuhuo ri dou xiangshou heping.
19|16|Ni yingdang zai zhe bu jingdian li ti ji mai er yan, dangri ta likaile jiashu er dao dongbian yige difang.
19|17|Ta yong yige weimu zhebizhe, bu rang renmen kanjian ta. Wo shi wo de jingshen dao ta mianqian, ta jiu dui ta xianxian cheng yige shencai yunchen de ren.
19|18|Ta shuo: Wo dique qiu bi yu zhiren zhu, mian zao ni de qinfan, ruguo ni shi jingwei de.
19|19|Ta shuo: Wo zhishi ni de zhu de shizhe, wo lai gei ni yige chunjie de erzi.
19|20|Ta shuo: Renhe ren meiyou jiechuguo wo, wo you bushi shijie de, wo zenme hui you erzi ni?
19|21|Ta shuo: Shishi shi xiang zheyang de, ni de zhu shuo: Zhe duiyu wo shi rongyi de. Wo yao yi ta wei shiren de jixiang, wei cong wo fachu de enhui, zhe shi yijing panjue de shiqing.
19|22|Ta jiu huaile yun, yushi ta tuibi dao yige pi yuan di difang.
19|23|Zhentong poshi ta lai dao yi ke ye zao shu pang, ta shuo: A! Dan yuan wo yiqian sile, erqie yi bian cheng bei ren yiwang de dongxi.
19|24|Ye zao shu xia you shengyin hanjiao ta shuo: Ni buyao youchou, ni de zhu yi zai ni de xiamian zaohuale yitiao xishui.
19|25|Ni xiangzhe ni de fangxiang yaohan ye zao shu, jiu you xinxian de, chengshu de ye zao fenfen luo zai ni de mianqian.
19|26|Ni chi ba, ni he ba, ni yukuai ba! Ruguo ni jian ren lai, ni keyi shuo:'Wo que yi xiang zhiren zhu fayuan zhaijie, suoyi jintian wo jue budui renhe ren shuohua'.
19|27|Ta baozhe ying'er lai jian ta de zuren, tamen shuo: Mai er yan a! Ni que yi zuole yi jian qi shi.
19|28|Ha lun de meimei a! Ni fuqin bushi quede de, ni muqin bushi shijie de.
19|29|Ta jiu zhi yi zhi nage ying'er, tamen shuo: Women zen neng dui yaolan li de ying'er shuohua ne?
19|30|Na ying'er shuo: Wo que shi zhenzhu de puren, ta yao ba jingdian shangci wo, yao shi wo zuo xianzhi,
19|31|yao shi wo wulun zai nali dou shi youfu de, bingqie zhufu wo, zhiyao huozhe jiu yao jin shou bai gong, wan na tian ke,
19|32|(ta shi wo) xiaojing wo de muqin, ta meiyou shi wo zuo badao de, boming de ren.
19|33|Wo zai chusheng ri, siwang ri, fuhuo ri, dou xiangshou heping.
19|34|Zhe shi mai er yan de erzi er sa, zhe shi nimen suo zhenglun de zhenli zhi yan.
19|35|Zhenzhu bu hui shouyang erzi--zansong zhenzhu, chaojue wanwu--dang ta panjue yi jian shi de shihou, ta zhi dui na jian shi shuo: You', ta jiu youle.
19|36|Zhenzhu que shi wo de zhu, ye que shi nimen de zhu, suoyi nimen yingdang chongbai ta. Zhe shi zhenglu.
19|37|Dan ge pai zhi jian yijian fenqi. Zhongda ri lailin de shihou, bei'ai guiyu buxindao zhe.
19|38|Tamen lai jian wo di na ri, tamen de er zhen cong, tamen de yan zhen ming, dan bu yi zhe, jintian que zai mingxian de mi wu zhi zhong.
19|39|Ni yingdang jinggao tamen huihen zhi ri, dangri yiqie shiqing yi bei panjue, er tamen xianzai hai zai shuhu zhi zhong. Tamen bu xin zhengdao.
19|40|Wo biding jicheng dadi he da dishang suoyou de yiqie, tamen jiang guiyu wo.
19|41|Ni yingdang zai zhe bu jingdian li ti ji yi bo la xin, ta yuan shi yige qiancheng de ren, you shi yige xianzhi.
19|42|Dangshi ta dui ta fuqin shuo: Wo de fuqin a! Ni weihe chongbai na ji buneng ting, you buneng jian, duiyu ni you meiyou renhe biyi de dongxi ne?
19|43|Wo de fuqin a! Meiyou jianglin ni de zhishi, que yi jianglin wole; ni shuncong wo ba, wo yao zhishi ni yitiao zhenglu.
19|44|Wo de fuqin a! Ni buyao chongbai emo, emo que shi weikang zhiren zhu de.
19|45|Wo de fuqin a! Wo dique pa ni zaoshou cong zhiren zhu fachu de xingfa, er bian cheng emo de pengyou.
19|46|Ta shuo: Ni yanwu wo de zhuzai ma? Yi bo la xin a! Ruguo ni bu tingzhi, wo shi bi ruma ni. Ni yingdang yuanli wo ge chang shiqi.
19|47|Ta shuo: Zhu ni ping'an! Wo jiang wei ni xiang wo de zhu qiurao, ta dui wo que shi renci de.
19|48|Wo jiang tuibi nimen, yiji nimen she zhenzhu er qidao de. Wo jiang qidao wo de zhu, wo huoxu bu wei qidao wo de zhu er bian wei boming de ren.
19|49|Ta ji tuibi tamen, yiji tamen she zhenzhu er qidao de, wo jiu shangci ta yi si ha ge he ye er gu bai, wo shi ta lia chengwei xianzhi,
19|50|wo ba wo de enhui shangci tamen, wo shi tamen heng you zhenshi de, chonggao de shengwang.
19|51|Ni yingdang zai zhe bu jingdian li ti ji mu sa, ta que shi chunjie de, que shi shizhe, que shi xianzhi.
19|52|Wo cong na zuo shan de youbian zhaohuan ta, wo jiao ta dao wo zheli lai mitan.
19|53|Wo weile ci'ai er ba ta gege xianzhi ha lun gei ta zuo zhushou.
19|54|Ni yingdang zai zhe bu jingdian li ti ji yi sima yi, ta que shi zhong ran nuo de, ta shi shizhe, you shi xianzhi.
19|55|Ta yi bai gong he tian ke mingling ta de jiashu, ta zai ta de zhu nali shi kexi de.
19|56|Ni yingdang zai zhe bu jingdian li ti ji yi de li si, ta shi yige laoshi ren, you shi yige xianzhi,
19|57|wo ba ta tigao dao yige chonggao di diwei.
19|58|Zhenzhu ceng jiayi en chong de zhexie xianzhi, shuyu a dan de houyi, shuyu wo shi (tamen) yu nu ha tongzhougongji zhe de (houyi), shuyu yi bo la xin he yi si la yi de houyi, shuyu wo suoyindao erqie xuanba de ren, dui tamen xuandu zhiren zhu de qishi de shihou, tamen fufu xiaqu koutou he kuqi.(Ci chu koutou!)※
19|59|Zai tamen qushi zhihou, you buxiao de houyi jicheng tamen, naxie houyi feiqi bai gong, shuncong shiyu, tamen jiang yu mi wu de guobao.
19|60|Dan huizui er xindao, qie xingshan zhe chuwai, tamen jiang ru leyuan, bu shou sihao kuidai.
19|61|Na shi changzhu de leyuan, zhiren zhu zai youxuan zhong yingxu qi zhong pu de, ta de nuoyan que shi yao luxing de.
19|62|Tamen zai nalimian, ting bu dao xiantan, zhi ting dao zhuyuan ping'an; tamen zai nalimian, zhaoxi huode jiyang.
19|63|Jiushi wo jiang shi zhong pu zhong de jingwei zhe jicheng de leyuan.
19|64|Women wei feng ni de zhu de mingling er suishi jianglin, zai women mianqian de, zai women houmian de, yiji zai women qianhou zhi jian de (shiqing), ta dou zhidao. Ni de zhu shi bu wangji de.
19|65|Ta shi tiandi wanwu de zhu, ni yingdang chongbai ta, ni yingdang naixin, ni zhidao ta you pidi ma?
19|66|Ren shuo: Wo si hou biyao fuhuo ma?
19|67|Ren wangjile ma? Ta yiqian bushi shi you de, er wo chuangzaole ta.
19|68|Zhi ni de zhu fashi, wo bi jiang tamen he zhong emo jihe qilai. Ranhou wo bi shi tamen qu gui zai huo yu de zhouwei.
19|69|Ranhou wo bi cong mei yi zongpai zhong tichu dui zhiren zhu zui beini de ren.
19|70|Ranhou, wo dique zhidao shei shi zui gai shou huoxing de.
19|71|Nimen zhong meiyou yige ren bu dao huo yu de, na shi ni de zhu jueding yao shixing de.
19|72|Ranhou, wo jiang zhengjiu jingwei zhe, er rang bu yi zhe gui zai na limian.
19|73|Dui tamen xuandu wo de mingxian de jixiang de shihou, buxindao zhe dui xindao zhe shuo: Na yipai di diwei geng youyue, huichang geng youmei ne?
19|74|Zai tamen zhiqian, wo ceng huimiele xuduo shidai, wulun zichan he waiguan, dou bi tamen geng youmei.
19|75|Ni shuo: Zai mi wu zhong de ren yuan zhiren zhu yourong tamen, zhidao tamen de jian tamen ceng bei jinggao de: Bushi xingfa, jiushi fuhuo shi tamen jiu zhidao shei di diwei geng elie, shei de jundui geng nuoruole.
19|76|Zhenzhu jiang wei zunxun zhengdao zhe zengjia qi yindao. Chang cun de shangong, zai ni de zhu kan lai shi baochou geng hao, jieju geng shan de.
19|77|Ni gaosu wo ba! Youren bu xin wo de jixiang, queshuo: Wo biyao huode caichan he zisi.
19|78|Ta ceng kuijian youxuan ne? Haishi ta ceng yu zhiren zhu ding yue ne?
19|79|Buran, wo jiang jilu tasuo shuo de, wo jiang wei ta jiazhong xingfa,
19|80|wo jiang jicheng tasuo shuo de caichan he zisi. Er ta jiang danshen lai jian wo.
19|81|Tamen she zhenzhu er chongbai xuduo zhuzai, zuowei ziji de quanli.
19|82|Buran, naxie zhuzai jiang fouren tamen de chongbai, er bian cheng tamen de choudi.
19|83|Ni hai bu zhidao ma? Wo ba emomen fang chuqu youhuo bu xindao zhe,
19|84|suo yi ni dui tamen buyao jizao, wo zhi shu tamen de shou shu.
19|85|Na ri, wo yao ba jingwei zhe jihe dao zhiren zhu di na li, xiangshou en rong.
19|86|Wo yao ba fanzui zhe quzhu dao huo yu qu, yi feishui jieke.
19|87|Dan yu zhiren zhu ding yue zhe chuwai, renmen bude shuo qing.
19|88|Tamen shuo: Zhiren zhu shouyang erzi.
19|89|Nimen que yi fanle yi jian zhongda zuixing. Weile na jian zuixing,
19|90|tian jihu yao po, de jihu yao lie, shan jihu yao beng.
19|91|Zhe shi yinwei tamen wangcheng renwei zhiren zhu de erzi.
19|92|Zhiren zhu bu hui shouyang erzi,
19|93|fan zai tiandi jian de, jianglai meiyou yige bu xiang nupu yiyang guiyi zhiren zhu de.
19|94|Ta que yi tongjiguo tamen, jiandianguo tamen.
19|95|Fuhuo ri tamen dou yao danshen lai jian ta.
19|96|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, zhiren zhu biding yao shi tamen xiangqin xiang'ai.
19|97|Wo yi ni de yuyan, shi “gulanjing” chengwei rongyi de, zhi wei yao ni jie ta xiang jingwei zhe baoxi, bing jinggao qiangbian de minzhong.
19|98|Zai tamen zhiqian, wo ceng huimiele xuduo shidai, ni neng faxian naxie shidai zhong de renhe ren, huo tingjian tamen suo fa de wei sheng ma?
20|1|Ta ha.

20|3|que wei jiaohui jingwei zhe,
20|4|shi jiang zi chuangzao dadi he cangqiong zhe de.
20|5|Zhiren zhu yi sheng shang baozuole.
20|6|Fan zai tianshang dixia de, zai tiandi zhi jian de, zai di dixia de, dou shi ta de.

20|8|Chu zhenzhu wai, jue wu ying shou chongbai zhe, ta you xuduo zuimei de ming hao.
20|9|Ni yi ting dao mu sa de gushile ma?
20|10|Dangshi, ta kanjian yi chu huoguang, jiu dui ta de jiashu shuo: Nimen shao liu yixia, wo que yi kanjian yi chu huole, yexu wo na yige huoba lai gei nimen, huoxu wo zai you huo di na li faxian xiangdao.
20|11|Ta lai dao nage huo de fujin, jiu you shengyin hanjiao shuo: Mu sa a!
20|12|Wo que shi ni de zhu, ni tuo diao ni de xiezi ba, ni que shi zai sheng gu du wa'zhong.
20|13|Wo que yi tiaoxuan ni, ni yingdang qingting qishi:
20|14|Wo que shi zhenzhu, chu wo wai, jue wu ying shou chongbai zhe. Ni yingdang chongbai wo, dang wei jinian wo er jin shou bai gong.
20|15|Fuhuo shi, que shi yao lailin de, wo jihu yao yincang ta, yibian mei geren dou yin ziji de xingwei er shou baochou.

20|17|Mu sa a! Zai ni youshou li de shi shenme?
20|18|Ta shuo: Zhe shi wo de shouzhang, wo zhuzhe ta, wo yong ta ba shuye jiluo xialai gei wo de yang chi, wo duiyu ta hai you bie de xuduo xuyao.

20|20|Ta jiu ba ta reng xiale, ta huran bian chengle yitiao wan yan de she.

20|24|Ni qu jian falao, ta que shi baonue wu dao de.

20|40|Dangshi, ni de jiejie zou qu shuo: Wo zhishi nimen yige yangyu ta de ren, hao ma? Wo jiu ba ni song hai ni muqin, yibian ta yukuai er bu youchou. Ni ceng shale yige ren, er wo zhengjiu ni tuoli youhuan, wo ceng yi xuduo zhemo kaoyan ni. Ni ceng zai mai de yan ren zhi jian douliule xuduo nian. Mu sa a! Ranhou, ni yi qian ding er lai dao zheli.
20|41|Wo wei ziji er tiaoxuan ni.
20|42|Ni he ni di gege, daizhe wo de xuduo jixiang qu ba! Ni lia duiyu jinian wo jue buke daiman.

20|44|Ni lia dui ta shuohua yao wenhe, huoxu ta hui jiqu jiaohui, huozhe you suo weiju.

20|47|Ni lia qu ta nali jiu shuo:'Wo lia que shi ni de zhu de shizhe, suoyi qing ni rang yiselie de houyi tong wo lia yidao qu, qing ni buyao nuedai tamen. Women yijing ba ni de zhu de yi zhong jixiang dai lai gei nile; zunshou zhengdao zhe, de xiang heping.
20|48|Women que yi feng dao qishi shuo: Fouren erqie beiqi zhe, jiang shou xingfa.
20|49|Ta shuo: Mu sa a! Shei shi ni lia de zhu?

20|53|Ta wei nimen yi dadi wei yaolan, ta wei nimen zai dadishang kaipi xuduo daolu, ta cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, er jie yushui shengchan ge zhong zhiwu.
20|54|Nimen keyi chi naxie zhiwu, keyi fangmu nimen de shengchu. Duiyu you lizhi zhe, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
20|55|Wo cong dadi chuangzao nimen, wo shi nimen fu fan yu dadi, wo zai yici shi nimen cong da di fuhuo.
20|56|Wo que yi zhishi ta wo suoyou de yi qie jixiang, er ta jiayi fouren, bu ken xindao.

20|70|Yushi, shushimen baidao xiaqu, tamen shuo: Women yi gui xin ha lun he mu sa de zhule.

20|72|Tamen shuo: Women jue bu yuan tiaoxuan ni er paoqi yi jianglin women de mingzheng he chuangzao women de zhuzai. Ni yao zenme ban jiu zenme ban ba! Ni zhi neng zai jinshi shenghuo zhong renyi er wei.
20|73|Women que yi xinyang women de zhu, yibian ta shemian women de guoshi, he zai ni de qiangpo xia women biaoyan moshu de zuixing. Zhenzhu (de shangci) shi geng hao de,(ta de xingfa) shi geng jiu de.

20|78|Falao tongling ta de jundui, gan shang tamen, sui wei haishui suo yanmo.

20|81|Nimen keyi chi wo suo shangci nimen de jiamei de shipin, dan buke guofen, yimian ying shou wo de qianze, shei ying shou wo de qianze, shei bi lunsang.

20|112|Xindao er xingshan zhe, bupa kui wang he kekou.
20|113|Wo zheyang jiang shi alabo wen de “gulanjing”, wo zai qizhong shenshu jinggao, yibian tamen jingwei, huo shi tamen jiyi.
20|114|Zhenzhu shi chaojue wanwu, zai zhi zhongsheng, ti yong zhenshi de. Dui ni qishi “gulanjing” hai meiyou wanquan de shihou, ni buyao jimang songdu. Ni shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni zengjia wo de zhishi.
20|115|Yiqian, wo que yi zhufu a dan, er ta wangji wo de zhufu, wo wei faxian ta you renhe juexin.

20|117|Wo shuo: A dan a! Zhe que shi ni de choudi, ye que shi ni de qizi de choudi, jue buyao rang ta ba ni lia zhu chu leyuan, yimian nimen xinku.
20|118|Ni zai leyuan li bi bu ji'e, bi bu luolu,
20|119|bi bu kou ke, bi bugan yanre.

20|122|Sihou, ta de zhu tiaoxuanle ta, raoshule ta, yindaole ta.
20|123|Ta shuo: Ni lia dou cong leyuan jiang xiaqu! Nimen jiang huxiang choushi. Ruguo zhengdao cong wo jianglin nimen, namo, shei zunxun wo de zhengdao, shei bu hui mi wu, ye bu hui daomei;

20|128|Nandao tamen bu zhidao ma? Zai tamen zhiqian, wo ceng huimiele xuduo shidai, tamen chang he naxie ren de guxiang wanglai, duiyu you lizhi zhe, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
20|129|Yao bushi you yiju hua cong ni de zhu yuxian fachu, yao bushi you qixian, ni de zhu jiayi yuding, name,(huimie duiyu tamen) shi biran de.

20|131|Ni buyao jiyu wo suoyong yi gongji tamen zhong ge deng ren xiangshou de, na shi jinshi shenghuo de fuhua, wo yong lai kaoyan tamen; ni de zhu de jiyang, shi geng hao de, shi geng jiu de.
20|132|Ni yingdang mingling ni de xintumen libai, ni duiyu bai gong, ye yingdang youheng, wo bu yi jiyang zecheng ni, wo gongji ni. Shan guo zhi guiyu jingwei zhe.
20|133|Tamen shuo: Ta zenme bu cong ta di nali na yi zhong jixiang lai gei women ne? Guanyu “gulanjing” de chanming, nandao meiyou jianglin tamen ma?

21|1|Dui zhongren de qingsuan yijing linjinle, tamen que zai shuhu zhi zhong, bu jiayi siwei.

21|112|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni binggong panjue. Women de zhu shi zhiren de zhu, duiyu nimen suoyong yi miaoshu ta de yanyu ta shi bei qiuzhu de.
22|1|Zhongren a! Nimen yingdang jingwei nimen de zhu, fuhuo shi di dizhen, que shi yi jian dashi.
22|2|Zai na ri, nimen kanjian dizhen xia mei ge rumu dou bei xia de wangjile ying'er, xia de mei ge yunfu dou yao liuchan; ni ba renmen kan cheng zui han, qishi tamen bingfei shi zui han, er shi yin wei zhenzhu de xingfa shi yanjun de.
22|3|Youren wuzhi di jinxing guanyu zhenzhu de zhenglun, bingqie shuncong panni de emo.
22|4|Fan jiejiao emo zhe, emo biding shi ta mi wu, biding ba ta yinru huo yu de xingfa, zhe shi emo gei zhudingle de.
22|5|Zhongren a! Ruguo nimen duiyu fuhuo de shi hai zai huaiyi zhi zhong, namo, wo que yi chuangzaole nimen, xian yong nitu, ji yong yi xiao di jingye, ji yong yikuai ningxie, ji yong wanzheng de he bu wanzheng de rou tuan, yibian wo dui nimen chanming (daoli). Wo shi wo suo yiyu de (tai'er) zai zigong li anju yige dingqi, ranhou, wo shi nimen chusheng wei ying'er, ranhou (wo rang nimen huozhe), yibian nimen dadao chengnian. Nimen zhong you yaozhe de; you fu fan yu zui lie de nianji de, yibian ta zai you zhishi zhihou, shenme ye bu zhidao. Ni kan dadi shi bumao de, dang wo shi yushui jiang yu dadi de shihou, ta jiu huodong he pengzhang, erqie shengchu ge zhong meili de zhiwu.
22|6|Zhe shi yin wei zhenzhu shi zhen zai, ta neng shi sizhe fusheng, ta duiyu wanshi shi quanneng de.
22|7|Fuhuo que shi yao lailin de, hao wuyi yi, zhenzhuyao shi fenmu li de ren fuhuo qilai.
22|8|Youren zhenglun zhenzhu, dan ta ji wu zhishi, you wu zhidao, qie wu canlan de jingdian.
22|9|Ta aoman de zou kai, yibian you ren panli zhenzhu de dadao. Ta zai jinshi yao shou lingru, fuhuo ri wo yao shi ta changshi shaozhuo de xingfa.
22|10|Zhe shi yinwei ni suo fan de zuixing, ye yin wei zhenzhu jue bushi kuidai zhong puren de.
22|11|Youren zai bianyuan shang chongbai zhenzhu, ruo huo fuli, ta jiu anran xiangshou; ruo zao huohai, ta jiu qingshuai beipan. Ta jiang sangshi jinshi he houshi, zhe shi mingxian de kuisun.
22|12|Ta she zhenzhu er qidao na duiyu ta ji wu huo you wu fu de dongxi, zhe shi bu jin qingli de mi wu.
22|13|Ta qidao na you jin huo er wu yuan fu de dongxi, ta de yuanzhu zhe zhen elie! Zuo ta de tongban de zhen elie!
22|14|Zhenzhu biding yao shi xindao erqie xingshan zhe jinru na xia lin zhu he de leyuan. Zhenzhu que shi weisuoyuwei de.
22|15|Shei caixiang zhenzhu zai jinshi he houshi jue bu xiangzhu ta, jiao shei xuanliang zijin, jiao ta kan ta de jice neng fou jiechu ta de fennu!
22|16|Wo zheyang jiang shi “gulanjing”, zuowei mingxian de jixiang, zhenzhu que shi yindao tasuo yu yindao de.
22|17|Xindao zhe, youtai jiaotu, bai xing jiaotu, jidu jiaotu, baihuojiao tu, yiji yi wu pei zhu zhe, fuhuo ri zhenzhu biding yao wei tamen panjue, zhenzhu que shi wanwu de jianzheng.
22|18|Ni nandao bu zhidao ma? Zai tianshang de he zai dishang de, yu ri yue qunxing, shanyue shumu, shengchu he xuduo ren, dou fucong zhenzhu, you xuduo ren dang shou xingfa. Zhenzhu lingru shei, shei bu shou ren zunjing. Zhen zhu que shi weisuoyuwei de.(Ci chu koutou!)※
22|19|Zhe liang pai shi xiang zheng de, tamen jinxing tamen guanyu tamen de zhu de zhenglun. Buxin zhe yijing you wei tamen er cai zhi de huo yile, feishui jiang qingzhu zai tamen de tou shang,
22|20|tamen de neizang he pifu jiang bei feishui suo ronghua,
22|21|tamen jiang xiangshou tie bian de chouda.
22|22|Tamen mei yin choumen er tao chu huo yu, dou bei lan huiqu. Nimen changshi shaozhuo de xingfa ba!
22|23|Zhenzhu biding yao shi xindao erqie xingshan zhe jinru na xia lin zhu he de leyuan, tamen zai qizhong de xiangyong jin zhuo he zhenzhu zuo zhuangshi, tamen de yifu shi sichou de.
22|24|Tamen ceng meng yindao, guchang shuo youmei de yuyan; tamen ceng meng yindao, gu zunxun shou zansong zhe de dadao.
22|25|Bu xindao erqie fang'ai zhu dao, bingqie fang'ai wo shi zhongren--dingju de he youmu de--gongtong zunjing jin si zhe,(wo jiang shi ta shaoshao changshi tongku de xingfa); shei yin bu yi er yu zai jin sizhong weibei zhengdao, wo jiang shi shei shaoshao changshi tongku de xingfa.
22|26|Dangshi wo ceng wei yi bo la xin zhiding tian fang di dizhi, wo shuo: Ni buyao yi renhe wu pei wo, ni yingdang wei huanxing zhe, lizheng zhe, jugong zhe he koutou zhe, dasao wo de fangwu.
22|27|Ni yingdang zai zhongren zhong xuangao chaojin, tamen jiu cong yuandao huo tubu huo chengzhe shou tuo, dao ni zheli lai,
22|28|yibian tamen jianzheng tamen suoyou de xuduo liyi, bingqie zai guiding de ruogan rinei, jinian zhenzhu zhi ming er tuzai ta ci gei tamen de shengchu nimen keyi chi naxie shengchu de rou, bingqie yingdang yong lai kuandai kunku de he pinqiong de ren.
22|29|Ranhou jiao tamen dichu tamen de wugou, jiao tamen luxing tamen de shiyuan, jiao tamen weirao na jian gu fang er huanxing.
22|30|Shiqing jiushi zheyang de, shei zunzhong zhenzhu de jielu, zai zhu di nali duiyu shei shi geng hao de. Yiqie shengchu dui nimen dou shi hefa de, dui nimen yi xuanbu jin jie de chuwai. Gu nimen yingdang bi kai wuhui ji ouxiang, yingdang yong li wangyu;
22|31|tongshi wei zhenzhu er xinfeng zhengjiao, bu yi wu pei ta. Shei yi wu pei zhenzhu, shei ru cong tiankong zhuiluo, er bei qun niao duo zou, huo bei dafeng saodang dao yuanfang.
22|32|Shiqing jiushi zheyang de, shei zunjing zhenzhu de biaozhi, na shi xinzhong de qiancheng fachu de.
22|33|Shengchu duiyu nimen, you ruogan liyi, zhiyu yige dingqi, ranhou (tuzai tamen zuo gong xian) de hefa difang yinggai shi gu fang de fujin.
22|34|Wo wei mei ge minzu zhiding yi zhong gong xian de yishi, yibian tamen jinian zhenzhu zhi ming er tuzai ta suo ci tamen de shengchu. Nimen de shenming shi du yi de shenming, gu nimen yingdang zhi guishun ta. Ni yingdang yi xixun chuan shi qiangong zhe.
22|35|Dang jinian zhenzhu de shihou, zhongxin gandao kongju zhe--gandao zhanli zhe--renshou kunan zhe, jin shou bai gong zhe, fen she wo suo ci zhi wu zhe,
22|36|wo wei nimen yi luotuo wei zhenzhu de biaozhi, tamen duiyu nimen you xuduo yongchu; tamen pailie chengxing de shihou, nimen yingdang wei tuzai tamen er jinian zhenzhu zhi ming; dang tamen ce wo zai dishang de shihou, nimen keyi chi tamen de rou, bing yingdang yong lai kuandai zhizu de pinmin he qitao de pinmin. Wo wei nimen zhifu tamen, yibian nimen ganxie.
22|37|Tamen de rou he xue, dou buneng dadao zhenzhu, dan nimen de qiancheng, neng dadao ta. Ta wei nimen zheyang zhifu tamen, yibian nimen wei zhenzhu dui nimen de yindao er zunchong ta. Ni yingdang xiang xingshan zhe baoxi.
22|38|Zhenzhu biding yao baohu xindao zhe, zhenzhu que shi bu xi'ai mei ge wang'enfuyi de panni zhe de.
22|39|Bei jingong zhe, yi huode fankang de xuke, yinwei tamen shi shou yapo de. Zhenzhu duiyu yuanzhu tamen, que shi quanneng de.
22|40|Tamen bei zhu chu guxiang, zhi yin tamen chang shuo: Women de zhu shi zhenzhu. Yao bushi zhenzhu yi shiren huxiang dikang, name xuduo xiudaoyuan, libaitang, youtai huitang, qingzhensi--qizhong chang youren jinian zhenzhu zhi ming de jianzhu wu--biding bei ren pohuaile. Fan fuzhu zhenzhu de dadao zhe, zhenzhu biding fuzhu ta; zhenzhu que shi zhi qiang de, que shi wanneng de.
22|41|Ruguo wo shi naxie ren zai dimian shang deshi, tamen jiang jin shou bai gong, wan na tian ke, quan shan jie e. Wanshi de jieju zhi guizhenzhu.
22|42|Ruguo tamen fouren ni, namo, zai tamen zhiqian, fouren shizhe de yi you nu ha de zongzu, a de ren, sai mo de ren,
22|43|yi bo la xin de zongzu, lu te de zongzu,
22|44|mai de yan ren; mu sa ye ceng fourenguo. Wo yourong bu xindao zhe, suihou wo chengzhile tamen; wo de qianze shi zenyang de ne?
22|45|You xuduo chengshi jumin bu yi, er wo huimie tamen, dishang wuding shang cun, bingqie you ruogan bei yiqi de shuijing he bei jiancheng de dasha.
22|46|Nandao tamen meiyou zai da dishang luxing, yin'er youxin keyi liaojie, huozhe you er keyi tingwen ma? Yinwei rouyan bu mang, xiongzhong de xinyan que mangle.
22|47|Tamen yaoqiu ni zaori zhaoshi xingfa. Zhen zhu jue bu shuangyue. Zai ni de zhu nali de yi ri, qiaru nimen suo shu de yiqian nian.
22|48|You xuduo chengshi, jumin bu yi, er wo yourong tamen, suihou, wo chengzhi tamen, wo shi weiyi de guisu.
22|49|Ni shuo: Zhongren a! Wo dui nimen zhishi yige zhishuang de jinggao zhe.
22|50|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, de meng she you, de xiang youhou de jiyang;
22|51|yi zunao de taidu nuli fandui wo de jixiang zhe, shi huo yu de jumin.
22|52|Zai ni zhiqian wo suo paiqian de shizhe he xianzhi, meiyouyige bushi zheyang de: Dang ta yuanwang de shihou, emo duiyu ta de yuanwang, you yi zhong jianyi, dan zhenzhu pochu emo de jianyi, ranhou, zhenzhu shi ziji de jixiang chengwei jian que de. Zhenzhu shi quanzhi de, shi zhi rui de.
22|53|(Ta zheyang zuo) yibian ta yi emo jianyi de shi kaoyan you xinbing de ren he xin ying de ren. Bu yi zhe bi xianyu changyuan de fenlie zhi zhong.
22|54|(Ta zheyang zuo) yibian you xueshi zhe zhidao na shi cong ni de zhu jiang shi de zhenli, yinwei tamen xinyang ta, er tamen dui ta xinhuai qianxun. Zhenzhu biding yao fan xindao zhe yin shang zhenglu.
22|55|Bu xindao zhe duiyu ta rengran zai youyu zhi zhong, zhidao fuhuo shike huran jianglin tamen, huo pohuai ri de xingfa lailin tamen.
22|56|Zai na ri, zhuquan zhishi zhenzhu de. Ta yao panjue tamen. Xindao erqie xingshan, jiang zai ji leyuan zhong;
22|57|bu xindao erqie fouren wo de jixiang zhe, jiang shou lingru de xingfa.
22|58|Wei zhenzhu er qianju, ranhou bei shahai huo binggu zhe, zhenzhu bi shangci tamen jiamei de jiyang; zhenzhu que shi zui shanyu jiyang de.
22|59|Ta bi shi tamen jinru tamen suo xiyue di difang; zhenzhu que shi quanzhi de, que shi rongren de.
22|60|Shiqing jiushi zheyang de. Fan yi yuan baoyuan, ranhou bei ren nuedai zhe, zhenzhu bi yuanzhu ta. Zhenzhu que shi zhi shu de, que shi zhi she de.
22|61|Zhe shi yin wei zhenzhu shi heiye qinru baizhou, shi baizhou qinru heiye; you yin wei zhenzhu shi quan cong de, shi quan ming de.
22|62|Zhe shi yin wei zhenzhu shi zhenshi de, tamen she zhenzhu er qidao de (ouxiang) shi xuwang de; you yin wei zhenzhu shi zhizun de, shi zhi da de.
22|63|Nandao ni bu zhidao ma? Zhenzhu cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, dimian jiu bian cheng cangcui de. Zhenzhu que shiren'ai de, que shi che zhi de.
22|64|Tiandi wanwu dou shi ta de, zhenzhu que shi wu qiu de, que shi ke song de.
22|65|Nandao ni bu zhidao ma? Zhenzhu wei nimen zhifu da dishang suoyou de shiwu, yiji feng ta de ming er zai haishang hangxing de chuanbo, ta weichizhe tian yimian zhuiluo zai dishang, chufei huode ta xuke. Zhenzhu duiyu shiren que shi zhi ai de, que shi zhi ci de.
22|66|Ta shi nimen sheng, ranhou shi nimen si, ranhou shi nimen fuhuo; ren que shi gu en de.
22|67|Wo wei mei ge minzu zhiding yi zhong gong xian yishi, rang tamen you de zunxun, jue bushi rang tamen wei zhe shi yu ni zhenglun. Ni yingdang zhaohuan zhongren lai chongbai ni de zhu, ni que shi zai zheng lushang de.
22|68|Ruguo tamen yu ni zhenglun, ni yingdang shuo: Zhenzhu shi zhidao nimen de xingwei de.
22|69|Fuhuo ri, zhenzhu jiang panjue nimen suo zhenglun de shifei.
22|70|Nandao ni bu zhidao ma? Zhenzhu zhidao tiandi wanwu, zhe que shi zai yi ben tian jing li de. Zhe duiyu zhenzhu que shi rongyi de.
22|71|Tamen she zhenzhu er chongbai zhenzhu suo wei zhengshi de, ye fei tamen suo zhidao de ouxiang; bu yi de ren jue meiyou renhe yuanzhu zhe.
22|72|Dang bieren dui tamen xuandu wo de mingxian de jixiang de shihou, ni kanjian bu xindao zhe de lian shang you bu yuezhi se; tamen jihu yao xiji dui tamen xuandu wo de jixiang zhe. Ni shuo: Wo gaosu nimen bi zhege geng elie de hao ma? Na jiushi huo yu. Zhenzhu yi huo yu yingxu bu xindao zhe, na guisu zhen elie!
22|73|Zhongren a! You yige piyu, nimen qingting ba! Nimen she zhenzhu er qidao de (ouxiang) sui quncequnli, jue buneng chuangzao yi zhi cangying; ruguo cangying cong tamen de shenshang duoqu yidian dongxi, tamen ye buneng ba na dian dongxi qiang huilai. Qidao zhe he bei qidao zhe, dou shi nuoruo de!
22|74|Tamen meiyou zhenshi di zunjing zhenzhu. Zhenzhu que shi zhi qiang de, que shi wanneng de.
22|75|Zhenzhu cong tianshen zhong, yu renlei zhong jianxuan ruogan shizhe, zhenzhu que shi quan cong de, que shi quan ming de.
22|76|Ta zhidao tamen yi zuo de he jiang zuo de shiqing, wanshi zhi guizhenzhu.
22|77|Xindao de renmen a! Nimen yingdang jugong, yingdang koutou, yingdang chongbai nimen de zhu, yingdang li xingshan gong, yibian nimen chenggong.(Ci chu koutou!)※
22|78|Nimen yingdang wei zhenzhu er zhenshi di fendou. Ta jianxuan nimen, guanyu zongjiao de shi, ta weiceng yi renhe fannan wei nimen de yiwu, nimen yingdang zunxun nimen de zuxian yi bo la xin de zongjiao, yiqian zhenzhu cheng nimen wei musilin, zai zhe bu jingdian li ta ye cheng nimen wei musilin, yibian shizhe wei nimen zuozheng, er nimen wei shi ren zuozheng. Nimen dang jin shou bai gong, wan na tian ke, xintuo zhen zhu; ta shi nimen de zhuzai, zhuzai zhen hao! Zhu zhe zhen hao!
23|1|Xinshimen que yi chenggongle;
23|2|tamen zai bai zhong shi gongshun de,
23|3|tamen shi yuanli miulun de,
23|4|tamen shi wan na tian ke de,
23|5|tamen shi baochi zhencao de
23|6|chufei dui tamen de qizi he nunu, yinwei tamen de xin bushi shou qianze de;
23|7|ciwai, shei zai you suo qiu, shei shi chaoyue fadu de
23|8|Tamen shi zunzhong ziji suo shou de xintuo he ziji suo di de mengyue de,
23|9|tamen shi jin shou bai gong de;
23|10|zhe deng ren, cai shijicheng zhe.
23|11|Tamen shi jicheng leyuan de, tamen jiang yong ju qizhong.
23|12|Wo que yi yong nitu de jinghua chuangzao ren,
23|13|ranhou, wo shi ta bian cheng jingye, zai jiangu de rongqi zhong de jingye,
23|14|ranhou, wo ba jingye zaocheng xiekuai, ranhou, wo ba xiekuai zaocheng rou tuan, ranhou, wo ba rou tuan zaocheng guge, ranhou, wo shi jirou fuzhuo zai guge shang, ranhou wo ba ta zaocheng bie de shengwu. Yuan zhenzhu jiang fu, ta shi zui shanyu chuangzao de.
23|15|Cihou, nimen biding siwang,
23|16|ranhou, nimen zai fuhuo ri biding yao fuhuo.
23|17|Wo zai nimen de shangmian que yi zaole qitiao guidao, wo dui zhongsheng, bushi shuhu de.
23|18|Wo cong yun zhong jiangxia dingliang de yushui, ranhou, wo shi ta tingliu zai dixia--wo duiyu shi ta ganhe, shi quanneng de
23|19|ranhou, wo jie ta er wei nimen chuangzao xuduo zao yuan he putao yuan, qizhong you xuduo shuiguo dou shi nimen de, nimen de qu er shi zhi.
23|20|Wo you jie ta er wei nimen chuangzao yi zhong shu, cong xinai shan fachu, nengsheng you zhi he zuoliao, gong shi zhe tiaowei zhi yong.
23|21|Shengchu zhong duiyu nimen que youyi zhong jiaoxun, wo shi nimen de yin tamen fu zhong de ruzhi, de xiangshou tamen de xuduo biyi, nimen you de shi tamen de rou,
23|22|nimen you de yong tamen he chuanbo lai gong zaiyun.
23|23|Wo que yi paiqian nu ha qu jiaohua ta de zongzu, ta shuo: Wo de zongzu a! Nimen yingdang chongbai zhenzhu, chu ta zhi wai, jue wu ying shou nimen chongbai de. Nandao nimen bu jingwei ma?
23|24|Ta de zongzu zhong buxindao de toumumen shuo: Zhege ren zhishi xiang nimen yiyang de yige fanren, ta xiang huode nimen de zunzhong. Jiaruo zhenzhuyao pai shizhe, biding jiangxia xuduo tianshen. Women meiyou ting dao zai women de zuxian de shidai fashengguo zheyang de shi.
23|25|Ta zhishi yige fengzi, gu nimen yingdang dengdai ta yige shiqi.
23|26|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni yuanzhu wo, yinwei tamen yi fouren wole.
23|27|Wo jiu qishi ta shuo: Ni zai wo de zhaogu xia, yi wo de qishi er zaochuan. Dang wo de mingling lailin, er hongshui fanlan yu dimian de shihou, ni ba mei zhong dongwu, ge qu yi dui, fang zai chuanshang, shi ni de jiashu ye shang chuan qu; tamen zhong yi bei panjue zhe chuwai. Ni buyao wei bu yi zhe er qidao wo, tamen biran bei yan si.
23|28|Dang ni he tongchuan zhe zai chuanshang zuo ding de shihou, ni yingdang shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu--ta ceng zhengjiu women tuo li liao bu yi de minzhong.
23|29|Ni yingdang shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qing ni shi women zai yige jixiang di difang denglu, ni shi zui hui anzhi zhongsheng de.
23|30|Ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang, wo que shi kaoyan zhe.
23|31|Zai tamen miewang zhihou, wo chuangzaole bie de shidai,
23|32|wo cong tamen zu zhong paile yige shizhe, qu jiaohua tamen (shuo): Nimen yingdang chongbai zhen zhu, chule ta, nimen jue wu ying shou chongbai zhe, nandao nimen bu jingwei ma?
23|33|Ta de zongzu zhong de toumu, bu xindao erqie fouren houshi de xiang hui zhe, wo shi tamen zai jinshi deguo haohua de shenghuo. Tamen shuo: Zhege zhishi xiang nimen yang de fanren: Ta chi nimen suo chi de, ta yin nimen suo yin de.
23|34|Ruguo nimen shuncong xiang nimen yang de yige fanren, nimen biding shi kuisun de.
23|35|Ta jinggao nimen shuo:'Dang nimen si hou, yibian cheng chen'ai he xiu gu shi, biding yao fuhuo'ma?
23|36|Ta suoyong lai jinggao nimen de shi, tai bu jin qinglile.
23|37|Women zhiyou jinshi shenghuo, women si, women sheng, women jue bu hui fuhuo.
23|38|Ta zhishi yige ren jiajie zhen zhu de mingyi er zaoyao, women jue bu xin ta!
23|39|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni yuanzhu wo, yinwei tamen yijing fouren wole.
23|40|Zhu shuo: Bujiu, tamen biran yao huihen.
23|41|Xingfa gongdao di xijile tamen, er wo shi tamen bian chengle feiliao, bu yi de minzhong yi zao huimiele.
23|42|Zai tamen miewang zhihou, wo you xingqi bie de ji ge shidai.
23|43|Renhe shidai, dou buneng zai ziji de qixian zhiqian miewang, ye buneng zai ziji de qixian zhihou lunsang.
23|44|Ranhou, wo luxu de paiqian wo de zhong shizhe, mei ge zu de shizhe lailin tamen shi, tamen dou fouren ta, guwo shi tamen xiangji miewang, er shi tamen de shi ji bian cheng huabing. Bu xindao de minzhong yi zao huimie.
23|45|Ranhou, wo paiqian mu sa he ta gege ha lun, ba wo de xuduo jixiang he mingzheng,
23|46|chuan shi falao he ta de chenmin, dan tamen zi da, tamen shi gao'ao de.
23|47|Tamen shuo: Women zen neng xinyang xiang women yang de liang ge fanren ne? Hekuang ta lia de zongzu shi fushi women de.
23|48|Tamen fouren ta lia, gu zaoyu huimie.
23|49|Wo que yi ba tian jing shangci mu sa, yi bian tamen zunxun zhengdao.
23|50|Wo yi mai er yan he ta de erzi wei yi zhong jixiang, wo shi ta lia zai you pingdi he liushui de gaoyuan huode yige yin bi zhi suo.
23|51|Zhong shizhe a! Nimen keyi chi jiamei de shiwu, yingdang li xingshan gong, wo duiyu nimen de xingwei que shi quanzhi de.
23|52|Zhege que shi nimen de tongyi de minzu wo shi nimen de zhu, gu nimen yingdang jingwei wo.
23|53|Dan tamen wei jiaoyi er fenlie cheng xuduo zongpai, ge pai dou yin ziji de jiaoyi er zhanzhanzixi.
23|54|Ni rang tamen zhanshi chenjin zai ziji de kunjing zhi zhong ba.
23|55|Tamen yiwei wo suoyong lai zizhu tamen de caichan he zisun,
23|56|shi wo yong lai shi tamen kuai de fuli de (shouduan) ma? Buran, tamen shi bu xiaode de.
23|57|Wei jingwei zhu er kongju zhe,
23|58|xinyang zhu de jixiang zhe,
23|59|bu yi wu pei zhu zhe,
23|60|you suo shishe, dan yinwei jiang guiyu zhu er xinhuai kongbu zhe,
23|61|zhe deng ren dou shi zhengxian xingshan, erqie zui xian huode shan bao de.
23|62|Wo zhi yige ren de nengli er jiayi zecheng. Wo youyi ben shu xuanyan zhenli, tamen shi bu bei kuidai de.
23|63|Buran, tamen de xin, duiyu zhe bu jingdian, shi jinchen zai kunjing zhi zhong de. Ciwai, tamen hai you xuduo xingwei, jiangyao zuo chulai.
23|64|Zhidao wo yi xingfa chengzhi tamen zhongguo haohua shenghuo zhe de shihou, tamen huran da hu qiujiu.
23|65|Jintian, nimen buyao da hu qiujiu. Nimen biding buneng huode wo de yuanzhu.
23|66|Wo de jixiang, que yi dui nimen xuanduguole, dan nimen xuanzhong er tui,
23|67|bu ken xinyang, que yong zuo ye tan de ziliao, erqie jiayi biqi.
23|68|Tamen meiyou shusi zhenyan ne? Haishi meiyou jianglin tamen de zuxian de jingdian yi jianglin tamen ne?
23|69|Haishi tamen meiyou renshi tamen de shizhe, yin'er bu chengren ta ne?
23|70|Haishi tamen shuo ta you feng bing ne?--Buran, ta yi zhenli zhaoshi tamen, dan tamen daban shi yanwu zhenli de.
23|71|Jiaruo zhenli shuncong tamen de siyu, tiandi wanwu, biran huihuai. Buran, wo yi ba tamen de jiaohui zhaoshi tamen, dan tamen beiqi tamen de jiaohui.
23|72|Nandao ni xiang tamen suoqu baochou ma? Ni de zhu de shangci shi geng hao de, ta shi zui shanyu jiyang de.
23|73|Ni que shi haozhao tamen zou zhenglu de.
23|74|Buxin houshi zhe, que shi pianli zhenglu de.
23|75|Jiaruo wo lianmin tamen, erqie jiechu tamen suo zao de kunan, tamen bi guzhi hengman, er pai paihuai yu qitu zhi zhong.
23|76|Wo que yi yong xingfa chengzhi tamen, dan tamen bu shuncong tamen de zhu, tamen ye budui ta biaoshi qianxun.
23|77|Zhidao wo dui tamen kaipi yanxing zhi men de shihou, tamen wei ta er huran bian cheng shiwang zhe.
23|78|Zhu ceng wei nimen chuangzao ermu he xin, nimen de ganxie shi hen shao de.
23|79|Ta ceng shi nimen zai dadishang fanzhi, nimen yao bei jihe zai ta nali,
23|80|ta shi si wu sheng, shi shengwu si, zhouye de gengdie you ta zhuchi. Nandao nimen bu liaojie ma?
23|81|Buran, tamen shuo liao ru guren suo shuo dehua,
23|82|tamen shuo: Women si hou, yi bian cheng chen'ai he xiu gu de shihou, nandao women hai biding yao fuhuo ma?
23|83|Women he women de zuxian, yiqian que yi shouguo zhe zhong jinggaole. Zhege zhishi guren de shenhua.

24|1|(Zhe shi) yi zhang jing, wo jiang shi ta, bing yi ta wei dingzhi, qie zai qizhong jiang shi xuduo mingxian de jixiang, yibian nimen jiyi.
24|2|Yin fu he jian fu, nimen yingdang ge da yibai bian. Nimen buyao wei lianmin ta lia er jianmian zhenzhu de xingfa, ruguo nimen quexin zhenzhu he mori. Jiao yi huo xinshi, jianshi ta lia de shouxing.
24|3|Jian fu zhide qu yin fu, huo qu duoshenjiao tu; yin fu zhide jia jian fu, huo jia duoshenjiao tu, xindao zhe bude qu ta.
24|4|Fan gaofa zhenjie de funu, er buneng ju chu si ge nanzi wei jianzheng zhe, nimen yingdang ba mei geren da bashi bian, bingqie yongyuan buke jieshou tamen de jianzheng. Zhe deng ren shi zuiren.
24|5|Yihou huiguo zi xin zhe chuwai, yin wei zhenzhu que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.

24|9|di wu ci shi shuo: Ta ganshou tianqian, ruguo ta shi shuo shihua de.
24|10|Jiaruo wu zhenzhu suo ci nimen de enhui he renci, ruguo zhenzhu bushi zhi she de, bushi zhi rui de,
24|11|zaoyao zhe que shi nimen zhong de yi huo ren. Nimen buyao yiwei zhe jian shi duiyu nimen shi youhai de, qishi shi youyi de. Tamen zhong de mei geren, ge yingdang shou tasuo mouqiu de zui'e; tamen zhong de zuikui, ying shou zhongda de xingfa.
24|12|Dang nimen tingjian yaoyan de shihou, xinshi hexin nu dui ziji de jiao bao, weihe buzuo shanyi de caixiang, bingqie shuo: Zhe shi mingxian de yaoyan ne?

24|21|Xinshimen a! Nimen buyao zhuisui emo de bufa. Shei zhuisui emo de bufa, emo bi mingling shei gan choushi he fan zuixing. 24|22|Nimen zhong you enhui he caifu zhe buke fashi (shuo): Yong bu zhouji qinqi, pinmin ji wei zhu dao er qianju zhe. Tamen yingdang shu rao, yingdang yuanliang. Nandao nimen bu yuan zhenzhu she you nimen ma? Zhenzhu shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
24|23|Fan gaofa zhenjie de erqie tianzhen lanman de xin nu de ren, zai jinshi he houshi, bi zao zuzhou, tamen jiang shou zhongda de xingfa.
24|24|Zai na ri, tamen de shetou he shouzu dou yao fanzheng tamen zhi suo wei.
24|25|Zai na ri, zhenzhuyao shi tamen xiangshou tamen suo ying de de wanquan de baoying, tamen yao zhidao zhen zhu cai shi zhenshi de, cai shi xianzhu de.
24|26|Elie de funu, zhuan pei elie de nanren; elie de nanren, zhuan pei elie de funu; shanliang de funu, zhuan pei shanliang de nanren; shanliang de nanren, zhuan pei shanliang de funu; zhe deng ren yu eren suo shuo de quan bu xianggan, tamen jiang meng she you, bing xiang youhou de jiyang.
24|27|Xindao de renmen a! Nimen buyao jin taren de jia qu, zhidao nimen qingqiu xuke, bing xiang zhuren zhu an. Zhe duiyu nimen shi geng gaoshang de,(zhenzhu zheyang zhidao nimen), yibian nimen neng jiqu jiaohui.

24|29|Ruguo fangwu nei meiyou sijia juzhu, er qizhong you nimen ziji de caiwu, nimen wufang jinqu. Zhenzhu zhidao nimen suo biaoxian de, he nimen suo yincang de.
24|30|Ni dui xinshimen shuo, jiao tamen jiangdi shixian, zhebi xiashen, zhe duiyu tamen shi geng chunjie de. Zhenzhu que shi che zhi tamen de xingwei de.
24|31|Ni dui xin numen shuo, jiao tamen jiangdi shixian, zhebi xiashen, mo luchushoushi, chufei ziran luchu de, jiao tamen yong miansha zhe zhu xiongtang, mo luchu shoushi, chufei dui tamen de zhangfu, huo tamen de fuqin, huo tamen de zhangfu de fuqin, huo tamen de erzi, huo tamen de zhangfu de erzi, huo tamen de xiongdi, huo tamen dixiong de erzi, huo tamen jiemei de erzi, huo tamen de nupu, huo tamen de nubi, huo wu xingyu de nan pu, huo bu dong funu zhi shi de ertong; jiao tamen buyao yongli tazu, shi ren de zhi tamen suo yincang de shoushi. 24|32|Nimen zhong weihun de nannu he nimen de shanliang de nubi, nimen yingdang shi tamen huxiang peihe. Ruguo tamen shi pinqiong de, namo, zhenzhuyao yi ta de enhui, shi tamen fuzu. Zhenzhu shi fuyu de, shi quanzhi.
24|33|Buneng qu qi zhe, jiao tamen jili baochi zhencao, zhidao zhenzhu yi ta de enhui er shi tamen fuzu. 24|34|Wo que yi ba xuduo mingbai de jixiang he zai nimen zhiqian shiqu zhe de xianli, yiji duiyu jingwei zhe de jiaoxun, jiang shi nimen.

24|61|Yu ren tongxi, duiyu mangren shi wu zuiguo de, duiyu quezi shi wu zuiguo de, duiyu bingren yeshi wu zuiguo de. 24|62|Xinshi zhishi xinyang zhenzhu ji qi shizhe de ren. Dang tamen wei renhe yao shi er yu shizhe jihui de shihou, tamen bu tuixi, zhidao tamen xiang ta qingqiu yunxu. 24|64|Zhen de, tiandi wanwu, que shi zhenzhu de. Ta que yi zhidao nimen de shiqing. Dang tamen bei zhao dao zhu nali zhi ri, ta yao ba tamen de xingwei gaosu tamen. Zhenzhu shi quanzhi wanshi de.
25|1|Shengjie zai zhenzhu! Ta jiang shi zhunze gei ta de puren, yibian ta zuo quan shijie de jinggao zhe.

25|8|huozhe ba yige caibao shangci ta, huozhe ta you yizuo guoyuan, gong ta shiyong ne? Bu yi zhe shuo: Nimen zhi shuncong yige bei guhuozhe.

25|13|Dang tamen bei jiasuozhe touru liehuo zhong yige xia'ai difang de shihou, tamen zai nali aihao qiu si.
25|14|Jintian nimen buyao aiqiu yisi, nimen dang aiqiu duo si.
25|15|Ni shuo: Zhe shi geng hao de ne? Haishi yingxu jingwei zhe yong ju qizhong de leyuan geng hao ne? Ta shi tamen suoyou de baochou he guisu,
25|16|tamen zai leyuan zhong de xiangshou ziji suo yiyu de (xingfu). Tamen jiang yong ju qizhong, zhe shi keyi xiang ni de zhu yaoqiu shijian de nuoyan.
25|17|Zai na ri, ta yao ba tamen he tamen she zhenzhu er chongbai de (ouxiang) jihe qilai, ranhou shuo: Jiujing shi nimen shi wo de zhexie puren mi wu ne? Haishi tamen ziji panli zhenglu ne?
25|18|Tamen shuo: Women zansong ni chaojue wanwu, women bu gai she ni er jing shi renhe shenling. Dan ni ceng shi tamen ji qi zuxian xiangle, zhidao tamen yiwangle jinian, tamen yuan shi miewang de minzhong.
25|19|Zhu shuo: Tamen que yi fouren nimen suo shuo dehua, nimen buneng taobi xingfa, ye buneng zizhu. Nimen zhong shei shi bu yi de, wo yao shi shei changshi yanjun de xingfa.
25|20|Wo zai ni zhiqian suo paiqian de shizhe, meiyou yige shi bu chifan de, meiyou yige shi bu laiwang yu shichang zhi jian de. Wo shi nimen huxiang kaoyan, kan kan nimen neng rennai ma? Ni de zhu shi mingcha de.
25|21|Bu xiwang yu wo xiang hui zhe ceng shuo: Zenme bu shi zhong tianshen jianglin women, huozhe de jian women de zhu ne? Tamen que yi wangzizunda, que yi danibudao.
25|22|Tamen kanjian zhong tianshen de rizi, fanzui zhe jiang meiyou hao xiaoxi, zhong tianshen yao dui tamen shuo:(Leyuan duiyu nimen) shi ying wei yanjin de.
25|23|Wo jiang chuli tamen suo xing de shangong, er shi ta bian cheng feiyang de huichen.
25|24|Zai na ri, leyuan de jumin jiang zai yige zui you de juzhu zhi di, yige zuimei de xiuxi zhi suo.
25|25|Zai na ri, zhu tian jiang yu baiyun yidao polie, zhong tianshen jiang fengming zhuangyan di jianglin.
25|26|Zai na ri, zhenshi de guotu shi shuyu zhiren zhu de. Na ri, dui bu xindao zhe shi yige yanku de rizi.
25|27|Zai na ri, bu yi zhe yimian yao shou yimian shuo: A! Dan yuan wo ceng yu shizhe caiqu tongyi daolu.
25|28|A! Ai zai! Dan yuan wo meiyou yi mou renwei pengyou.
25|29|Jinian ji jianglin zhihou, ta que yi shi wo weibei ta. Emo xianglai shi yiqi ren de.
25|30|Shizhe ceng shuo: Wo de zhu a! Wo de zongzu yi zhe “gulanjing” wei qi wu.
25|31|Wo zheyang shi mei ge xianzhi, dou you yixie zuiren zuo ta de choudi, ni de zhu zu wei yindao zhe he yuanzhu zhe.
25|32|Bu xindao zhe ceng shuo: Zenme bu ba quanbu “gulanjing” yici jiang shi ta ne? Wo nayang ling ling xingxing di jiang shi ta yibian wo ping ta lai jianding ni de xin, wo zhujian jiang shi ta.
25|33|Tamen mei xiang ni tichu yi zhong feinan, wo jiu qishi ni zhenli he geng meiman de jieshi.
25|34|Naxie bei pufuzhe jihe yu huo yu zhe diwei geng elie, shi pianli zhenglu geng yuan de.
25|35|Wo que yi ba jingdian shangci mu sa, bingqie renming ta di gege ha lun zuo ta de zhushou.
25|36|Wo shuo: Ni lia qu jiaohua naxie fouren wo de jixiang de minzhong. Wo zhongyu huimiele tamen.
25|37|Nu ha de zongzu fouren shizhe de shihou, wo yan sile tamen, bingqie yi tamen wei shiren de jianjie. Wo yiwei bu yi zhe zhunbeile tongku de xingfa.
25|38|A de ren, sai mo de ren, lan si de jumin yiji zai tamen zhi jian de ruogan shidai,
25|39|wo yi wei mei yige shidai de ren chanmingguo xuduo piyu, wo huimiele mei yi shidai de ren.
25|40|Tamen que yi jingli na zao e yu de chengshi, nandao tamen meiyou kanjian ta ma? Buran, tamen bu xiwang fuhuo.
25|41|Dang tamen jian ni de shihou, zhi ba ni dang zuo xiaobing, (tamen shuo): Zhe jiushi zhenzhu pai lai dang shizhe de ma?
25|42|Yao bushi women jianchizhe yao chongbai women de shenling, name, ta jihu shi women pianli tamenle. Tamen kanjian xingfa de shihou, jiangyao zhidao shei shi pianli zhenglu de.
25|43|Ni gaosu wo ba, yi siyu wei qi shenling zhe, ni neng zuo ta de jianhu zhe ma?
25|44|Nandao ni yi wei tamen daban shi neng tingcong huo zhe neng liaojie de ren ma? Tamen zhi xiang shengchu yiyang, tamen shenzhi shi geng mi wu de.
25|45|Nandao ni meiyou kanjian ni de zhu zenyang shenzhan yinying ma? Jiaruo ta yiyu, ta biding shi yinying chengwei jingzhi de. Wo yi taiyang wei qi biaozhi,
25|46|ranhou wo zhujian de shouhui yinying.
25|47|Zhu yi heiye wei nimen de yifu, yi shuimian gong nimen anxi, yi baizhou gong nimen suxing.
25|48|Zhu zai jiang en zhiqian, shi feng xian lai fu xi. Wo cong yun zhong jiangxia qingjie de yushui,
25|49|yibian wo jie yushui er shi yi si de dadi fuhuo, bingyong yushui gong wo suo chuangzao de shengchu he renmen zuo yinliao.
25|50|Wo que yi ba yushui fen pei zai tamen zhi jian, yibian tamen jiyi. Dan tamen daban zhi yuan wang'enfuyi.
25|51|Jiaruo wo yiyu, wo bi zai mei zuo chengshi zhong paiqian yige jinggao zhe.
25|52|Suoyi ni buyao shuncong bu xindao zhe, ni yingdang jie ci “gulanjing” er yu tamen nuli fendou.
25|53|Ta jiushi ren liang hai zhi jian ziyou jiaoliu de, zhe shi hen tian de danshui, na shi hen ku de xian shui; ta zai liang hai zhi jian shezhi pingzhang he difang.
25|54|Ta jiushi yong jing shui chuangzao ren, shi ren chengwei xuezu he yinqin de. Ni de zhu shi quanneng de.
25|55|Tamen she zhenzhu er chongbai naxie dui tamen ji wu fu you wu huo de dongxi, bu xindao zhe shi xiezhu taren yi fankang ziji de zhu de.
25|56|Wo zhi paiqian ni wei baoxi zhe he jinggao zhe.
25|57|Ni shuo: Wo duiyu wancheng zhe xiang shiming, bu xiang nimen suoqu renhe baochou, dan wang youzhi zhe neng you ci dadao er dadao qi zhuzai.
25|58|Ni yingdang xinren yongsheng bu mie de zhu, ni yingdang zansong ta chaojue wanwu. Ta zuyi che zhi ta de zuiguo.
25|59|Zai liu rinei chuangzao tiandi wanwu, ranhou sheng shang baozuo de, shi zhiren zhu. Ni yingdang yi ta (de dexing) qingjiao jingming zhe.
25|60|Ruguo youren dui tamen shuo: Nimen yingdang wei zhiren zhu er koutou. Tamen jiu shuo: Zhiren zhu shi shenme? Nandao women yin feng ni de mingling er koutou ma? Na shi tamen gengjia fangan.(Ci chu koutou!)※
25|61|Shengjie zai zhenzhu! Ta ba xuduo gong zao zai tianshang, youzao mingdeng he canlan de yueliang.
25|62|Ta jiushi wei yu juewu huo yu ganxie zhe, er shi zhouye gengdie de.
25|63|Zhiren zhu de puren shi zai dadishang qianxun er xing de; dang yuren yi e yan shanghai tamen de shihou, tamen shuo: Zhu nimen ping'an.
25|64|Tamen wei tamen de zhu er tongxiao koutou;
25|65|tamen chang shuo: Women de zhu a! Qiu ni wei women bi kai huo yu de xingfa. Huo yu de xingfa shi ling ren feichang tongku de,
25|66|que shi elie de zhuchu he jusuo.
25|67|Tamen yong qian de shihou, ji bu huihuo, you bu linse, jin shou zhong dao;
25|68|tamen zhi qidao zhenzhu, bu qidao bie de shenling; tamen bu weibei zhenzhu de jinling er sharen, chufei youyu changming; tamen ye bu tongjian. Shei fan ci lei (zui'e), shei zao chengfa;
25|69|fuhuo ri yao shou jiabei de xingfa, er shouru de yong ju qizhong.
25|70|Wei huiguo erqie xindao bingxingshangong zhe, zhenzhu jiang gouxiao qi zuixing, er luqu qi shangong. Zhenzhu shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
25|71|Huiguo erqie xing shan zhe, que yi zhuanxiang zhenzhu.
25|72|Tamen bu zuo jia jianzheng, tamen ting dao e yan de shihou qianxun de zou kai.
25|73|Youren yi tamen de zhu de jixiang quan jie tamen de shihou, tingjiang bing bu zhuang long zuo xia de dahan.
25|74|Tamen shuo: Women de zhu a! Qiu ni yi women de qi zi er nu wei women de anwei, qiu ni yi women wei jingwei zhe de dianfan.
25|75|Zhe deng ren neng jianren, yinci jiang shou gaoji de baochou, tamen zai leyuan li, jiang tingjian zhushou he zhu an.
25|76|Tamen jiang yong ju qizhong. Leyuan shi youmei de zhuchu he jusuo.
25|77|Ni shuo: Jiaruo meiyou nimen de qidao, wo de zhu bing bu guanqie nimen, dan nimen ji yi fouren zhenli, nimen jiangyao shou wufa jietuo de xingfa.

27|1|Ta, xin. Zhexie shi “gulanjing”--panbie zhen wei de jingdian--de jie wen,
27|2|shi xinzhe de xiangdao he jiayin.
27|3|Xindao zhe jin shou bai gong, wan na tian ke, duxin houshi.
27|4|Bu xin houshi zhe, wo que yi wei tamen er zhuangshile tamen de xingwei, gu tamen shi paihuai qitu de.
27|5|Zhe deng ren shi ying shou yanxing de, tamen zai houshi shi zui kui she de.
27|6|Ni que yi feng dao cong zhi rui quanzhi de zhu jiang shi de “gulanjing”.
27|7|Dangri, mu sa ceng dui ta de jiashu shuo: Wo que yi kanjian yi chu huoguang, wo jiang cong you huo di difang dai yige xiaoxi lai gei nimen, huo na yige huoba yi gei nimen kaohuo.
27|8|Ta daole nage huo de fujin, jiu you shengyin hanjiao ta shuo: Zai huo de fujin he sizhou de ren, dou meng fu you. Zansong zhenzhu--quan shijie de zhu, chaojue wanwu.
27|9|Mu sa a! Wo que shi zhenzhu--wanneng de, zhi rui de zhu.
27|10|Ni pao xia ni de shouzhang ba! Dang ta kanjian na tiao shouzhang wan yan ru she shi, jiu zhuanlian taobi, bu gan huigu. Mu sa a! Buyao weiju, shizhemen zai wo zheli, que shi bu weiju de.
27|11|Ji xing bu yi, ranhou gaiguo cong shan zhe chuwai, wo (duiyu ta) que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
27|12|Ni bashou charu ni de huai zhong, ranhou, chou chulai ta jiang bailiang liang de. Que wu eji. Zhe shi pai ni qu zhaoshi falao he ta de baixing de jiu zhong jixiang zhi yi. Tamen que shi youzui de minzhong.
27|13|Wo de xuduo mingxian jixiang jianglin tamen de shihou, tamen shuo: Zhe shi mingxian de moshu.
27|14|Tamen de neixin chengren naxie jixiang, dan tamen wei bu yi he aoman er fouren ta. Ni kan bainong shifei zhe de jieju shi zenyang de.
27|15|Wo que yi ba xuewen shangci da wu de he su lai man, ta lia shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Ta ceng shi women chaoyue ta de xuduo xindao de puren.
27|16|Su lai man jicheng da wu de; ta shuo: Zhongren a! Women ceng xuehui bai niao de yuyan, women ceng huode wanwu de xiangshou, zhe que shi mingxian de enhui.
27|17|Su lai man de dajun--you jingling, renlei, niao lei zucheng de--bei zhaoji dao ta mianqian, tamen shi bushu zhengqi de.
27|18|Dengdao tamen lai dao yi gu de shihou, yige mu yi shuo: Mayimen a! Kuai jin ziji de zhuchu qu, yimian bei su lai man he ta de dajun buzhi bu jue de jianta.
27|19|Su lai man wei ta dehua er chayi di weixiaole, ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni qishi wo, shi wo changchang ganxie ni suo ci wo he wo de fumu de enhui, bing shi wo changchang zuo ni suo xiyue de shangong qiu ni jie ni de enhui shi wo de ru ni de shanliang de puren zhi lie.
27|20|Ta ceng jianyue zhong niao, ta shuo: Wo zenme bujian dai sheng ne? Ta quexi ma?
27|21|Wo biding yanli de chengfa ta, huo sha diao ta, chufei ta dai yige mingzheng lai gei wo.
27|22|Ta douliu bujiu, jiu laile, ta shuo: Wo zhidaole ni bu zhidao de shi, wo cong sai bai yi dai laile yige queshi de xiaoxi gei ni.
27|23|Wo que yi faxian yige fu ren, tongzhi yizu ren, ta huode wanwu de xiangshou, ta you yige pangda de baozuo.
27|24|Wo faxian ta he ta de chenmin dou she zhenzhu er chongbai taiyang, emo ceng yi tamen de xingwei, mihuo tamen, yizhi zu'ai tamen zou shang zhengdao, suoyi tamen bu zunxun zhengdao.
27|25|Tamen bu chongbai zhenzhu--jieshi tiandi aomi, erqie shen zhi nimen suo yinhui he biaobai de zhu.
27|26|Zhenzhu, chu ta wai, jue wu ying shou chongbai zhe, ta shi weida de baozuo de zhu.(Ci chu koutou!)※
27|27|Ta shuo: Wo yao kan kan ni jiujing shi chengshi de, haishi shuohuang de.
27|28|Ni ba wo zhe feng xin dai qu tou gei tamen, ranhou, likai tamen, ni shikan tamen ruhe dafu.
27|29|Ta shuo: Chen pumen a! Wo jie dao yi feng guizhong de xin.
27|30|Zhe feng xin que shi su lai man ji lai de, zhe feng xin de neirong que shi'feng zhiren zhi ci de zhenzhu zhi ming.
27|31|Nimen buyao dui wo aoman wu li, nimen yingdang lai guishun wo.
27|32|Ta shuo: Chen pumen a! Guanyu wo de shi, wang nimen chu ge yijian. Wo conglai bu jueding renhe yi jian shi, zhidao nimen zai wo mianqian.
27|33|Tamen shuo: Women ji you wuli, you you yongqi. Women dui ni wei ming shi cong, qing ni xiang yi xiang, ni yao women zuo shenme.
27|34|Ta shuo: Guowangmen mei gong ru yige chengshi, bi pohuai qizhong de jianshe, bi shi qizhong guizu bian zai jianmin, tamen zhexie ren, ye hui zheyang zuo de.
27|35|Wo biding yao pai ren song liwu qu gei tamen, ranhou, dengdaizhuo kan shi chen dai hui shenme xiaoxi lai.
27|36|Dang shizhe daole su lai man de mianqian de shihou, ta shuo: Nimen zenme yi caichan lai zizhu wo ne? Zhenzhu suo ci wo de, shengguo ta suo ci nimen de. Buran, nimen wei nimen de liwu er yangyang deyi.
27|37|Ni zhuan huiqu ba, wo biding tongshuai tamen wufa dikang de jundui qu taofa tamen, wo biding ba tamen beijian de zhu chu jingwai shi tamen chengwei shou lingru de.
27|38|Ta shuo: Chen pumen a! Zai tamen lai guishun wo zhiqian, nimen zhong you shei neng ba ta de baozuo na lai gei wo ne?
27|39|Yige qiangliang de jingling shuo: Zai ni li xi zhiqian, wo ba ta na lai gei ni. Wo duiyu zhe jian shi que shi ji shengren, you zhongshi kekao de.
27|40|Na shen zhi tian jing de ren shuo: Zhuan shunjian wo jiu ba ta na lai gei ni. Dang ta kanjian nage baozuo anzhi zai ta mianqian de shihou ta shuo: Zhe shi wo de zhu de enhui zhi yi, ta yu yi ci shiyan wo, kan wo shi ganxie zhe haishi gufu zhe. Ganxie zhe, zhi wei ziji de liyi er ganxie; gufu zhe (xuzhi) wo de zhu que shi wu qiu de, que shi zun rong de.
27|41|Ta shuo: Nimen ba ta de baozuo gaizhuang yixia, yibian women kan ta neng fou renshi ziji de baozuo.
27|42|Dang ta lai dao de shihou, youren shuo: Ni de baozuo xiang zheyang ma? Ta shuo: Zhe hao xiang shi wo de baozuo. Zai ta zhiqian, women yi huode zhishi, women yi shi guishun de.
27|43|Ta she zhen zhu er chongbai de, fang'ai ta, ta ben shi shuyu bu xindao de minzhong.
27|44|Youren dui ta shuo: Ni jin na gongdian qu ba! Dang ta kanjian na zuo gongdian de shihou ta yiwei gongdian li shi yipian wangyang,(jiu tiqi yishang) luchu ta de liang tiao xiaotui. Ta shuo: Zhe que shi yong boli zaocheng de guanghua de gongdian. Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Wo que shi zi qi de, wo (xianzai) genzhe su lai man guishun zhenzhu--quan shijie de zhu.
27|45|Wo que yi paiqian sai mo de ren de xiongdi--sa li ha--qu jiaohua tamen (shuo): Nimen yingdang chongbai zhenzhu. Tamen like fen wei liang pai, huxiang zhenglun.
27|46|Ta shuo wo de zongzu a! Nimen weisheme zai enhui zhiqian yaoqiu xingfa zaori shixian ne nimen zenme bu xiang zhenzhu qiurao, yibian nimen meng zhu de lianmin ne?
27|47|Tamen shuo: Women wei ni he ni de xintu er zao eyun. Ta shuo: Nimen de eyun shi zhenzhu zhuding de. Buran, nimen shi yao shou kaoyan de.

27|50|Tamen ceng yong yige jimou, wo ye ceng yong yige jimou, dan tamen buzhi bu jue.
27|51|Ni kan tamen de jimou de jieju shi zenyang de.(Jieguo) shi wo ba tamen he tamen de zongzu, quanti huimiele.
27|52|Naxie shi tamen de fangwu, yin tamen de bu yi er bian wei tanta de. Duiyu you zhishi de minzhong ci zhong que you yige jixiang.
27|53|Wo ceng zhengjiule xindao erqie jingwei de renmen.

27|55|Nimen wubi yao she nuren er yi nanren manzu xingyu ma? Buran, nimen shi wu zhishi de minzhong.

27|58|Wo ceng jiang dayu qu shang tamen. Ceng shou jinggao zhe suo zao de yu zhen elie!
27|59|Ni shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu. Zhu ta suo xuan de zhong pu ping'an. Jiujing shi zhenzhu geng hao ne? Haishi tamen yong lai pei zhenzhu de geng hao ne?
27|60|Shi nei tiandi de chuangzao zhe (geng hao), ta wei nimen cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, yi peizhi meili de yuanpu, er nimen buneng shi yuanpu zhong de shumu shengzhang. Chu zhenzhu wai, nandao huan you ying shou chongbai de ma? Buran, tamen shi beimiu de minzhong.
27|61|Haishi yi dadi wei anju zhi suo, shi zhu heliu guan qijian, shi zhu shan zhenya qi shang, bing zai liang hai zhi jian she yige pingzhang zhe ne? Chu zhenzhu wai, nandao huan you ying shou chongbai de ma? Buran, tamen daban buzhidao.
27|62|Haishi na daying shounan zhe de qidao, er jiechu qi zaihai, qie yi nimen wei dadi de dai zhi zhe ne? Chu zhenzhu wai, nandao huan you ying shou chongbai de ma? Nimen hen shao juewu.
27|63|Haishi na zai lu hai de chongchong hei'an zhong yindao nimen, zai jiang qi enhui zhiqian, shi feng wei chuan jiayin zhe ne? Chu zhenzhu wai, nandao huan you ying shou chongbai de ma? Zhenzhu chao hu tamen yong lai pei ta de.
27|64|Haishi na chuangzao wanwu, ranhou jiayi fu zao, bing cong tianshang dixia gong nimen jiyang zhe ne? Chu zhenzhu wai, nandao huan you ying shou chongbai de ma? Ni shuo: Nimen na nimen de zhengju lai ba, ruguo nimen shi chengshi de.
27|65|Ni shuo: Chu zhenzhu wai, zai tiandi jian de, bu zhi youxuan, tamen bu zhidao shenme shihou fuhuo.
27|66|Nandao tamen guanyu houshi de zhishi yijing chengshule ma? Buran, tamen duiyu houshi shi huaiyi de. Buran, tamen duiyu houshi shi mangmu di.
27|67|Bu xindao de ren shuo: Nandao women he women de zuxian hai yao bei fuhuo qilai ma?
27|68|Women he women de zuxian, yiqian que yi tingguo zhe yi lei de konghe, zhege zhishi guren de shenhua.
27|69|Ni shuo: Nimen yingdang zai dimian shang luxing, yin'er guancha fanzui ren de jieju shi zenyang de.
27|70|Ni buyao wei tamen de (beini) er youchou, buyao wei tamen de jimou er fanmen.
27|71|Tamen shuo: Zhege jinggao shenme shihou shixian ne? Ruguo nimen shi chengshi de.
27|72|Ni shuo: Nimen yaoqiu zaori shixian de, huoxu you yibufen shi linjin nimen de.
27|73|Ni de zhu duiyu shiren, que shi you da en de, dan tamen daban shi bu ganxie de.
27|74|Ni de zhu, dique zhidao tamen de xiongzhong yinni de he tamen suo biaobai de.
27|75|Tianshang dixia, meiyou yi jian yin wei de shiwu, bu jilu zai yi ben mingbai de tian jing zhong.
27|76|Zhe bu “gulanjing”, dique ba yiselie de houyi suo zhenglun de da bufen de shili gaosu tamen.
27|77|Zhe bu “gulanjing” duiyu xindao zhe que shi xiangdao he enhui.
27|78|Ni de zhu, bi wei ta yizhao ta de jueding er caipan. Ta que shi wanneng de, que shi quanzhi de.
27|79|Ni yingdang xinlai zhen zhu, ni que shi ju you mingbai de zhenli de.
27|80|Ni biding buneng shi siren ting (ni jiang dao). Ni biding buneng shi tuibi de longzi ting ni zhaohuan.
27|81|Ni jue buneng yindao xiazi likai mi wu. Ni zhi neng shi xin wo de jixiang de ren, ting ni (jiang dao), tamen yin'er chengyi xindao.
27|82|Dang yuyan dui tamen shixian de shihou, wo jiang shi yi zhong dongwu cong di zhong chusheng, shanghai tamen, yinwei zhongren buxin wo de jixiang.
27|83|Zai na ri, wo jiang cong mei ge minzu zhong, jihe yiqun buxin wo de jixiang de ren, er tamen shi bei pailie de zheng zhengqi qi de.
27|84|Dengdao tamen lai dao (zhenzhu) nali de shihou, ta shuo: Nimen meiyou chedi zhidao wo de jixiang jiu jiayi fouren ma? Nimen jiujing zuole shenme ne?
27|85|Yuyan jiang dui tamen de bu yi er dui tamen shixian, suoyi tamen ya kou wu yan.
27|86|Nandao tamen buzhidao ma? Wo yi heiye zuo tamen de anxi shijian, yi baizhou zuo tamen guankan de shijian, duiyu xindao de minzhong qizhong que you xuduo jixiang.
27|87|Zai na ri, jiang chui haojiao, chu zhenzhu suo yiyu de wai, fan zai tianshang dixia de dou yao kongbu, ge ge dou yao beijian de lai dao zhenzhu nali.
27|88|Ni jian qun shan er yiwei dou shi guding de, qishi qun shan du xiang xing yun yang shiqu. Na shi jingzhi wanwu de zhenzhu dehuagong, ta que shi che zhi nimen de xingwei de.
27|89|Xingshan de ren jiang huode geng jia de baochou, zai na ri, tamen jiang de mian yu kongbu.
27|90|Zuo e de ren, jiang pufuzhe touru huo yu: Nimen zhi shou nimen de xingwei de baochou.
27|91|(Ni shuo): Wo zhi fengming chongbai zhe chengshi de zhu, ta ceng yi zhe chengshi wei jindi. Wanwu dou shi ta suoyou de. Wo yi fengming zuo yige guishun de ren,
27|92|bing xuandu “gulanjing”. Shei zunxun zhengdao, shei zi shou qi yi; shei wu ru qitu, ni dui shei shuo: Wo zhishi yige jinggao zhe.
27|93|Ni shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu, ta jiang xianshi gei nimen ta de jixiang, nimen jiu renshi ta. Ni de zhu, bing bu hushi nimen de xingwei.
28|1|Ta, xin, mi mu.
28|2|Zhexie shi mingbai de jingdian de jie wen.
28|3|Wo benzhe zhenli, wei xindao de minzhong er dui ni xushu mu sa he falao de shiji.
28|4|Falao que yi zai guo zhong aoman, ta ba guomin fencheng xuduo zongpai, er qifu qizhong de yipai ren; tusha tamen de nanhai, baoquan tamen de nuhai. Ta que shi shangfengbaisu de.
28|5|Wo yao ba endian shangci gei da dishang shou qifu de ren, wo yao yi tamen wei biaoshuai, wo yao yi tamen wei jicheng zhe,
28|6|wo yao shi tamen zai da dishang deshi, wo yao zhaoshi falao, ha man he tamen lia de jundui, duiyu zhexie bei qifu zhe de tifang de shi.
28|7|Wo ceng qishi mu sa de muqin (shuo): Ni yingdang buru ta, dang ni pa ta shouhai de shihou, ni ba ta tou zai he li, ni buyao weiju, buyao youchou, wo biding yao ba ta song hai ni, wo biding yao renming ta wei shizhe.
28|8|Falao de shicong ceng shiqule ta, yizhi ta chengwei tamen de diren he youhuan. Falao, ha man he ta lia de jundui, que shi cuowu de.
28|9|Falao de qizi shuo:(Zhe) shi wo he ni de weiji. Nimen buyao sha ta, yexu ta you liyu women, huozhe women ba ta shou wei yi zi.(Tamen tingcong ta de hua), tamen bu zhi bu jue.
28|10|Mu sa de muqin de xin, bian cheng kongxu de. Ruo bushi wo shi ta an xiaxin lai, yi shi ta chengwei xindao de ren, ta jihu baolu zhenqingle.
28|11|Ta dui ta de jiejie shuo: Ni zhuizhe ta qu ba. Ta jiu yuan yuan di kuice ta, tamen hao bu zhijue.
28|12|Yiqian, wo jinzhi ta chi renhe ren de nai, ta de jiejie jiu shuo: Wo jieshao nimen yijia ren, ti nimen yangyu ta, tamen shi zhongyu ta, hao ma?
28|13|Yushi, wo ba ta song hai ta de muqin, yibian ta huode wei ji, bu zai youchou, erqie zhidao zhenzhu de yingxu shi zhenshi de, dan tamen daban bu zhidao.
28|14|Dang ta tige qiangzhuang, zhili jianquan de shihou, wo shangci ta zhihui he xueshi. Wo yao zheyang baochou shanren.
28|15|Cheng cheng li de ren shuhu de shihou, ta zou jin cheng lai, bing zai cheng li faxianle liang geren zhengzai zhengdou, zhege shi shuyu ta de zongzu, nage shi shuyu ta de diren, shuyu tongzu de ren yaoqiu ta bangzhe duifu ta de diren, mu sa jiu ba na diren yi quan da si. Ta shuo: Zhe shi youyu emo de youhuo, emo que shi miren de ming di.
28|16|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Wo que yi zi qile, qiu ni raoshu wo ba. Zhen zhu jiu raoshule ta, ta que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
28|17|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Wo jie ni suo ci wo de endian er qiu ni baoyou wo, wo jue bu zuo fanzui zhe de zhushou.
28|18|Ci ri zaochen, ta zai cheng li zhanzhanjingjing de. Zuori xiang ta qiujiu di nageren huran you xiang ta gao sheng qiujiu. Mu sa dui ta shuo: Ni que shi mingxian de mi wu zhe.
28|19|Dang ta yu pu ji ta lia de diren de shihou, qiujiu di nage ren shuo: Mu sa a! Ni yao xiang zuori sharen yang sha wo ma? Ni zhi xiang zuo zhe difang de baonue zhe, que buxiang zuo tiaojie zhe.
28|20|Youyi ge ren, cong cheng de ji yuan chu mang lai shuo: Mu sa a! Chen pumen dique zhengzai shangyi yao sha ni, ni kuai chuzou ba. Wo que shi zhongyu ni de.
28|21|Ta jiu cong cheng li zhanzhanjingjing de tao chulaile, ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni shi wo tuo li bu yi de minzhong.
28|22|Dang ta yi quxiang mai de yan de shihou, ta shuo: Wo de zhu yexu zhishi wo zhengdao.
28|23|Dang ta lai dao mai de yan de quan bian de shihou, ta kanjian youyiqun ren zai nali yin yang, ta faxian chu tamen wai hai you liang nuzi, lanzhe tamen lia de yang qun. Ta shuo: Nimen lia weisheme zheyang ne? Ta lia shuo: Women yao dao mu renmen shi tamen de yang likai quanshui, cai de yin women de yang, women de fuqin shi yi wei long zhong de laoren.
28|24|Ta jiu ti ta lia yin yang, ranhou tui dao shu yin xia, ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Wo que xuqiu ni suo jiang gei wo de renhe fuli de.

28|28|Ta shuo: Zhe shi wo yu ni suo ding de hetong, wo wulun zuo man na yige qixian duiyu wo du buke you guofen de yaoqiu. Zhenzhu shi jiancha women de yue yan de.
28|29|Dang mu sa yi zuo man qixian, er daizhe ta de jiashu luxing de shihou, ta kanjian na zuo shan de zhe bian you yi chu huoguang, ta dui ta de jiashu shuo: Nimen dengdai yixia, wo que yi kanjian yi chu huoguang, yexu wo cong huoguang di nali dai yige xiaoxi lai gei nimen, huo dai yige huoba lai gei nimen kaohuo.
28|30|Ta yi lai dao nage huoguang de fujin, shangu de you'an shang, you conglin de jixiang chu, fachu husheng shuo: Mu sa a! Wo que shi zhenzhu--quan shijie de zhu,

29|3|Wo que yi kaoyan zai tamen zhiqian de ren. Zhenzhu biding yao zhidao shuo shihua zhe, biding yao zhidao shuohuang zhe.
