29|5|Fan xiwang huijian zhenzhu zhe, shei dou yingdang zhidao zhenzhu de qixian shi biding jianglin de, zhenzhu que shi quan cong de, que shi quanzhi de.
29|6|Fan fendou zhe, dou zhi wei ziji er fendou, zhenzhu que shi wu qiu yu quan shijie de.
29|7|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, wo biding gouxiao tamen de zui'e, wo biding yi tamen de xingwei de zui you de baochou shangci tamen.
29|8|Wo ceng ming ren xiaojing fumu; ruguo ta lia leling ni yong ni suo bu zhidao de dongxi pei wo, namo, ni buyao fucong ta lia. Nimen yao guiyu wo, wo yao ba nimen de xingwei gaosu nimen.
29|9|Xindao heng erqie xingshan zhe, wo biding shi tamen ru yu shanren zhi lie.
29|10|Youxie ren shuo: Women yi xin zhenzhule. Dang tamen wei zhenzhu er shou pohai de shihou, tamen ba zhongren de pohai dangzuo zhenzhu de xingfa. Ruguo yuanzhu cong nimen de zhu jianglin, tamen biding shuo: Women que shi yu nimen tong zai yiqi de. Nandao zhenzhu bushi zhidao shiren de xiongjin de ma?
29|11|Zhenzhu dique zhidao xindao zhe, dique zhidao wei xinzhe.
29|12|Bu xindao de ren dui xindao de ren shuo: Nimen zunshou women de jiao dao ba! Rang women danfu nimen de zuiguo. Qishi, tamen jue buneng danfu tamen de yidian zuiguo, tamen que shi shuohuang de.
29|13|Tamen biding danfu ziji de zhongdan, zai jia shang bie de zhongdan, fuhuo ri tamen duiyu ziji suo weizao de huangyan bi shoushen wen.
29|14|Wo que yi pai nu ha qu jiaohua ta de zongzu, ta zai tamen zhi jian, douliule jiubai wushi nian, hongshui jiu xijile tamen, yinwei tamen shi bu yi de.
29|15|Wo zhengjiule ta he yu ta tongchuan de ren, wo yi na wei quan shijie de yige jixiang.
29|16|(Wo que yi paiqian) yi bo la xin, dangri, ta dui ta de zongzu shuo: Nimen yingdang chongbai zhenzhu, bing dang jingwei ta, zhe duiyu nimen shi geng hao de. Ruguo nimen zhidao.
29|17|Chu zhenzhu wai, nimen zhi chongbai ouxiang, nimen zhi niezao wangyan. Nimen she zhenzhu er chongbai de (ouxiang), buneng zhuchi nimen de jiyang, suoyi, nimen yingdang dao zhenzhu nali xunqiu jiyang, nimen yingdang chongbai ta, nimen yingdang ganxie ta, nimen zhi bei zhao gui ta.
29|18|Ruguo nimen fouren (wo), namo, zai nimen zhiqian de xuduo minzu, ye fourenguo (tamen de shizhe). Shizhe de zeren zhishi mingbai di chuanda.
29|19|Nandao tamen meiyou kanjian zhenzhu zenyang chuangzao zhongsheng, ranhou shi tamen fuhuo ma? Zhe duiyu zhenzhu shi rongyi de.
29|20|Ni shuo: Nimen yingdang zai da dishang luxing, yin'er guancha zhenzhu zenyang chuangzao zhongsheng, you zenyang zaizao tamen. Zhen zhu duiyu wanshi que shi quanneng de.
29|21|Ta chengfa tasuo yiyu zhe, lianxu tasuo yiyu zhe, nimen zhi bei zhao guiyu ta.
29|22|Nimen wulun zai dishang huo tianshang, dou buneng taobi tianqian, chu zhenzhu wai, nimen meiyou renhe jianhu zhe, ye meiyou renhe yuanzhu zhe.
29|23|Buxin zhenzhu de jixiang ji yu zhenzhu huijian de, zhe deng ren, dui wo de enhui yi juewangle, zhe deng ren, jiang shou tongku de xingfa.
29|24|Ta de zongzu shuo: Nimen sha si ta, huo shao si ta ba! Zhe shi tamen weiyi de dafu. Zhenzhu zhengjiu ta tuoli liehuo, duiyu xindao de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
29|25|Ta shuo: Nimen she zhenzhu er yi ouxiang wei shenling, zhi wei jinshi shenghuo zhong huxiang qin'ai bale. Dan zai fuhuo ri, nimen jiang huxiang dilai, huxiang zuzhou, nimen de guisu shi huo yu, nimen jue meiyou yuanzhu zhe.
29|26|Lu te jiu wei ta er xindao. Yi bo la xin shuo: Wo biding qianyi dao wo de zhu nali qu, ta que shi wanneng de, que shi zhi rui de.
29|27|Wo shangci ta yi si ha ge he ye er gu bai, wo yi yuyan he tian jing shangci ta de houyi, wo ba ta zai jinshi de baochou shangci ta, zai houshi bi zai shanren zhi lie.
29|28|(Wo ceng paiqian) lu te, dangri, ta dui ta de zongzu shuo: Nimen dique gan choushi, zai nimen zhiqian, quan shijie de ren meiyouyige ganguo zhe zhong choushi de.
29|29|Nimen wubi yao jiang nan zuo nu, lanlu zuo'e, dangzhong xuan yin ma? Ta de zongzu shuo: Ni ba zhenzhu de xingfa zhaoshi women ba, ruguo ni shi chengshi de ren. Zhe shi tamen weiyi de dafu.
29|30|Ta shuo: Wo de zhu a! Qiu ni zhu wo, yi duikang shangfengbaisu de renmen.
29|31|Dang wo de shizhe daizhe jiayin laifang yi bo la xin de shihou, tamen shuo: Women biding huimie zhege chengshi de jumin. Zhege chengshi de jumin, que shi bu yi de.
29|32|Ta shuo: Lu te dique zai zhege chengshi li. Tamen shuo: Women zhidao zai zhege chengshi li de ren, women biding yao zhengjiu ta he ta de xintu, ta de qizi chuwai, ta shi he qiyu de ren tong shou xingfa de.
29|33|Dang wo de shizhe laifang lu te de shihou, ta wei tamen er youchou, ta wufa baohu tamen. Tamen shuo: Ni buyao haipa, buyao youchou, women biding zhengjiu ni he ni de xintu, ni de qizi chuwai, ta shi he qiyu de ren tong shou xingfa de.
29|34|Wo bi shi tianzai cong tiankong jiang yu zhege chengshi de jumin, na shi youyu tamen di fangdang.
29|35|Wo que yi wei neng liaojie de minzhong er jiang zhege chengshi de yizhi liuzhe zuo yige mingxian de jixiang.
29|36|(Wo ceng paiqian) shu a bo qu jiaohua mai de yan ren, ta jiu shuo: Wo de zongzu a! Nimen yingdang chongbai zhenzhu, yingdang weiju mori, buyao zai difang shang wei fei zuo dai, bainong shifei.
29|37|Dan tamen fouren ta, dizhen jiu xijile tamen. Qingke zhi jian, tamen dou jiang wo zai ge ren de jiazhong.
29|38|(Wo ceng huimie) a de ren he sai mo de ren, nimen cong tamen juzhu di difang, que yi mingbai tamen bei huimie de qingxing. Emo yi tamen de xingwei, mihuo tamen er zu'ai tamen zunxun zhengdao, tamen yuanlai shi neng siwei de.
29|39|(Wo ceng huimie) ge lun, falao he ha man. Mu sa ceng zhaoshi tamen xuduo mingzheng, dan tamen zai difang shang zi da, tamen wei neng taobi tianqian.
29|40|Mei yige ren, wo du yin ta de zuiguo er jiayi chengfa, tamen zhong you wo ceng shi feishazoushi de baofeng qu shanghai de, you wei kongbu suo xiji de, you wo shi ta lunxian zai dimian xia de, you bei wo ni sha de, zhenzhu buzhi kui wang tamen, dan tamen kui wangle ziji.
29|41|Youxie ren, she zhenzhu er bie qiu jianhu zhe, tamen piru zhizhu zao wu, zui cuiruo de fangwu, que shi zhizhu de fangwu. Jiaruo tamen renshi zhege daoli,(jiu bu hui chongbai ouxiangle).
29|42|Zhenzhu dique zhidao tamen she ta er qidao de renhe wu, ta shi wanneng de, shi zhi rui de.
29|43|Zhexie piyu, shi wo wei zhongren er she de, zhiyou xuezhe neng liaojie ta.
29|44|Zhenzhu ben zhenli er chuangzao tiandi, duiyu xindao de ren, ci zhong que you yi zhong jixiang.
29|45|Ni yingdang xuandu qishi ni de jingdian, ni dang jin shou bai gong, bai gong dique neng fangzhi choushi he zui'e, jinian zhenzhu que shi yi jian geng da de shi. Zhenzhu zhidao nimen de zuo wei.
29|46|Chu yi zui you de fangshi wai, nimen buyao yu xinfeng tian jing de ren bianlun, chufei tamen zhong bu yi de ren. Nimen yingdang shuo: Women quexin jiang shi women de jingdian, he jiang shi nimen de jingdian; women suo chongbai he nimen suo chongbai de shi tong yige shenming, women shi guishun ta de.
29|47|Wo zheyang ba jingdian jiang shi ni, meng wo shangci jingdian de ren, you quexin ta de. Zhe deng ren zhong, yeyou quexin ta de, zhiyou bu xindao de ren, fouren wo de jixiang.
29|48|Yiqian, ni bu hui dushu, ye bu hui xiezi,(jiaruo ni hui dushu xiezi), namo, fandui zhenli de ren biding huaiyi.
29|49|Buran, zhe shi wo de mingxian de jixiang, ta baocun zai xuezhe de xiongzhong, zhiyou bu yi de ren fouren wo de jixiang.
29|50|Tamen shuo: Zenme meiyou yi zhong jixiang cong ta de zhu jianglin ta ne? Ni shuo: Jixiang zhi zai zhenzhu nali, wo zhishi yige tanshuai de jinggao zhe.
29|51|Wo jiang shi ni zhe bu jingdian, keyi dui tamen changchang xuandu, nandao huan buneng shi tamen manyi ma? Zai zhe jingdian li duiyu xindao de ren que you enhui he jinian.
29|52|Ni shuo: Zhenzhu zuo wo he ni zhi jian de jianzheng yijing goule. Ta zhidao tiandi jian de yiqie, quexin xieshen er buxin zhenzhu zhe, que shi kui she de.
29|53|Tamen yaoqiu ni zaori zhaoshi xingfa, jiaruo meiyou dingqi, namo xingfa bi yi jianglin tamen. Dang tamen buzhi bu jue de shihou, xingfa biding huran jianglin tamen.
29|54|Tamen yaoqiu ni zaori zhaoshi xingfa. Huo yu biding shi baowei buxindao zhe de.
29|55|Zai na ri, xingfa jiang cong tamen de tou shang he jiaoxia jianglin tamen. Ta shuo: Nimen changshi nimen de xingwei de guobao ba!
29|56|Wo de xindao de purenmen a! Wo de dadi que shi kuanda de, nimen yingdang chongbai wo.
29|57|Mei yige you xi qi de, dou yao chang si de ziwei, ranhou, nimen jiang bei zhao guiyu wo.
29|58|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, wo bi shi tamen zai leyuan zhong de ju zaixia lin zhu he de lou shang, tamen jiang yong ju qizhong. Gongzuo zhe de baochou zhen hao!
29|59|Tamen shi jianren de, tamen zhi xintuo tamen de zhu.
29|60|Xuduo dongwu, buneng danfu ziji de jiyang, zhenzhu gongji tamen he nimen, ta shi quan cong de, shi quanzhi de.
29|61|Ruguo ni wen tamen: Shei chuangzaole tiandi, zhifule ri yue? Tamen biding shuo: Zhenzhu. Tamen shi ruhe huangmiu de!
29|62|Zhenzhuyao shi nage puren de jiyang kuanyu, jiu shi ta kuanyu,(yao shi nage pu ren de jiyang jiongpo,) jiu shi ta jiongpo, zhenzhu que shi quanzhi wanshi de.
29|63|Ruguo ni wen tamen: Shei cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui? Er jie yushui shi yi si de dadi fuhuo ne? Tamen biding shuo: Zhenzhu. Ni shuo: Yiqie zansong quan guizhenzhu! Buran, tamen daban shi bu liaojie de.
29|64|Zhe zhong jinshi de shenghuo, zhishi yule he youxi; houshi de zhuzhai, que shi chongman shenghuo de. Jiaruo tamen zhidao
29|65|dang tamen cheng chuan de shihou, tamen chengken de qidao zhenzhu, dang ta shi tamen ping'an denglu de shihou, tamen like jiu yi wu pei zhu.
29|66|Jiao tamen gufu wo shangci ba, jiao tamen xiangle ba. Tamen jianglai jiu zhidaole.
29|67|Nandao tamen meiyou zhidao ma? Wo ceng yi tamen de chengshi wei anning de jindi, er tamen sizhou de jumin bei ren jie lue. Nandao tamen quexin xieshen, er gufu zhenzhu de enhui ma?
29|68|Jiajie zhenzhu de mingyi er zaoyao, huo fouren yi jianglin de zhenli zhe, shei bi ta hai bu yi ne? Nandao huo yu li meiyou gu en zhe de zhuchu ma?
29|69|Wei wo er fendou de ren, wo biding zhiyin tamen wo de daolu, zhenzhu que shi yu shanren tong zai yiqi de.
30|1|Ai lie fu, lia mu, mi mu.
30|2|Luoma ren yi baibei yu
30|3|zuijin di difang. Tamen ji bai zhihou, jiang huo shengli,
30|4|yu shu nian zhi jian. Yiqian he yihou, fanshi guizhenzhu zhuchi. Zai na ri, xindao de ren jiangyao huanxi.
30|5|Zhe shi youyu zhenzhu de yuanzhu, ta yuanzhu tasuo yiyu zhe. Ta que shi wanneng de, que shi zhi ci de.
30|6|Zhenzhu yingxu (tamen shengli), zhenzhu bing bu shuangyue, dan renmen daban bu zhidao.
30|7|Tamen zhi zhidao jinshi shenghuo de biaomian, tamen duiyu houshi, shi shuhu de.
30|8|Nandao tamen meiyou siwei ma? Zhenzhu chuangzao tiandi wanwu, zhi yi zhenli he dingqi, you xuduo ren dique bu xin jiang yu tamen de zhu xiang hui.
30|9|Nandao tamen meiyou zai dadishang luxing er guancha qian ren de jieju shi zenyang de ma? Qian ren bi tamen nuli geng da, qian ren yu difang de ken zhi he jianshe, shengguo tamen. Tamen zu zhong de shizhe lailin tamen, zhenzhu buzhi kui wang tamen, dan tamen kui wangle ziji,
30|10|ranhou e bao nai zuo'e zhe de jieju, yinwei tamen fouren zhen zhu de jixiang, erqie jiayi chaoxiao.
30|11|Zhen zhu chuangzao zhongsheng, ranhou zaizao tamen, ranhou, nimen bei zhao guiyu ta.
30|12|Fuhuo shi lailin zhi ri, fanzui de ren, jiangcheng jusang de.
30|13|Tamen de pei zhu zhong, jianglai meiyou wei tamen shuo qing de, tamen jiang fouren tamen de pei zhu.
30|14|Fuhuo shi lailin zhi ri, tamen jiang bici fenli.
30|15|Zhiyu xindao erqie xingshan zhe, jiang zai yige shengdi, ganjue kuaile;
30|16|zhiyu bu xindao erqie fouren wo de jixiang, yiji houshi de xiang hui zhe, jiang bei jujin zai xingfa zhong.
30|17|Gu nimen zai wan xi he zaochen, yingdang zansong zhen zhu chaojue wanwu.
30|18|Tiandi jian de zansong, yiji bangwan de he zhongwu de zansong dou zhi guiyu ta.
30|19|Ta shi shengwu cong si wu zhong shengchu, shi si wu cong shengwu zhong shengchu, shi yi si de da di fuhuo, nimen ye yao ruci bei fuhuo.
30|20|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Ta yong nitu chuangzao nimen, ranhou, nimen like chengwei renlei, sanbu ge fang.
30|21|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Ta cong nimen de tonglei zhong wei nimen chuangzao pei'ou, yibian nimen yilian tamen, bingqie shi nimen huxiang ai yue, huxiang lianxu. Duiyu neng siwei de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
30|22|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Tiandi de chuangzao, yiji nimen de yuyan he fuse de chayi, duiyu you xuewen de ren, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
30|23|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Nimen zai heiye he baizhou shuimian bingqie xunqiu ta de enhui; duiyu hui tinghua de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
30|24|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Ta shi nimen yi kongbu he qitu de xinqing kan dianguang, ta cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, jie yushui shi yi si de dadi fuhuo, duiyu neng liaojie de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
30|25|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Tiandi yi ta de yizhi er jianding, dang ta dui changmian dixia de nimen jiaohuan yisheng de shihou, nimen like jiu chulaile.
30|26|Tiandi wanwu, zhishi ta de; yiqie dou fucong ta.
30|27|Ta chuangzao zhongsheng, ranhou zaizao tamen, zaizao duiyu ta shi rongyi de. Tiandi jian zuigao de dianxing, zhi shuyu ta, ta shi wanneng de, zhi rui de.
30|28|Ta wei nimen er jiu nimen zishen she yige piyu; nandao nimen zhunxu nimen de nubi yu nimen gongtong xiangshou wo shangci nimen de jiyang, er nimen yu tamen wanquan pingdeng, nimen weiju tamen, youru nimen huxiang weiju yiyang ma? Wo zheyang wei neng liaojie de minzhong jieshi wo de jixiang.
30|29|Buran, bu yi zhe, wuzhi di shuncong ziji de siyu. Zhenzhu suo wudao de ren, shei neng yindao ta ne? Tamen jue meiyou yuanzhu zhe.
30|30|Ni yingdang quxiang zhengjiao,(bing jin shou) zhenzhu suo fuyu ren de benxing. Zhenzhu suo chuangzao de, shi burong biangeng de; zhe cai shi zhengjiao, dan renmen bu ban bu zhidao.
30|31|Nimen yingdang guiyi zhenzhu, yingdang jingwei ta, yingdang jin shou bai gong, buyao zuo yi wu pei zhu zhe,
30|32|ji fenli ziji de zongjiao, er ge cheng zongpai zhe; ge pai dou xihuan ziji suo feng de zongpai.
30|33|Renmen zaonan de shihou, qidao tamen de zhu, tongshi guiyi ta. Dang ta shi tamen changshi ta de enhui de shihou, tamen zhong de yibufen ren, like yi wu pei zhu,
30|34|yizhi gufu ta de ci tamen de endian. Nimen xiangshou ba, nimen jianglai jiu zhidaole.
30|35|Nandao wo ceng jiang shi tamen yige mingzheng, mingling tamen yi wu pei zhu ma?
30|36|Dang wo shi renmen changshi enhui de shihou, tamen jiu wei na jian enhui er zhanzhanzixi; ruguo tamen yinwei cengjing fanzui er zaonan, tamen like jiu juewangle.
30|37|Nandao tamen bu zhidao ma? Zhenzhu yu shi shei de jiyang kuanyu, jiu shi ta kuanyu;(yu shi shei de jiyang jiongpo), jiu shi ta jiongpo. Duiyu xindao de minzhong, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
30|38|Ni yingdang ba jinqin, pinmin he luke suo ying xiang de quanli, jiao gei tamen, duiyu yao xiang huode zhenzhu de xiyue zhe, zhe shi geng hao de, zhe deng ren que shi chenggong de.
30|39|Nimen wei chi li er fang de zhai, yu zai taren de caichan zhong zengjia de, zai zhenzhu nali, bu hui zengjia; nimen suo shi de caiwu, yu de zhenzhu de xiyue de, bidei jiabei de baochou.
30|40|Zhenzhu chuangzao nimen, ranhou gongji nimen, ranhou shi nimen siwang, ranhou shi nimen fuhuo, nimen de pei zhu, shei neng zuo naxie shiqing zhong de renhe yi jian shiqing ne? Zansong zhenzhu, chaojue wanwu, ta chao hu tamen suoyong lai pei ta de.
30|41|Zaihai yin zhongren suo fan de zui'e er xianxian yu dalu he haiyang, yizhi zhenzhu shi tamen changshi ziji de xingwei de yidian baochou, yibian tamen huiwu.
30|42|Ni shuo: Nimen yingdang zai dadishang luxing, yin mian guancha qian ren de jieju shi zenyang de. Tamen daban shi yi wu pei zhu de.
30|43|Zai buke kangju de rizi cong zhenzhu lailin yiqian, ni yingdang quxiang zhengjiao, zai na ri, tamen jiang bici fenli.
30|44|Buxindao zhe, jiang zi shou qi bu xin de e bao, xingshan zhe zhi wei ziji yubei anzhai,
30|45|yibian zhenzhu yong ta de endian qu baochou xindao erqie xingshan zhe. Zhenzhu que shi bu xi'ai bu xindao zhe de.
30|46|Ta de yi zhong jixiang shi: Ta paiqian feng lai chuanda jiayin, shi nimen changshi ta de enhui, shi chuanbo feng ta de mingling er hangxing, yibian nimen xunqiu ta de enhui, yibian nimen ganxie.
30|47|Zai ni zhiqian, wo que yi paiqianle xuduo shizhe, qu jiaohua tamen de zongzu, naxie shizhe jiu zhaoshi tamen xuduo mingzheng, ranhou, wo chengzhi fanzui de ren. Yuanzhu xinshi, yuan shi wo de zeren.
30|48|Zhenzhu pai feng qu xingqi yun lai, ranhou renyi di shi yun sanbu zai tiankong, bingqie ba yun fencheng suipian, ni jiu kanjian yu cong yun zhong luoxia. Dang ta shi yu luo zai tasuo yiyu de puren shang de shihou, tamen like huanle,
30|49|jishi zai jiangyu zhiqian, tamen que shi jusang de.
30|50|Ni kan zhenzhu de enhui de xiaoguo ba! Ta zenyang shi yi si de da di fuhuo, na que shi neng qisihuisheng de. Ta duiyu wanshi shi quanneng de.
30|51|Ruguo wo shi yizhenfeng chui qu, er tamen kanjian hemiao bian cheng weihuang de, cihou, tamen jiu biding bian cheng gu en zhe.
30|52|Ni bi buneng shi siren ting (ni jiang dao), ni bi buneng shi tuibi de longzi ting ni huhuan.
30|53|Ni bi buneng yindao xiazi likai mi wu, ni zhi neng shi quexin wo de jixiang de renmen ting ni (jiang dao), tamen shi guishun zhe.
30|54|Zhenzhu cong nuoruo chuangzao nimen, zai nuoruo zhihou, you chuangzao qiangzhuang, zai qiangzhuang zhihou you chuangzao nuoruo he bai fa, ta yao chuangzao shenme, jiu chuangzao shenme. Ta que shi quanzhi de, que shi quanneng de.
30|55|Fuhuo shi jianglin zhi ri, fanzui de ren fa shi shuo tamen zhi douliule yi shashi, tamen yuan shi zheyang beimiu de.
30|56|You xuewen he xinde zhe shuo: Yi zhenzhu de qian ding, nimen que yi douliu dao fuhuo ri. Zhe jiushi fuhuo ri, dan nimen bu zhidao.
30|57|Zai na ri, bu yi zhe de bian ci, wu bi yu zishen, tamen ye bude yao en.
30|58|Zai zhe “gulanjing” zhong, wo que yi wei zhongren shele ge zhong piyu. Ruguo ni zhaoshi tamen yi zhong jixiang, namo, buxindao zhe biding shuo: Nimen zhishi huangdan de!
30|59|Zhenzhu zheyang fengbi wuzhishi zhe de xin.
30|60|Ni jianren ba, zhenzhu de yingxu que shi zhenshi de. Ni buyao rang bu jianxin de ren shi ni qingshuai.
31|1|Ai lie fu, lia mu, mi mu.
31|2|Zhexie shi you zhihui de jingdian de jie wen,
31|3|shi xingshan zhe de de xiangdao he enhui.
31|4|Xingshan zhe, jin shou bai gong, wan na tian ke, qie quexin houshi.
31|5|Zhe deng ren, shi zunshou tamen de zhu de zhengdao de, zhe deng ren que shi chenggong de.
31|6|Youren goumai wuwei de tanhua, yibian ta wu zhi wu shi di shi ren beili zhenzhu de zhengdao, erqie ba ta dang zuo xiaobing. Zhe deng ren, jiang shou lingru de xingfa.
31|7|Youren dui ta xuandu wo de jixiang de shihou, ta zi dadi tuibi, fangfu meiyou tingjian yiyang, fangfu ta de liang er zhong ting yiyang. Ni yi tongku de xingfa, xiang ta baoxi ba.
31|8|Xindao erqie xingshan zhe, bi jiang xiangshou ji leyuan,
31|9|er yong ju qizhong. Zhe shi zhenzhu de zhenshi de yingxu, ta que shi wanneng de, que shi zhi rui de.
31|10|Ta chuangzao zhu tian, er buyong nimen suo neng jian de zhizhu; ta zai dadishang anzhi xuduo shanyue, yimian da di dongyao, shi nimen bu'an; ta zai da dishang sanbu ge zhong dongwu. Ta cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, er zai da dishang zisheng ge zhong youliang de zhiwu.
31|11|Zhe shi zhenzhu suo chuangzao de, nimen zhishi wo ba. Nimen she zhenzhu er chongbai de (ouxiang) jiujing chuangzaole shenme ne? Buran, bu yi de ren shi zai mingxian de mi wu zhong de.
31|12|Wo que yi ba zhihui shangci lu ge man,(wo shuo): Ni dang ganxie zhenzhu. Ganxie de ren, zhi wei ziji er ganxie, gufu de ren, xuzhi zhenzhu que shi wu qiu de, que shi ke song de.
31|13|Dangri, lu ge man ceng jiaoxun ta de erzi shuo: Wo de xiaozi a! Ni buyao yi renhe wu pei zhu. Yi wu pei zhu, que shi danibudao de.
31|14|Wo ceng ming ren xiaojing fumu--ta muqin ruo shang jia ruo de huaizhe ta, ta de duan ru shi zai liang nian zhi zhong--wo shuo: Ni yingdang ganxie wo he ni de fumu; wei wo shi zuihou de guisu.
31|15|Ruguo ta lia leling ni yi ni suo bu zhidao de dongxi pei wo, name, ni buyao fucong ta lia, zai jinshi, ni yingdang yi li yi er feng shi ta lia, ni yingdang zunshou guiyi wo zhe de daolu; wei wo shi nimen de guisu, wo yao ba nimen de xingwei gaosu nimen.
31|16|Lu ge man shuo: Wo de xiaozi a! Shan e de xingwei, sui xiao ru jiezi, yincang zai panshi li, huo zai tiankong zhong, huo zai di dixia, zhenzhu dou yao xianshi ta. Zhenzhu que shi mingcha de, que shi che zhi de.
31|17|Wo de xiaozi a! Ni yingdang jin shou bai gong, yingdang quan shan jie e, yingdang renshou huannan, zhe que shi yinggai juexin zuo de shiqing.
31|18|Ni buyao wei miaoshi zhongren er zhuanlian, buyao yangyang deyi di zai da dishang xingzou. Zhenzhu que shi bu xi'ai yiqie aoman zhe, jinkua cai de.
31|19|Ni yingdang jiezhi ni de bufa, ni yingdang yizhi ni de shengyin; zui taoyan de shengyin, que shi luzi de shengyin.
31|20|Nandao nimen bu zhidao ma? Zhenzhu ceng wei nimen zhifu tiandi jian de yiqie, ta bo shi nimen biao li de enhui. Youren zhenglun zhenzhu de de xing, dan tamen ji wu zhishi, you wu xiangdao, qie wu canlan de jingdian.
31|21|Ruguo youren dui tamen shuo: Nimen yingdang zunshou zhenzhu suo jiang shi de (jingdian). Tamen jiu shuo: Buran, women zunshou women zuxian de yijiao. Jishi emo jiao tamen qu shou liehuo de xingfa,(tamen reng yao zunxun) ma?
31|22|Chengxin guishun zhenzhu erqie changxing shanshi zhe, que yi bawo zhu jiangu de babing. Wanshi de jieju, zhi guizhenzhu.
31|23|Bu xindao zhe, ni buyao wei tamen de bu xin er youchou, tamen zhi guiyu wo, wo yao ba tamen de xingwei gaosu tamen. Zhenzhu que shi quanzhi tamen de xionghuai de.
31|24|Wo shi tamen shaoshao xiangshou xingfu, ranhou, qiangpo tamen qu shou yanli de xingfa.
31|25|Ruguo ni wen tamen: Shei chuangzaole tiandi? Tamen biding shuo: Zhenzhu. Ni shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Buran, tamen daban bu zhidao.
31|26|Tiandi wanwu zhishi zhenzhu de, zhenzhu que shi wu qiu de, que shi ke song de.
31|27|Jiaruo yong da dishang suoyou de shu lai zhi cheng bi, yong haishui zuo mozhi, zai jia shang qihai de mozhi, zhong buneng xie jin zhenzhu de yanyu. Zhenzhu que shi wanneng de, que shi zhi rui de.
31|28|Chuangzao nimen he fuhuo nimen, zhi xiang chuangzao yige ren he fuhuo yige ren yiyang. Zhenzhu que shi quan cong de, que shi quan ming de.
31|29|Nandao ni bu zhidao ma? Zhen zhu shi heiye qinru baizhou, shi baizhou qinru heiye, bing zhifu ri yue, gezi yunxing, zhi yi dingqi. Zhen zhu shi che zhi nimen de xingwei de.
31|30|Na shi yin wei zhenzhu que shi zhenshi de; tamen she ta er qidao de, que shi xuwei de; zhenzhu que shi zhizun de, que shi zhi da de.
31|31|Nandao ni bu zhidao ma? Chuanbo zai haizhong daizhe zhenzhu de enhui er hangxing, yibian ta zhishi nimen ta de yibufen jixiang, duiyu mei ge jianren de, ganxie de ren, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
31|32|Dang shanyue ban de botao longzhao tamen de shihou, tamen qiancheng de qidao zhenzhu, dang ta shi tamen ping'an denglu de shihou, tamen zhong you zhong he de ren; zhiyou mei ge jiaohua de, gu en de ren, fouren wo de jixiang.
31|33|Renmen a! Nimen yingdang jingwei nimen de zhu, nimen yingdang weiju na yi ri, fuqin duiyu erzi hao wu biyi, erzi duiyu fuqin ye hao wu biyi. Zhenzhu de yingxu, que shi zhenshi de. Jue buyao rang jinshi de shenghuo qipian nimen, jue buyao rang hua zei yi zhenzhu de rongren qipian nimen.
31|34|Zai zhenzhu nali, dique you guanyu fuhuo shi de zhishi, ta chang jiang jishiyu, ta zhidao tai'er de (xingbie); er renhe ren dou bu zhidao ziji mingri jiang zuo shenme shi, renhe ren dou bu zhidao ziji jiang si zai shenme difang. Zhenzhu que shi quanzhi de, que shi che zhi de.
32|1|Ai lie fu, lia mu, mi mu.
32|2|(Zhe) shi cong quan shijie de zhu jiang shi de jingdian, qizhong hao wuyi yi.
32|3|Tamen shuo: Ta niezao ta ma? Buran! Ta shi cong ni de zhu jiang shi de zhenli, yibian ni jinggao zai ni zhiqian meiyou renhe jinggao zhe lailinguo de yiqun minzhong, yibian tamen zunxun zhengdao.
32|4|Zhenzhu ceng zai liu rinei chuangzao tiandi wanwu, ranhou, sheng shang baozuo, chu ta wai, nimen meiyou renhe jianhu zhe he shuo qing zhe. Nimen zenme bu jinian ne?
32|5|Ta zhili zi tian zhi di de shiwu, ranhou na shiwu zai yi ri zhi nei shangsheng dao ta nali, na yi ri de changdu, shi nimen suo jisuan de yiqian nian.
32|6|Na shi quanzhi youming de, wanneng de, zhi ci de zhu.
32|7|Ta jingzhi tasuo chuangzao de wanwu, ta zuichu yong nitu chuangzao ren.
32|8|Ranhou yong jian shui de jinghua chuangzao ta de zisun.
32|9|Ranhou shi ta jianquan, bing jiang ta de jingshen chui zai ta de shenti zhong, you wei nimen chuangzao ermu xinling. Nimen hen shao ganxie.
32|10|Tamen shuo: Women xiaoshi zai dixia zhihou, nandao women biding chongxin shou zao ma? Buran! Tamen buxin jiang yu tamen de zhu xiang hui.
32|11|Ni shuo: Fengming zhuguan nimen de shengming de sishen, jiang shi nimen siwang, ranhou nimen jiang bei zhao guiyu nimen de zhu.
32|12|Jiaruo ni de jian fanzui zhe zai tamen de zhu nali chuitousangqi de shuo: Women de zhu a! Women yijing kanjianle, tingjianle, qiu ni rang women zhuan huiqu, women jiang zuo shanshi, women que shi quexin zhe. Jiaruo ni kanjian zhe zhong qingzhuang.
32|13|Jiaruo wo yiyu, bi yi xiangdao fuyu mei geren, dan cong wo fachu de panci yi quedingle, wo bi yi jingling he renlei yiqi tian man huo yu.
32|14|Nimen changshi ba! Yinwei nimen wangji jinri de xiang hui, wo que yi wangji nimenle. Nimen yinwei ziji de xingwei er changshi yongjiu de xingfa ba.
32|15|Xinyang wo de jixiang de, zhiyou na deng ren; bieren yi wo de jixiang quan jie tamen de shihou, tamen bian fufu koutou bing zansong tamen di na chaojue wanwu de zhu, tamen bu gan wangzizunda,(ci chu koutou!)※
32|16|Tamen le bu luo chuang, tamen yi kongju he xiwang de xinqing qidao tamen de zhu; tamen fen she wo suo ciyu tamen de.
32|17|Renhe ren dou bu zhidao yi wei tamen zhucangle shenme weiji, yi baochou tamen de xingwei.
32|18|Xindao zhe yu beini zhe yiyang ma? Tamen shi bu xiangdeng de.
32|19|Zhiyu xindao erqie xingshan zhe, jianglai deyi leyuan wei guisu, na shi weile baochou tamen de xingwei de.
32|20|Zhiyu beini zhe, tamen de guisu, zhishi huo yu, mei dang tamen yao xiang tao chu, dou bei lan huiqu. You shengyin dui tamen shuo: Nimen changshi yiqian nimen suo fouren de huoxing ba!
32|21|Zai zuida de xingfa zhiqian, wo bi shi tamen changshi zuijin de xingfa, yibian tamen huiwu.
32|22|Youren yi zhu de jixiang quan jie ta, er ta bu ken tingcong, zheyang de ren, shei bi ta hai bu yi ne? Wo biran yao chengzhi fanzui de ren.
32|23|Wo que yi ba jingdian shangci mu sa, suoyi nimen duiyu jieshou jingdian, buyao xianyu youyu zhong, wo ceng yi na bu jingdian wei yiselie houyi de xiangdao.
32|24|Wo ceng yi tamen zhong de yibufen renwei biaoshuai, dang tamen renshou jiannan, quexin wo de jixiang de shihou, feng wo de mingling qu yindao zhongren.
32|25|Fuhuo ri, ni de zhu biding panjue tamen suo zhenglun de shifei.
32|26|Nandao tamen hai bu xiaode ma? Zai tamen zhiqian, wo ceng huimiele xuduo shidai, tamen changchang jingguo naxie ren de guxiang, zai nali que you xuduo jixiang. Tamen zenme bu tingcong ne?
32|27|Tamen hai bu zhidao ma? Wo ba yushui gan dao wu cao di difang, er jie ta shengchu tamen de shengchu he tamen ziji suo shi de zhuangjia. Nandao tamen kan bujian ma?
32|28|Tamen shuo: Zhe zhong panjue shenme shihou shixian ne? Ruguo nimen shi shuo shihua de.
32|29|Ni shuo: Bu xindao zhe, zai panjue ri, sui xin wuyi, bingqie bu huode kuandai.
32|30|Ni yingdang bi kai tamen, ni yingdang dengdai, tamen biding shi dengdai de.
33|1|Xianzhi a! Ni yingdang jingwei zhenzhu, ni buyao shuncong buxinzhe he wei xinzhe, zhenzhu que shi quanzhi de, que shi zhi rui de.
33|2|Ni yingdang zunxun cong ni de zhu jiang shi ni de (jingdian), zhenzhu que shi che zhi nimen de xingwei de.
33|3|Ni yingdang xintuo zhenzhu, zhenzhu zu wei jianhu zhe.
33|4|Zhenzhu meiyou zai renhe ren de xiongtang li chuangzao liang ge xin. Nimen de qizi, nimen ba tamen de jibei dangzuo ziji de muqin de jibei--zhenzhu meiyou ba tamen dangzuo nimen de muqin, ye meiyou ba nimen de yi zi dang zuo nimen de erzi. Zhe shi nimen xinkoukaihe dehua. Zhenzhu shi shuoming zhenli de, shi zhishi zhengdao de.
33|5|Nimen yingdang yi tamen de fuqin de xingshi chenghu tamen, zai zhenzhu kan lai, zhe shi geng gongping de. Ruguo nimen bu zhidao tamen de fuqin shi shei, namo, tamen shi nimen de jiao bao he qinyou. Nimen suo wu fan de shi, duiyu nimen meiyou zuiguo, nimen suo gu fan de shi, jiu buranle. Zhenzhu shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
33|6|Xianzhi dui xinshi di quanli, zhong yu tamen zishen de quanli, ta de zhong qi, shi tamen de muqin. Xueqin yu xueqin xianghu jian de quanli, yi zhenzhu de jingdian, shi zhong yu xinshi he qian shi di quanli de, chufei nimen dui ziji de qinyou xingshan. Zhe shi jilu zai tian jing li de.
33|7|Dangri, wo yu zhong xianzhi ding yue, yu ni he nu ha, yi bo la xin, mu sa, mai er yan zhizi er sa ding yue, wo yu tamen ding zhuangyan de mengyue,
33|8|yibian zhenzhu xiang chengshi zhe xunwen tamen de chengshi. Ta yiwei bu xindao zhe yubeile tongku de xingfa.
33|9|Xindao de renmen a! Nimen yingdang jiyi zhenzhu suo ci nimen de endian. Dangshi, di jun lai gong nimen, wo jiu dui tamen paiqian baofeng he nimen suo wei jian de tianbing. Zhenzhu shi mingcha nimen de xingwei de.
33|10|Dangshi, tamen cong nimen de shangmian he nimen de xiamian lai gong nimen; dangshi, nimen yanhua xintiao, bing dui zhenzhu zuo zhongzhong caice.
33|11|Zai na shi, xinshimen ceng shoudao kaoyan, bing shou julie de zhendong.
33|12|Dangshi, wei xinzhe he xinzhong you bing de ren dou shuo: Zhenzhu ji qi shizhe, zhi xuwei di ying xu women.
33|13|Dangshi, tamen zhong de yipai ren shuo: Ye si li bo ren a, nimen bubi zai zheli douliule. Nimen hui jia qu ba! Tamen zhong de yipai ren, xiang xianzhi gaojia shuo: Women de fangwu, que shi polan de. Qishi tamen de fangwu bing bushi polan de, tamen yao xiang taozou.
33|14|Jiaruo zhe zuo chengshi bei diren simian gongpo, erhou di jun yaoqiu tamen pan jiao, tamen biding chengnuo. Tamen yin ci shi zhi dan yan pianke.
33|15|Yiqian tamen yu zhenzhu que yi yueding, tamen jue bu zhuan bei. Zhenzhu de mengyue, shi yinggai fuze luxing de.
33|16|Ni shuo: Ruguo nimen taobi siwang, huo shalu, namo, taobi duiyu nimen jue wu biyi. Nimen jishi taobi, ye zhi dedao shaoshao xiangshou.
33|17|Ni shuo: Ruguo zhenzhu yu jiang huo yu nimen, shei neng fankang zhenzhu er baohu nimen ne? Ruguo ta yu jiang fu yu nimen,(shei neng ganshe ta) ne? Chu zhenzhu wai, tamen buneng faxian renhe jianhu zhe he renhe yuanzhu zhe.
33|18|Zhenzhu zhidao nimen zhong youxie ren zu'ai bieren, bingqie dui tamen de tongbao shuo: Nimen dao women zhe bian lai ba! Tamen zhi ou'er canzhan.
33|19|Tamen dui nimen shi linse de. Dang kongbu jianglin de shihou, ni jian tamen wangzhe ni, tamen de yanjing zhuandong de xiang hun si de ren yiyang; dang kongbu xiaoshi de shihou, tamen que yi jianli de koushe tong ma nimen, er tamen dui qiancai shi linse de. Zhe deng ren, meiyou xindao, gu zhenzhu jieshi tamen de xingwei de xuwei, zhe duiyu zhenzhu shi rongyi de.
33|20|Tamen yi wei tongmeng jun hai meiyou chetui, ruguo tongmeng jun juantuchonglai, tamen jiang xiwang ziji zai shamo zhong de youmu de alabo ren zhongjian, bing cong nali tanting nimen de xiaoxi, jiaruo tamen yu nimen xiangchu, tamen zhi ou'er canjia zhandou.
33|21|Xiwang zhenzhu he mori, bingqie duoduo jinian zhenzhu zhe, nimen you shizhe keyi zuo nimen de youliang mofan.
33|22|Dang xinshi jian tongmeng jun de shihou, tamen shuo: Zhe shi zhenzhu ji qi shizhe suo yingxu women de, zhenzhu ji qi shizhe shuo duile. Zhe jian shi zhi neng shi tamen gengjia quexin, gengjia shuncong.
33|23|Xinshi zhong you xuduo ren, yi shijian tamen yu zhenzhu suo ding de mengyue: Tamen zhong you chengren de, youdai yi de, tamen meiyou bianjie.
33|24|Yibian zhenzhuyin chengshi zhe de chengshi er shan bao tamen, bingqie suiyi di chengfa wei xin zhe, huo she you tamen. Zhenzhu que shi zhi she de, que shi zhi ci de.
33|25|Zhenzhu shi bu xindao zhe mo neng huosheng, fenfen er gui; zhenzhu shi xinshi bu zhan er sheng. Zhenzhu shi zhi gang de, shi wanneng de.
33|26|Ta ceng shi bangzhu tamen di naxie xinfeng tian jing zhe, cong ziji de baolei shang xialai, bingqie ba kongbu tou zai tamen xinli, nimen shalu yibufen, fulu yibufen.
33|27|Ta shi nimen jicheng tamen de tudi, fangwu, caichan he nimen shangwei taguo de tudi. Zhen zhu duiyu wanshi shi quanneng de.
33|28|Xianzhi a! Ni dui ni de zhong qi shuo: Ruguo nimen yu de jinshi de shenghuo yuqi zhuangshi, namo, nimen lai ba! Wo jiang yi li yi kuizeng nimen, wo ren nimen yi li er li qu.
33|29|Ruguo nimen yu de zhenzhu ji qi shizhe de xiyue, yu houshi de anzhai, namo zhenzhu que yi wei nimen zhong de xingshan zhe, yubeile zhongda de baochou.
33|30|Xianzhi de qizimen a! Nimen zhong shei zuole mingxian de choushi zhe, jiang shou jiabei de xingfa, zhe shi duiyu zhenzhu shi rongyi de.
33|31|Nimen zhong shei fucong zhenzhu ji qi shizhe, erqie xingshan, wo jiang jiabei baochou shei, wo yi wei ta yubeile youhou de jiyang.
33|32|Xianzhi de qizimen a! Nimen bu xiang bie de renhe funu, ruguo nimen jingwei zhenzhu, jiu buyao shuo wenrou dehua, yimian xinzhong you bing de ren, tanlian nimen; nimen yingdang shuo zhuangzhong dehua.
33|33|Nimen yingdang anju yu nimen de jiazhong, nimen buyao xuan lu nimen di meili, ru congqian mengmei shidai de funu nayang. Nimen yingdang jin shou bai gong, wan na tian ke, shuncong zhenzhu ji qi shizhe. Xianzhi de jiashu a! Zhenzhu zhi yu xiaochu nimen de wuhui, xi jing nimen de zui'e.
33|34|Nimen yingdang jin ji zai nimen jiazhong suo xuandu de zhenzhu de jixiang he geyan, zhenzhu shi xuanmiao de, shi che zhi de.
33|35|Shunfu de nannu, xindao de nannu, fucong de nannu, chengshi de nannu, jianren de nannu, gongjing de nannu, hao shi de nannu, zhaijie de nannu, baoshou zhencao de nannu, chang nian zhenzhu de nannu, zhenzhu yi wei tamen yubeile she youhe zhongda de baochou.
33|36|Dangzhenzhu ji qi shizhe panjue yi jian shi de shihou, xindao de nannu duiyu tamen de shi, buyi you xuanze. Shei weikang zhenzhu ji qi shizhe, shei yi xianru xianzhu de mi wule.
33|37|Dangshi, ni dui na zhenzhu ceng shi yi enhui, ni ye ceng shi yi enhui de ren shuo: Ni yingdang wanliu ni de qizi, ni yingdang jingwei zhenzhu. Ni ba zhenzhu suo yu zhaoshi de, yincang zai ni de xinzhong, zhenzhu shi geng yingdang wei ni suo weiju de, ni que weiju zhongren. Dang zai de li jue ta de shihou, wo yi ta wei ni de qizi, yimian xinshimen wei tamen de yi zi suo li jue de qizi er ganjue fannan. Zhenzhu de mingling, shi bixu fengxing de.
33|38|Xianzhi duiyu zhenzhu suo xu ta de shi, buyi ganjue fannan. Zhenzhu ceng yi ci wei guren de changdao. Zhenzhu de mingling shi buke biangeng de ding'an.
33|39|Xianzhimen shi chuanda zhenzhu de shiming de, tamen weiju ta, chu zhenzhu wai, tamen bu weiju renhe ren. Zhenzhu zu wei jiancha zhe.
33|40|Muhanmode bushi nimen zhong renhe nanren de fuqin, er shi zhenzhu de shizhe, he zhong xianzhi de fengyin. Zhenzhu shi quanzhi wanwu de.
33|41|Xinshimen a! Nimen yingdang changchang jinian zhenzhu,
33|42|nimen yingdang zhaoxi zansong ta chaojue wanwu.
33|43|Ta lianmin nimen, ta de tianshenmen wei nimen qidao, yibian ta jiang nimen cong chongchong hei'an yinru guangming, ta shi lianmin xinshi di.
33|44|Tamen yu zhenzhu huijian di neitian, zhenzhu dui tamen de zhuci shi: Zhu nimen ping'an. Ta yi wei tamen yubeile youhou de baochou.
33|45|Xianzhi a! Wo que yi paiqian ni wei jianzheng, wei baoxi zhe, wei jinggao zhe,
33|46|wei feng zhenzhu zhi ming zhao ren yu zhenzhu zhe, wei canlan de mingdeng.
33|47|Ni yingdang xiang xinshimen baoxi, tamen jiang huode zhenzhu jiangxia de hong en.
33|48|Ni buyao shuncong buxinzhe he wei xin zhe, ni yingdang ren sui tamen ruma, ni yingdang xinren zhenzhu, zhenzhu zu wei jianhu zhe.
33|49|Xindao de renmen a! Nimen ruo qu xindao de funu, ranhou zai jiaojie qian xiule tamen, namo, tamen bu gai wei nimen er shou xianqi, suoyi nimen yingdang shi ta xiangshou, yingdang rang tamen yi li er li qu.
33|50|Xianzhi a! Wo que yi zhun ni xiangshou ni jiyu pinli de qizi, ni de nubi, ji zhenzhu yiwei ni de zhanlipin de, ni de cong fu de nu'er. Ni de gumu de nu'er. Ni de jiufu de nu'er. Ni de yimu de nu'er. Tamen shi tong ni yidao qianju de. Xindao de funu, ruo jiang zishen zengyu xianzhi, ruo xianzhi yuanyi qu ta, zhe shi texu ni de, xinshimen bude yuanli--wo zhidao wo wei tamen de qizi yu nubi er dui tamen zuo chu de guiding--yimian ni ganshou kunnan. Zhenzhu shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
33|51|Ni keyi renyi di li jue tamen zhong de renhe ren, ye keyi renyi di wanliu tamen zhong de renhe ren. Ni suo zan li de qizi, ni xiang zhaohui ta, duiyu ni shi hao wu zuiguo de. Na shi zuijin yu shi tamen gandao anwei er wu bei'ai di, bingqie dou manyi ni suo jiyu tamen de. Zhenzhu zhidao nimen de xinshi, zhenzhu shi quanzhi de, shi zhi rui de.
33|52|Yihou bu zhun ni zai qu funu, ye bu zhun ni yi tamen huan diao bie de qizi, jishi ni xianmu tamen di meimao, chufei shi ni de nubi. Zhen zhu shi jianshi wanwu de.
33|53|Xinshimen a! Nimen buyao jin xianzhi de jia, chufei yaoqing nimen qu chifan de shihou; nimen buyao jinqu deng fan shu, dang qing ni qu de shihou cai jinqu; ji chi zhihou jiu dang gaotui, buyao liulian xianhua, yinwei na hui shi xianzhi gandao weinan, ta bu haoyisi citui nimen. Zhenzhu shi bu chi yu jieshi zhenli de. Nimen xiang xianzhi de qizimen suoqu renhe wupin de shihou, yingdang zai weimu wai suoqu, na duiyu nimen de xin he tamen de xin shi geng qingbai de. Nimen buyi shi shizhe weinan, zai ta zhihou, yong buyi qu ta de qizi, yinwei zai zhenzhu kan lai, na shi yi jian dazui.
33|54|Ruguo nimen yao biaobai shenme, huo yinni shenme,(zhenzhu zong shi zhidao de), yin wei zhenzhu que shi quanzhi wanwu de.
33|55|Tamen wufang huijian tamen de fuqin, erzi, dixiong, zhizi, waisheng, xindao de funu, he ziji de nubi. Nimen yingdang jingwei zhenzhu, zhenzhu que shi jianzheng wanwu de.
33|56|Zhenzhu dique lianmin xianzhi, ta de tianshenmen dique wei ta zhufu. Xinshimen a! Nimen yingdang wei ta zhufu, yingdang zhu ta ping'an!
33|57|Feibang zhenzhu he shizhe de ren, zhenzhu zai jinshi he houshi bi qi jue tamen, bing wei tamen yubei lingru de xingfa.
33|58|Yi xinshimen hexin numen suo wei fan de zui'e feibang tamen zhe, que yi danfu wumie he mingxian de zui'e.
33|59|Xianzhi a! Ni yingdang dui ni de qizi, ni de nu'er he xinshimen de funu shuo: Tamen yingdang yong waiyi mengzhe ziji de shenti. Zheyang zuo zui rongyi shi ren renshi tamen, er bu shou qinfan. Zhenzhu shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
33|60|Wei xin de, xinzhong you bing de, zai chengzhong shanhuo renxin de, ruguo tamen reng bu baxiu, wo bi ming ni zhicai tamen, tamen jiu bude jiuju chengzhong yu ni wei linle.
33|61|Tamen jiang bei qi jue, wulun tamen zai nali pi fa xian, jiu zai nali bei daibu, er bei chusi.
33|62|Zhe shi zhenzhu duiyu guren de changdao, ni jue buneng faxian renhe biangeng.
33|63|Zhongren wen ni fuhuo shi zai shenme shihou? Ni shuo: Na zhiyou zhenzhu cai zhidao. Shenme shi ni zhidao ta he shi fasheng ne? Fuhuo shi, huoxu shi hen jin de.
33|64|Zhenzhu que yi qi jue buxindao zhe, bing wei tamen yubei liehuo.
33|65|Tamen jiang yong ju qizhong, buneng dedao renhe baohu zhe, ye buneng dedao renhe yuanzhu zhe.
33|66|Tamen de mianpi zai huo zhong bei fanzhuan zhi ri, tamen jiang shuo: Dan yuan women ceng fucong zhenzhu, fucong shizhe!
33|67|Tamen shuo: Women de zhu a! Women que yi fucong women de lingxiu he women de weiren, shi tamen shi women weibei zhengdao.
33|68|Women de zhu a! Qiu ni yong jiabei de xingfa chuzhi tamen, qiu ni yanli de qi jue tamen.
33|69|Xinshimen a! Nimen buyao fangxiao yuan wu mu sa de renmen. Zhenzhu yi wei ta xi xueyuan wu, ju zhenzhu kan lai, ta shi you mianzi de.
33|70|Xinshimen a! Nimen yingdang jingwei zhenzhu, yingdang shuo zheng hua.
33|71|Ta jiu gaishan nimen de xingwei, jiu she you nimen de zuiguo. Fucong zhenzhu ji qi shizhe de ren, que yi huode weida de chenggong.
33|72|Wo que yi jiang zhongren xintuo tiandi he shanyue, dan tamen bu ken chengdan ta, tamen weiju ta, er ren que chengdanle--ren que shi bu yi de, que shi wuzhi de,
33|73|yizhi zhenzhu chengfa wei xin de nannu he yi wu pei zhu de nannu, er she you xindao de nannu! Zhenzhu shi zhi she de, shi zhi ci de.
34|1|Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Tiandi wanwu, dou shi ta de. Houshi de zansong, zhi guiyu ta. Ta shi zhi rui de, shi che zhi de.
34|2|Ta zhidao qianru dixia de, cong dixia fachu de, cong tianshang jiangxia de, sheng dao tianshang de. Ta shi zhi ci de, shi zhi she de.
34|3|Bu xindao de renmen shuo: Fuhuo shi bu hui lailin women. Ni shuo: Buran. Zhi wo de zhu fashi, ta bi lailin nimen. Wo de zhu shi quanzhi youxuan de, tiandi jian wei chen zhong de zhong wu, buneng yuanli ta; bi na geng xiao de, he geng da de, wu yi jian bu jilu zai yi ben mingbai de jingdian zhong.
34|4|Yibian ta zai fuhuo shi baochou xindao er xingshan de renmen. Zhe deng ren, jiang huo she youhe youhou de jiyang.
34|5|Jieli fandui wo de jixiang yiwei yijing chenggong de ren, jiang shou tongku de xingfa.
34|6|You xueshi de renmen, zhidao cong ni de zhu jiang shi ni de jingdian, que shi zhenli, neng zhishi (shiren zou shang) wanneng de, ke song de zhu de dadao.
34|7|Bu xindao de renmen shuo: Women zhishi nimen yige ren hao ma? Ta hui gaosu nimen, dang nimen bei fensui zhihou, nimen biding yao bei zaizao.
34|8|Ta jiajie zhen zhu de mingyi er niezao ne? Haishi ta you feng bing? Buran! Bu xin houshi de renmen shi zai xingfa he shen shen de mi wu zhong.
34|9|Nandao tamen meiyou guancha zai tamen shangmian he xiamian de tiandi ma? Ruguo wo yiyu, wo bi shi tamen lunxian zai dimian xia, huo shi tian yikuai yikuai di luo zai tamen de tou shang. Duiyu mei yige guiyi de puren, ci zhong que youyi zhong jixiang.
34|10|Wo que yi shangci da wu de cong wo fachu de enhui. Qun shan a! Zhong niao a! Nimen yingdang hezhe ta zansong, wo wei ta shi tie rouruan,
34|11|Wo dui ta shuo: Ni yingdang zhizao wanshan de kaijia, ni yingdang dinghao kaijia de kuandu. Nimen ying dang xingshan, wo que shi mingcha nimen de xingwei de.
34|12|Wo ceng shi feng gong su lai man de qushi, feng zai shangwu zou yi yue de lucheng, zai xiawu ye zou yi yue de lucheng. Wo wei ta shi rong tong xiang quanshui yang yong chu. Youxie jingling feng zhu de mingling zai ta de mianqian gongzuo; shei weibeile wo de mingling, wo jiu shi shei changshi liehuo de xingfa.
34|13|Tamen wei ta xiujian tasuo yu xiujian de gongdian, diaoxiang, shuichi ban de dapan, guding de da guo.(Wo shuo): Da wu de de jiashu a! Nimen yingdang ganxie. Wo de puren zhong, ganxie zhe shi hen shao de.
34|14|Wo jueding ta siwang de shihou, zhiyou chi ta de shouzhang de zhu chong, zhishi tamen ta yijing sile. Dang ta dao xia de shihou, jinglingmen huangrandawu: Jiaruo tamen neng zhi youxuan, namo, tamen weiceng douliu zai lingru de xingfa zhong.
34|15|Sai bo yi zu, zai tamen de ju chu, que youyi zhong jixiang: Liang ge yuanpu, fen lie zuoyou. Nimen keyi chi nimen de zhu de jiyang, nimen yao ganxie ta. Yige feimei di difang, yige zhi she de zhuzai.
34|16|Suihou, tamen beini, suoyi wo shi shuiku de jiliu qu yanmo tamen, wo ba tamen de liang ge yuanpu, bian cheng liang ge zhi shengzhang kuguo, chengliu, he xiewei de suanzao shu de yuanpu.
34|17|Wo yin tamen de wang'en er yi zhe baochou tamen, wo zhi chengfa wang'en de ren.
34|18|Wo zai tamen yu wo suo fu you di naxie chengshi zhi jian, jianshele xuduo xianzhu de chengshi, wo jun fen ge zhan jian de juli. Nimen zai qijian ping'an di luxing ruogan zhouye ba!
34|19|Ranhou, tamen shuo: Women de zhu a! Qiu ni fang zhang ge zhan zhi jian de juli. Tamen zi qi, suoyi wo yi tamen wei tan zhu. Wo shi tamen liulishisuo. Duiyu mei ge duo ren duoxie de ren, ci zhong que you xuduo jixiang.
34|20|Yi bo lie si que yi faxian ta dui tamen de caice shi zhengque de, yinwei tamen dou zhuisui ta; zhiyou yi huo xinshi chuwai.
34|21|Ta dui tamen suoyi you quanli zhe, zhi wei wo yao bianbie shei shi xinyang houshi de, shei shi huaiyi houshi de. Ni de zhu, shi wanwu de jianhu zhe.
34|22|Ni shuo: Nimen she zhenzhu er ren zuo shenling de, nimen qidao tamen ba: Tamen buneng guanli tiandi jian wei chen zhi zhong de shiwu, tamen sihao buneng canyu tiandi de zaohua. Zhenzhu bu yi tamen zhong de renhe yige wei zhushou.
34|23|Chu zhenzhu suo xuke zhe wai, zai zhenzhu nali, shuo qing jiang wu biyi. Zhidao tamen xinzhong de kongju bei paichu de shihou, tamen cai shuo: Nimen de zhu shuole shenme? Tamen shuo: Zhenli. Ta que shi zhizun de, que shi zhi da de.
34|24|Ni shuo: Shei cong tianshang he dixia gongji nimen? Ni shuo: Zhenzhu. Women huo nimen, shi zai zhengdao shang de, huo shi zai xianzhu de mi wu zhong de.
34|25|Ni shuo: Duiyu women suo fan de zui, nimen bu shoushen wen; duiyu nimen suo zuo de shi, women ye bu shoushen wen.
34|26|Ni shuo: Women de zhu, jiang zhaoji women, ranhou, yi zhenli er wei women caipan, ta que shi zui shanyu caipan de, que shi quanzhi de.
34|27|Ni shuo: Nimen gaosu wo, nimen suo cheng wei ta de huoban de. Jue buneng de. Buran, ta shi zhenzhu, shi wanneng de, shi zhi rui de.
34|28|Wo zhi paiqian ni wei quan renlei de baoxi zhe he jinggao zhe, dan shiren daban bu zhidao.
34|29|Tamen shuo: Ruguo ni shi shuo shihua de, zhege jinggao shenme shihou shixian ne?
34|30|Ni shuo: Nimen de yue qi shi you shi ri de, nimen bude shaoshao chidao, ye bude shaoshao zao dao.
34|31|Buxindao de renmen shuo: Women jue buxin zhe “gulanjing”, ye buxin yiqian de jingdian. Jiaruo ni de jian bu yi de renmen bei juliu zai tamen de zhu nali de shihou, tamen huxiang bianbo, bei qifu de renmen jiang dui jiao'ao de renmen shuo: Jiaruo meiyou nimen, women biding shi xindao de.
34|32|Jiao'ao de renmen jiang dui bei qifu de renmen shuo: Dang zhengdao lailin nimen de shihou, women ceng fang'ai nimen zunxun zhengdao ma? Buran, nimen ziyuan zuo fanzui.
34|33|Bei qifu de renmen jiang dui jiao'ao de renmen shuo: Buran! Zhe shi nimen zhouye de jimou. Dangshi, nimen jiao women buxin zhenzhu, que wei ta shuli xuduo pidi. Dang tamen kanjian xingfa de shihou, tamen biaoshi huihen. Wo yao fan jiasuo fang zai zai xindao zhe de bozi shang, tamen zhi shou tamen de xingwei de baochou.
34|34|Mei feng wo paiqian jinggao zhe dao yige chengshi qu, qizhong haohua de renmen zong shi shuo: Women dique bu xin ni de shiming.
34|35|Tamen shuo: Wo ren caichan geng fu, er zi geng duo, wo ren jianglai jue bu zhen shou chengfa.
34|36|Ni shuo: Wo de zhu yu shi shei de jiyang kuanyu, jiu shi ta kuanyu; yu shi shei de jiyang jiongpo, jiu shi ta jiongpo. Dan zhongren daban bu zhidao.
34|37|Nimen de caichan, nimen de erzi, dou buneng shi nimen shaoshao de qinjin wo; dan xindao erqie xingshan de renmen, jiang yin tamen de xingwei er shou jiabei de baochou, tamen jiang anju yu lou shang.
34|38|Jieli fandui wo de jixiang de renmen, jiang bei jujin zai xingfa zhong.
34|39|Ni shuo: Wo de zhu, dique yu shi nage puren de jiyang kuanyu, jiu shi ta kuanyu; yu shi nage puren de jiyang jiongpo, jiu shi ta jiongpo. Nimen suo shishe de dongxi, ta jiang buchang ta; ta shi zui you de gongji zhe.
34|40|Zai na ri, ta yao jiang tamen tongtong jihe qilai, ranhou dui tianshenmen shuo: Zhexie ren chongbaiguo nimen ma?
34|41|Tamen shuo: Women zansong ni chaojue wanwu! Ni shi women de zhu, tamen bushi women de nupu. Tamen que shi chongbai jingling de, tamen daban xinyang jingling.
34|42|Jinri, tamen buneng huli, ye buneng xiang hai; wo jiang dui bu yi de renmen shuo: Nimen changshi nimen suo fouren de huoxing ba!
34|43|Youren dui tamen xuandu wo de mingbai de jixiang shi, tamen shuo: Zhege ren zhi xiang fang'ai nimen chongbai nimen de zuxian suo chongbai de ouxiang. Tamen you shuo: Zhe zhishi niezao de huangyan. Dang zhenli lailin de shihou, bu xindao de renmen shuo: Zhe zhishi yi zhong mingxian de moshu.
34|44|Wo meiyou ba tamen de neng song xi de renhe jingdian shangci tamen, zai ni zhiqian, wo meiyou paiqian renhe jinggao zhe qu jiaohua tamen.
34|45|Zai tamen zhiqian shiqu de renmen ceng fouren zhenli, tamen meiyou dadao wo suo ciyu qian ren de shi fen zhi yi, dan qian ren fouren wo de shizhemen, wo de qianze shi zenyang de?
34|46|Ni shuo: Wo zhi yi yi jian shi quandao nimen, nimen yingdang wei zhenzhu er shuangshuang de huo dandu de zhan qilai, ranhou siwei. Nimen de tongxiang, jue wu feng bing. Zai yanli de xingfa lailin zhiqian, ta dui nimen zhishi yige jinggao zhe.
34|47|Ni shuo: Wo bu xiang nimen suoqu shenme baochou, ta quan gui nimen; wo de baochou, zhi guizhenzhu fudan. Ta shi jianzheng wanwu de.
34|48|Ni shuo: Wo de zhu, yi zhenli sheji xuwei, ta shi quanzhi youxuan de.
34|49|Ni shuo: Zhenli yi lailinliao, xuwei jiang huanmie, er bu fuchu.
34|50|Ni shuo: Ruguo wo wu ru qitu, ze wo zi shou qi hai; ruguo wo zunxun zhengdao, ze youyu wo de zhu suo qishi de jingdian. Ta que shi quan cong de, que shi linjin de.
34|51|Jiaruo ni de jian dangshi tamen kongbu er wu chu taobi, zai yige bu yuan di difang bei daibu.
34|52|Tamen jiang shuo: Women yi xinyang tale. Tamen zen neng cong yaoyuan di difang huode xinyang ne?
34|53|Tamen yiqian bu xinyang ta, tamen cong yaoyuan di difang wang tan youxuan,
34|54|tamen jiang yin zhang'ai er buneng huode tamen suo yuwang de. Youru tamen de tonglei yiqian shou zhang'ai yiyang, tamen que zai fannao de yilu zhong.
35|1|Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu--tiandi de chuangzao zhe! Ta shi mei ge tianshen juyou liangyi, huo san yi, huo si yi. Ta zai chuangzao zhong zengjia tasuo yu zengjia de. Zhenzhu duiyu wanshi que shi quanneng de.
35|2|Wulun zhenzhu shangci nimen shenme enhui, jue wu ren neng jiayi zulan; wulun ta kouliu shenme enhui, zai jin shi zhihou, jue wu ren neng jiayi kaishi. Ta que shi wanneng de, que shi zhi rui de.
35|3|Renmen a! Nimen yingdang mingji zhenzhu suo ci nimen de enhui, chu zhenzhu wai, hai you she me chuangzao zhe neng cong tianshang dixia gongji nimen ma? Chu ta wai, jue wu ying shou chongbai de, nimen zenme ruci beimiu ne?
35|4|Ruguo tamen fouren ni, zai ni zhiqian de shizhemen, yi bei fourenle. Wanshi zhi guizhenzhu.
35|5|Renmen a! Zhenzhu de yingxu, que shi zhenshi de, suoyi jue buyao rang jinshi de shenghuo qipian nimen, jue buyao rang hua zei yi zhenzhu de yourong qipian nimen.
35|6|Emo que shi nimen de choudi, suoyi nimen yingdang ren ta wei choudi. Ta zhi haozhao ta de dangyu, yibian tamen zuo liehuo de jumin.
35|7|Bu xindao zhe, jiang shou yanli de xingfa; xindao erqie xingshan zhe, jiang meng she youhe zhongda de baochou.
35|8|Wei ziji de e xing suo mihuo, yin'er ren e wei shan zhe, xiang zhenzhu suoyindao de ren ma? Zhenzhu bi shi tasuo yiyu zhe wu ru mitu, bi shi tasuo yiyu zhe zunxun zhengdao, suo yi ni buyao wei aidao tamen er sangsheng, zhenzhu que shi quanzhi tamen de xingwei de.
35|9|Zhen zhu shi feng qu xingqi yun lai, ranhou, ba yun gan zhi yige yi si di difang, er jie ta shi yi si de dadi fuhuo. Siren de fuhuo jiushi zheyang de.
35|10|Yu de guangrong zhe, xuzhi guangrong quan guizhen zhu. Liangyan jiang wei tasuo zhi, ta sheng qi shanxing. Tumoubugui zhe, jiang shou yanli de xingfa; zhexie ren de tumou, shi buneng decheng de.
35|11|Zhen zhu chuangzao nimen, xian yong nitu, ji yong jingye, ranhou, shi nimen chengwei pei'ou. Renhe nuren de huaiyun he fenmian, wu yi jian bushi ta suo zhidao de; zengjia chang ming zhe de shou shu, jianshao duanming zhe de nianling, wu yi jian bu jilu zai tian jing zhong; na dui zhen zhu shi rongyi de.
35|12|Liang hai bu yiyang, zhe hai shi hen tian de, kekou de danshui, na hai shi hen ku de xian shui. Nimen ke chi mei yi haizhong suo chan de xinxian de rou, you ke cai nimen suo dai de shoushi. Ni kan chuanbo zai haishang polang er xing, yibian nimen xunqiu ta de enhui, yibian nimen ganxie ta.
35|13|Ta shi heiye qinru baizhou, shi baizhou qinru heiye; ta zhifu ri yue, gezi yunxing zhi yi dingqi. Zhe shi zhenzhu--nimen de zhu, guotu zhishi ta de, nimen she ta er qidao de, buneng guanli yi sihao.
35|14|Ruguo nimen qidao tamen, tamen ting bujian nimen de qidao; jibian tingjianle, tamen ye buneng daying nimen; fuhuo ri, tamen jiang fouren nimen ceng yi tamen pei zhenzhu. Renhe ren buneng xiang che zhi zhe nayang gaosu ni.
35|15|Renmen a! Nimen cai shi xuqiu zhenzhu de, zhenzhu que shi wu qiu de, que shi ke song de.
35|16|Ruguo ta yiyu, ta jiang huimie nimen, er chuangzao xin de zhongsheng.
35|17|Na dui zhenzhu bushi fannan de.
35|18|Yige fu zui zhe, bu zai fu bieren de zui; yige fuzhong zui zhe, ruguo jiao bieren lai ti ta fu zui, namo, bieren sui shi ta de jinqin, ye buneng ti ta danfu yi sihao. Ni zhi neng jinggao zai mimi zhong jingwei zhu, qie jin shou bai gong zhe. Xidi shenxin zhe, zhi wei ziji er xidi. Zhenzhu shi weiyi de guisu.
35|19|Mangren he fei mangren bu xiangdeng,
35|20|hei'an yu guangming ye bu xiangdeng,
35|21|beiyin he dang yang ye bu xiangdeng,
35|22|huo ren he siren ye bu xiangdeng. Zhenzhu bi shi ta de yiyu zhe neng tingwen, ni jue buneng shi zai fen zhong de ren neng tingwen,
35|23|ni zhishi yige jinggao zhe.
35|24|Wo que yi shi ni ben zhenli er wei baoxi zhe he jinggao zhe. Meiyou yige minzu ze yi, zhiyao you yige minzu, qizhong jiu you jinggao zhe cengjing shiqule.
35|25|Ruguo tamen fouren ni, namo, zai tamen zhiqian shiqu zhe, yi fourenle; tamen zu zhong de shizhe ceng zhaoshi tamen mingzheng, tian jing he canlan de jingdian.
35|26|Ranhou, wo cheng fa liao buxindao zhe, wo de qianze shi zenyang de?
35|27|Nandao ni hai bu zhidao ma? Zhenzhu cong yun zhong jiangxia yushui, ranhou jie yushui er shengchan ge zhong guoshi. Shanshang you bai de, hong de, gese de tiaowen, he qihei de yanshi.
35|28|Renlei, yeshou he shengchu zhong, ye tongyang di you butong de zhonglei. Zhenzhu de puren zhong, zhiyou xuezhe jingwei ta. Zhenzhu que shi wanneng de, que shi zhi she de.
35|29|Songdu zhenzhu de jingdian, qie jin shou bai gong, bing mimi de huo gongkai di fen she wo suo ciyu tamen de caiwu zhe, tamen xiwang zhe jingying bu pochan,
35|30|yibian ta shi tamen xiangshou ziji de wanquan de baochou, bing ba ta de enhui jia ci tamen; ta que shi zhi she de, que shi shan bao de.
35|31|Wo suo qishi ni de, que shi zhenli, zu zheng yiqian de jingdian shi zhenshi de. Zhenzhu duiyu ta de pu renmen que shi che zhi de, que shi mingcha de.
35|32|Ranhou, wo shi wo suo jianxuan de pu renmen jicheng jingdian; tamen zhong you zi qi de, you zhong he, you feng zhenzhu de mingling er zhengxian xingshan de. Na que shi hong en.
35|33|Changzhu de leyuan, tamen jiang ru qizhong, tamen zai limian, dai de shi jin zhuo he zhenzhu, chuan de shi sichou.
35|34|Tamen shuo: Yiqie zansong, quan guizhenzhu! Ta quchu women de youchou. Women de zhu, que shi zhi she de, que shi shan bao de.
35|35|Ta shi women juzhu zai changzhu de fangwu zhong, na shi chu yu ta de enhui. Women zai limian, hao bu xinku, hao bu pijuan.
35|36|Buxindao zhe, jiang zao huo yu de huoxing, ji bu pan tamen sixing, rang tamen siwang; you bu jianqing tamen suo zao de huoxing. Wo zheyang baochou yiqie wang'en de renmen.
35|37|Tamen zai limian qiujiu shuo: Women de zhu a! Qiu ni fang women chuqu, women jiang gaiguo qian shan. Nandao wo meiyou yanchang nimen de shou shu, shi neng juewu zhe you juewu de shijian ma? Jinggao zhe yi jianglin nimenle. Nimen changshi xingfa ba, bu yi zhe jue meiyou renhe yuanzhu zhe.
35|38|Zhenzhu que shi quanzhi tiandi de youxuan de, ta que shi quanzhi xinshi de.
35|39|Ta shi nimen wei dadishang de dai zhi zhe. Buxindao zhe zi shou qi bu xin de baochou; bu xindao zhe de bu xin, zhi shi tamen zai tamen de zhu na shou tonghen; bu xindao zhe de bu xin, zhi shi tamen geng meng kui she.
35|40|Ni shuo: Nimen gaosu wo ba, nimen she zhenzhu er qidao di naxie pei zhu, zenme ying shou chongbai ne? Nimen gaosu wo ba! Tamen ceng duzi chuangzaole da di de na yibufen ne? Haishi tamen ceng yu zhenzhu gongtong chuangzao zhu tian ne? Haishi zhenzhu ceng shouyu tamen yi ben jingdian, er tamen shi yiju na ben jingdian zhong de xuduo mingzheng ne? Buran, bu yi zhe jin yi qipian huxiang ying xu.
35|41|Zhenzhu dique weichi tiandi, yimian huimie; ruguo tiandi yao huimie, ze chu zhenzhu wai, renhe ren buneng weichi ta. Ta que shi zhi rong de, que shi zhi she de.
35|42|Tamen zhi zhenzhu er fachu de zui yanzhong de shiyan shuo: Ruguo you yige jinggao zhe lailin women, namo, women zunxun zhengdao bi shenguo renhe yige minzu. Dang jinggao zhe lailin tamen de shihou, tamen que gengjia beimiu,
35|43|zai difang shang gengjia zi da, gengjia tumoubugui. Yinmou zhi kun qi chuangzao zhe, tamen chule dengdai guren suo zaoshou de changdao wai, hai neng dengdai shenme ne? Duiyu zhenzhu de changdao, ni jue buneng faxian renhe biangeng; duiyu zhen zhu de changdao, ni jue buneng faxian renhe bianqian.
35|44|Nandao tamen meiyou zai dadishang luxing, yi guancha qian ren de jieju shi zenyang de ma? Qian ren bi tamen shili geng da. Zhenzhu shi tiandi jian renhe wu buneng shi ta wunai de, ta que shi quanzhi de, que shi quanneng de.
35|45|Jiaruo zhenzhu wei shiren suo fan de zui'e er chengzhi tamen, namo, ta bu liu yigeren zai dimian shang, dan ta rang tamen yanchi dao yige dingqi, dang tamen de dingqi lailin de shihou,(ta jiang yi tamen de xingwei er baochou tamen), yin wei zhenzhu que shi mingcha ta de zhong pu de.
36|1|Ya xin.
36|2|Yi zhihui de “gulanjing” fashi,
36|3|ni que shi zhong shizhe zhi yi,
36|4|ni dique shi zai zheng lushang bei paiqian de shizhe zhi yi.
36|5|Wanneng zhi ci de zhenzhu jiang shi ci jing.
36|6|Yibian ni jinggao yizu ren, tamen de zuxian wei bei jinggaoguo, suoyi tamen shi shuhu dayi de.
36|7|Tamen zhong da duoshu ren que yi yingdang shou panjue, suoyi tamen bu xindao.
36|8|Wo que yi ba jiasuo fang zai tamen de bozi shang, naxie jiasuo dadao xiaba, suoyi tamen buneng ditou.
36|9|Wo zai tamen de qianmian anzhi yige zhang'ai, zai tamen de houmian anzhi yige zhang'ai, mengbile tamen, suoyi tamen kan bujian.
36|10|Ni dui tamen jiayi jinggao yu fou, zhe zai tamen shi yiyang de, tamen bijing bu xindao.
36|11|Ni zhi neng jinggao na zunshou jiaohui, erqie zai mimi zhong jingwei zhiren zhu zhe, ni yao yi she youhe youhou de baochou xiang ta baoxi.
36|12|Wo biding yao shi siren fuhuo, wo biding yao jilu tamen suozuo de shan e, he tamen de shiji; wo jiang yiqie shiwu, xiangming di jilu zai yi ce mingbai de fanben zhong.
36|13|Ni dang yi chengshi de jumin wei tamen she yige piyu. Dangshi, shizhemen lailin naxie jumin.
36|14|Dangshi, wo ceng paiqian liang ge shizhe qu jiaohua naxie jumin, dan tamen fouren tamen lia de shiming, wo jiu yi di san ge shizhe qu yuanzhu tamen lia. Tamen shuo: Women que shi bei paiqian lai jiaohua nimen de.
36|15|Tamen shuo: Nimen zhishi xiang women yiyang de fanren. Zhiren zhu meiyou jiang shi renhe wu, nimen zhishi shuohuang de.
36|16|Tamen shuo: Women de zhu zhidao, women que shi bei paiqian lai jiaohua nimen de,
36|17|women zhi fu mingbai de chuanda de zeren.
36|18|Tamen shuo: Women que yi wei nimen er zao eyun, ruguo nimen bu tingzhi xuanchuan, women shi bi ruma nimen, huo yi tongku de xingfa jia yu nimen.
36|19|Tamen shuo: Nimen de eyun shi bansuizhe nimen de. Nandao youren jiaohui nimen,(nimen cai wei ta er zao eyun ma?) Buran! Nimen shi guofen de minzhong.
36|20|Youyige ren cong chengzhong zui yuan di difang pao lai shuo: Wo de zongzu ya! Nimen yingdang shuncong shizhemen,
36|21|nimen yingdang shuncong naxie zunxun zhengdao, er bu xiang nimen suoqu baochou de renmen.
36|22|(You shuo): Wo zen neng bu chongbai na chuangzaole wo, er nimen jiang bei zhao guiyu ta de zhuzai ne?
36|23|Nandao wo neng she ta er jing shi yixie shenling ma? Ruguo zhiren zhu yu jiang zai yu wo, ze tamen de shuo qing, duiyu wo hao wu biyi, tamen ye buneng zhengjiu wo.
36|24|Ruguo nayang, wo que shi zai mingxian de mi wu zhong.
36|25|Wo que yi gui xin nimen de zhu, gu nimen yingdang tingcong wo.
36|26|You shengyin dui ta shuo: Ni ru leyuan ba! Ta shuo: Dan yuan wo de zongzu zhidao,
36|27|wo de zhu yi she you wo, bing shi wo chengwei shou youdai zhe!
36|28|Zai ta zhihou, wo meiyou jiang tianshen qu chengzhi ta de zongzu, wo ye bu changchang jiang tianshen.
36|29|Cai tingjian yisheng nahan, tamen jiu miewangle.
36|30|Ai zai zhong pu! Zhiyao you shizhe lai jiaohua tamen, tamen bian jiayi yunong.
36|31|Nandao tamen bu zhidao ma? Zai tamen zhiqian, wo ceng huimiele xuduo shidai, naxie bei huimie de shidai yong bu zhuan hui chenshi.
36|32|Tamen jiang tong tong bei jujin zai wo nali.
36|33|Tamen youyi zhong jixiang: Yi si de da di, wo shi ta fuhuo, wo shi ta shengzhang liangshi, yi zuo tamen de shipin.
36|34|Wo zai da dishang chuangzao xuduo ye zao yuan, putao yuan, wo shi xuduo yuanquan, cong di zhong yong chu,
36|35|yibian tamen shi qi guoshi. Zhexie guoshi bushi tamen de shou zao chulai de, nandao tamen bu ganxie me?
36|36|Zansong zhenzhu, chaojue wanwu! Ta chuangzao yiqie pei'ou, dimian suo shengchan de, tamen ziji, yiji tamen suo bu zhidao de, dou you pei'ou.
36|37|Tamen youyi zhong jixiang, wo shi baizhou tuoli heiye, tamen bian huran zai hei'an zhong.
36|38|Taiyang ji xing, zhi yiding suo, na shi wanneng de, quanzhi de zhu suo yuding de.

36|41|Tamen youyi zhong jixiang: Wo shi tamen de zisun, chengzuo manzai de chuanbo.
36|42|Wo wei tamen er chuangzao xiang chuanbo nayang ke gong qi cheng de dongxi.
36|43|Ruguo wo yiyu, wo jiu ba tamen yan si, er tamen meiyou renhe yuanzhu zhe, tamen jiang bu huo zhengjiu;

36|48|Tamen shuo: Zhege jinggao shenme shihou shixian ne? Ruguo nimen shi shuo shihua de.

36|53|Cai tingjian yisheng nahan, tamen jiu tongtong bei jujin zai wo zheli.

36|65|Zai na ri, wo jiang fengbi tamen de kou, tamen de shou jiang dui wo shuohua, tamen de jiao jiang zuozheng tamen suo xing de shan e.
36|66|Jiaruo wo yiyu, wo bi huimie tamen de yanjing, ranhou tamen mangzhe zoulu, dan tamen zen neng kanjian ne?
36|67|Jiaruo wo yiyu, wo bi shi tamen zai ziji de jiazhong bianxing, ranhou tamen ji buneng qianjin, you buneng houtui;
36|68|wo shi shei changshou, wo jiangdi shei de tizhi. Nandao tamen bu ming li me?

36|70|yibian ta jinggao huo ren, yibian bu xindao de renmen dang shou xingfa de panjue.
36|71|Nandao tamen bu zhidao ma? Cong wo suo qinshou zao zuozhe zhi zhong, wo ceng wei tamen er chuangzao shengchu, er tamen guanli tamen.
36|72|Wo wei tamen er zhifu shengchu, yi yibufen gong tamen qi, yibufen gong tamen chi.

36|74|Tamen she zhenzhu er jing shi xuduo shenling, xiwang ziji huode yuanzhu.

37|157|Na chu nimen de jingdian lai ba, tangruo nimen shi chengshi de!
37|158|Tamen wangyan ta yu jingling zhi jian, you yinqin guanxi. Jingling que yi zhidao tamen jiang bei jujin
37|159|chaojue zai zhenzhu! Ta shi chao hu tamen de xushu de,
37|160|wei zhenzhu de chunjie de zhong pu, bu bei jujin.

37|162|jue buneng ba renhe ren yinyou qu chongbai tamen,
37|163|chufei shi jiang ru huo yu de ren.

37|165|women biding shi pai ban de,
37|166|women biding shi zansong zhenzhu de.

37|168|Jiaruo women you guren suo yiliu de jiaohui,
37|169|namo, women bi shi zhenzhu de chunjie de puren.
37|170|Tamen que buxin zhenzhu, tamen bujiu jiu zhidaole.

37|172|tamen biding shi bei yuanzhu de,
37|173|wo de jundui, biding shi shengli de.
37|174|Ni zhanshi tuibi tamen ba!
37|175|Ni kanzhe ba! Tamen bujiu jiu kanjianle.

37|177|Wo de xingfa yidan jiang yu tamen de tingyuan de shihou, bei jinggao zhe de zaochen, zhen elie ya!
37|178|Ni zhanshi tuibi tamen ba!
37|179|Ni kanzhe ba! Tamen bujiu jiu kanjianle.
